### `services/core-dev-services/PLATFORM_PATHWAYS.md`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2840 bytes

```md
# Platform Pathways

XLOTYL Core Dev Services is the source of truth for imported capabilities, workflow policy, task cards, permissions, and adapter generation.

Platform pathways are adapter bridges. They are allowed to be marked as working for a specific IDE or AI platform, but they are not the main XLOTYL pathway unless a separate platform-neutral contract says so.

## Canonical Flow

1. Import and approve capabilities in Core Dev Services.
2. Compile user work with `xlotyl_orchestrate`.
3. Treat the returned task graph as the canonical task card contract.
4. Let each platform adapter decide how to expose or execute those task cards.

## Working For Stoneforge (runtime adapter)

| Field | Value |
| --- | --- |
| `id` | `stoneforge-runtime` |
| `label` | `Stoneforge runtime (Director bypass)` |
| `target` | `stoneforge` |
| `role` | `adapter-pathway` |
| `sourceOfTruth` | `xlotyl-core-dev-services` |
| `isDefaultPathway` | `false` |

This pathway imports a governed XLOTYL graph into **Stoneforge** as the execution substrate while keeping **XLOTYL** as planning authority. It is exposed through the `xsf` CLI (`xlotyl-dev-services xsf …`) and MCP tools `xlotyl_stoneforge_*`.

Runtime implementation target: [HHPE-HRG/stoneforge](https://github.com/HHPE-HRG/stoneforge) (canonical org fork). Upstream: [stoneforge-ai/stoneforge](https://github.com/stoneforge-ai/stoneforge). Fork vs upstream policy: [`docs/stoneforge.md`](../../docs/stoneforge.md) in this repository.

Contract and artifacts:

- `xlotyl/docs/xlotyl-stoneforge-adapter-contract.md`
- `xlotyl/docs/xlotyl-stoneforge-run-artifacts.md`
- `xlotyl/docs/stoneforge-director-bypass-mode.md`
- `xlotyl/docs/stoneforge-adapter-rollout-checklist.md`

## Working For Codex

The current Codex-specific pathway is:

| Field | Value |
| --- | --- |
| `id` | `codex-supervised-swarm` |
| `label` | `Working for Codex` |
| `target` | `codex` |
| `role` | `adapter-pathway` |
| `sourceOfTruth` | `xlotyl-core-dev-services` |
| `isDefaultPathway` | `false` |

This pathway is exposed by `xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan`. It promotes a governed XLOTYL task graph into Codex sub-agent dispatch phases and keeps final aggregation in the supervising Codex thread.

It must not be treated as the default for Claude Code, Cursor, Antigravity, or future front ends. Those targets should get their own explicitly labeled pathways when they have equivalent native dispatch support.

## Adapter Rule

Every platform-specific pathway should declare:

- the target platform,
- whether it is working, experimental, or disabled,
- whether it is an adapter pathway or a platform-neutral pathway,
- the Core Dev Services capability or workflow it wraps,
- whether it can run only after explicit user delegation.

When in doubt, use `xlotyl_orchestrate` and the task graph as the portable path.
```

### `services/core-dev-services/SHELL_HOOK_RESPONSIBILITIES.md`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2984 bytes

```md
# Shell Hook Responsibilities

This package currently treats shell and hook access as an XLOTYL orchestration concern, not as something upstream plugin entries receive directly.

The source registry may import workflows, skills, commands, agents, and MCP servers that imply future execution authority. Until the permission and hook layer is in scope, adapters should expose those entries as tools/features only. XLOTYL owns task card scoping, approval, sandbox selection, and any future shell or hook brokering.

## Current Policy

- Approved feature entries should not emit direct shell hooks.
- Existing shell hooks stay quarantined and are not generated into adapters.
- Secret-bearing or mutating MCP servers stay quarantined until explicitly approved.
- Workflows that need execution authority should describe the responsibility, then let XLOTYL decide if and how to grant it.

## Source Status

| Source | Direct Shell Hook Capability | Current Responsibility |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `compound-engineering` | No | Provides planning, review, and work-mode workflows. XLOTYL turns those workflows into scoped task cards and owns execution authority. |
| `superpowers` | Not emitted | Source supports hook-like components, but the current imported capabilities are skills only. XLOTYL may later broker any worktree, test, or review commands implied by the skills. |
| `runlayer-plugins` | Quarantined | `runlayer-block-env-hook` is classified as a shell hook and must not be emitted to adapters until XLOTYL has an explicit hook policy. Non-hook Runlayer builder skills remain normal approved features. |
| `smolagents` | No | Provides code-agent and MCP-tool-adapter features. Any Python/code execution must be launched through a future XLOTYL runtime adapter with sandbox and scoped tool authority. |
| `spectacular` | No | Provides spec, plan, and execution-shaping workflows. Worktree, git-spice, subagent, and phase execution responsibilities are expected to be mediated by XLOTYL task cards. |
| `private-journal-mcp` | No shell hook; quarantined MCP | Secret-bearing and mutating MCP access remains quarantined. XLOTYL must broker secrets, reads, writes, and audit policy before this is emitted. |
| `smallest-agent` | No imported hook; quarantined agent | The upstream agent model implies unrestricted bash. XLOTYL must sandbox and scope all shell authority before this can become an approved runtime. |

## Expected XLOTYL Ownership

These responsibilities are intentionally not implemented in the current scope:

- approving shell-capable hooks,
- merging hook configs into platform adapters,
- granting raw bash access to imported runtimes,
- passing secrets to MCP servers,
- selecting or enforcing sandboxes for code-agent execution,
- authorizing worktree, git-spice, branch, or PR operations.

When this area becomes active work, the implementation should add a first-class permission broker rather than embedding shell behavior in individual imported capabilities.
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/capability_graph_compiler.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2525 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, test } from "vitest"

import { compileCapabilityPackageGraph } from "../capability-package/graph-compiler.js"

describe("compileCapabilityPackageGraph", () => {
  test("compiles stoneforge-runtime into a valid terminal graph", async () => {
    const result = await compileCapabilityPackageGraph({
      packageId: "stoneforge-runtime",
      sourceGoal: "Validate and activate minimal Stoneforge graph",
      terminalityPolicy: "require_terminal",
    })
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!result.ok) return

    expect(result.graph.execution_mode).toBe("xlotyl_stoneforge")
    expect(result.graph.planning_owner).toBe("xlotyl")
    expect(result.graph.runtime_target).toBe("stoneforge")
    expect(result.graph.tasks.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1)

    const task = result.graph.tasks[0]!
    expect(task.decomposition_policy).toBe("terminal")
    expect(typeof task.runtime_environment_id).toBe("string")
    expect(task.runtime_environment_id?.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(typeof task.execution_adapter_id).toBe("string")
    expect(task.execution_adapter_id?.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(Array.isArray(task.validator_ids)).toBe(true)
    expect((task.validator_ids ?? []).length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(task.expected_artifacts).toEqual(["VERIFICATION_REPORT"])
    expect(task.orchestration_state).toBeDefined()
    expect(task.orchestration_state?.terminality).toBe("terminal")
    expect(["none", "low"]).toContain(task.orchestration_state?.ambiguity_level)
  })

  test("compiles source-corroboration-runtime into a valid terminal graph", async () => {
    const result = await compileCapabilityPackageGraph({
      packageId: "source-corroboration-runtime",
      sourceGoal: "Compile, import, approve, and activate a minimal source corroboration operator graph",
      terminalityPolicy: "require_terminal",
    })
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!result.ok) return

    const task = result.graph.tasks[0]!
    expect(task.decomposition_policy).toBe("terminal")
    expect(typeof task.runtime_environment_id).toBe("string")
    expect(task.runtime_environment_id?.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(typeof task.execution_adapter_id).toBe("string")
    expect(task.execution_adapter_id?.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(task.expected_artifacts).toEqual(["VERIFICATION_REPORT"])
    expect(task.orchestration_state?.terminality).toBe("terminal")
    expect(["none", "low"]).toContain(task.orchestration_state?.ambiguity_level)
  })
})

```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_activate.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2246 bytes

```ts
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { activateRun, validateAndImportRun, writeApproval } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"

function graph(runId: string, requiresApproval: boolean) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    workflow_title: "Activate test",
    source_goal: "G",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: requiresApproval },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "P" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "One",
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["x"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge activate", () => {
  it("refuses activation without approval when required", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-act-"))
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(graph("run-act-1", true), root)
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      const first = await activateRun(root, "run-act-1")
      expect(first.ok).toBe(false)
      await writeApproval(root, "run-act-1", { approved: true, approved_by: "ci" })
      const second = await activateRun(root, "run-act-1", { approvedBy: "ci" })
      expect(second.ok).toBe(true)
      const third = await activateRun(root, "run-act-1")
      expect(third.ok).toBe(true)
      if (third.ok) {
        expect(third.idempotent).toBe(true)
      }
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("activates without approval file when policy is off", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-act-2-"))
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(graph("run-act-2", false), root)
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      const activated = await activateRun(root, "run-act-2")
      expect(activated.ok).toBe(true)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_aggregate.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2669 bytes

```ts
import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { aggregateRun } from "../stoneforge/aggregate-run.js"
import { appendEvaluationEvent, appendSyncEvent, validateAndImportRun } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"

function graph(runId: string) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "wf",
    workflow_title: "agg",
    source_goal: "goal",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "t",
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge aggregate", () => {
  it("writes final report and dataset", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-agg-"))
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(graph("run-agg-1"), root)
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      await appendSyncEvent(root, "run-agg-1", { task_card_id: "T1", status: "completed" })
      await appendEvaluationEvent(root, "run-agg-1", {
        task_card_id: "T1",
        evaluation_status: "passed",
      })
      const out = await aggregateRun(root, "run-agg-1")
      const report = await readFile(out.reportPath, "utf8")
      expect(report).toContain("run-agg-1")
      const dataset = await readFile(out.datasetPath, "utf8")
      expect(dataset).toContain("xlotyl_stoneforge_dataset_v0")
      expect(dataset).toContain('"row_type":"run"')
      expect(dataset).toContain('"row_type":"taskCard"')
      expect(dataset).toContain('"row_type":"aggregate"')
      expect(dataset).toContain('"row_type":"evaluation"')
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("appendEvaluationEvent rejects malformed steward payloads", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-agg-eval-"))
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(graph("run-agg-bad-eval"), root)
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      await expect(
        appendEvaluationEvent(root, "run-agg-bad-eval", {
          task_card_id: "T1",
          evaluation_status: "not-a-status",
        }),
      ).rejects.toThrow(/appendEvaluationEvent/)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_daemon_decision.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5245 bytes

```ts
import { mkdtemp, readFile, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import {
  createStoneforgeDaemonDecisionProvider,
  decideStoneforgeDispatch,
  type StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest,
} from "../stoneforge/daemon-decision.js"

function request(overrides: Partial<StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest> = {}): StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest {
  return {
    workspace_root: "/workspace",
    poll_id: "poll-1",
    dispatch_policy: {
      max_parallel_workers: 2,
      allowed_worker_providers: ["codex"],
      default_worker_provider: "codex",
    },
    ready_tasks: [
      {
        stoneforge_task_id: "sf-low",
        title: "Low priority",
        priority: 3,
        ready_order: 0,
        metadata: {
          xlotyl: {
            schema_version: 1,
            run_id: "run-1",
            task_card_id: "low",
            workflow_id: "wf",
            execution_mode: "stoneforge",
          },
        },
      },
      {
        stoneforge_task_id: "sf-high",
        title: "High priority",
        priority: 1,
        ready_order: 1,
        metadata: {
          xlotyl: {
            schema_version: 1,
            run_id: "run-1",
            task_card_id: "high",
            workflow_id: "wf",
            execution_mode: "stoneforge",
          },
        },
      },
    ],
    agents: [
      {
        agent_id: "worker-codex",
        name: "Codex worker",
        role: "worker",
        provider: "codex",
        session_status: "idle",
        metadata: { agent: { agentRole: "worker", provider: "codex" } },
      },
    ],
    busy_worker_count: 0,
    max_parallel_workers: 2,
    ...overrides,
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge daemon decision provider", () => {
  it("routes the highest-priority ready task to an idle worker and maps XLOTYL metadata", async () => {
    const result = await decideStoneforgeDispatch(request())

    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    expect(result.decisions).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(result.decisions[0]).toMatchObject({
      action_type: "dispatch_task",
      decision_id: "poll-1:dispatch_task:high:0",
      stoneforge_task_id: "sf-high",
      task_card_id: "high",
      xlotyl_run_id: "run-1",
      agent_id: "worker-codex",
      provider: "codex",
    })
  })

  it("uses synthetic taskCard ids for untagged Stoneforge tasks", async () => {
    const result = await decideStoneforgeDispatch(
      request({
        ready_tasks: [
          {
            stoneforge_task_id: "sf-plain",
            title: "Plain Stoneforge task",
            priority: 1,
            ready_order: 0,
            metadata: {},
          },
        ],
      }),
    )

    expect(result.decisions[0]).toMatchObject({
      action_type: "dispatch_task",
      stoneforge_task_id: "sf-plain",
      task_card_id: "stoneforge:sf-plain",
    })
  })

  it("respects provider allow-list and max parallel slots", async () => {
    const wrongProvider = await decideStoneforgeDispatch(
      request({
        dispatch_policy: {
          max_parallel_workers: 2,
          allowed_worker_providers: ["opencode"],
          default_worker_provider: "opencode",
        },
      }),
    )
    expect(wrongProvider.decisions[0]).toMatchObject({
      action_type: "noop",
      reason: "No idle worker is eligible for the ready Stoneforge tasks.",
    })

    const capped = await decideStoneforgeDispatch(
      request({
        busy_worker_count: 2,
        max_parallel_workers: 2,
      }),
    )
    expect(capped.decisions[0]).toMatchObject({
      action_type: "noop",
      reason: "XLOTYL dispatch policy has no available worker slots.",
    })
  })

  it("records daemon and run-scoped decision outcomes deterministically", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-daemon-decision-"))
    try {
      const provider = createStoneforgeDaemonDecisionProvider({ now: () => "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z" })
      const result = await provider.decideDispatch(request({ workspace_root: root }))
      const decision = result.decisions[0]!

      await provider.recordDispatchOutcome({
        workspace_root: root,
        poll_id: "poll-1",
        decision,
        executed: true,
      })

      const daemonLog = await readFile(join(root, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "daemon", "decision-log.jsonl"), "utf8")
      expect(daemonLog.trim()).toBe(
        JSON.stringify({
          schema_version: 1,
          ts: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
          poll_id: "poll-1",
          decision_id: "poll-1:dispatch_task:high:0",
          action_type: "dispatch_task",
          task_card_id: "high",
          stoneforge_task_id: "sf-high",
          agent_id: "worker-codex",
          reason: "Selected highest-priority ready Stoneforge task high for idle worker worker-codex.",
          executed: true,
          decision_provider: "xlotyl",
          xlotyl_run_id: "run-1",
        }),
      )

      const runLog = await readFile(
        join(root, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", "run-1", "decision-log.jsonl"),
        "utf8",
      )
      expect(runLog).toBe(daemonLog)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_decision.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 7794 bytes

```ts
import { mkdtemp, readFile, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { validateAndImportRun } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"
import {
  buildContextBundle,
  buildOrchestrationState,
  decisionLogRecordFromAction,
  SimpleTaskRouter,
  type OrchestrationState,
  type StoneforgeAdapter,
} from "../stoneforge/decision/index.js"

function baseState(overrides: Partial<OrchestrationState> = {}): OrchestrationState {
  const graph = {
    run_id: "run-decision-unit",
    workflow_id: "wf",
    workflow_title: "Decision unit",
    source_goal: "Ship decision routing",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl" as const,
    runtime_target: "stoneforge" as const,
    dispatch_policy: {
      requires_human_approval_before_activation: false,
      max_parallel_workers: 3,
      allowed_worker_providers: ["codex"],
      default_worker_provider: "codex",
    },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "P" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "A",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Lower priority",
        task_card_type: "task",
        priority: 3,
        dependencies: [],
        tools: ["rg"],
        acceptance_criteria: ["done"],
      },
      {
        id: "B",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Higher priority",
        task_card_type: "task",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        tools: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["done"],
      },
    ],
  }
  return {
    runId: graph.run_id,
    graph,
    taskMap: { A: "sf-A", B: "sf-B" },
    tasks: [
      { taskCardId: "A", stoneforgeTaskId: "sf-A", title: "Lower priority", priority: 3, graphIndex: 0, ready: true },
      { taskCardId: "B", stoneforgeTaskId: "sf-B", title: "Higher priority", priority: 1, graphIndex: 1, ready: true },
    ],
    dependencies: [],
    agents: [
      {
        agentId: "agent-codex",
        name: "Codex worker",
        role: "worker",
        provider: "codex",
        sessionStatus: "idle",
        idle: true,
      },
    ],
    recentEvents: [],
    ...overrides,
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge decision module", () => {
  it("routes the highest-priority ready taskCard to an idle worker", async () => {
    const actions = await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(baseState())

    expect(actions).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(actions[0]).toMatchObject({
      action_type: "dispatch_task",
      task_card_id: "B",
      stoneforge_task_id: "sf-B",
      agent_id: "agent-codex",
      routing: {
        taskId: "sf-B",
        taskCardId: "B",
        agentId: "agent-codex",
        provider: "codex",
        priority: 1,
      },
    })
  })

  it("respects provider allow-list and max_parallel_workers", async () => {
    const providerState = baseState({
      graph: {
        ...baseState().graph,
        dispatch_policy: {
          requires_human_approval_before_activation: false,
          max_parallel_workers: 2,
          allowed_worker_providers: ["opencode"],
          default_worker_provider: "opencode",
        },
      },
      agents: [
        {
          agentId: "busy",
          role: "worker",
          provider: "codex",
          sessionStatus: "running",
          sessionId: "session-1",
          idle: false,
        },
        { agentId: "wrong-provider", role: "worker", provider: "codex", sessionStatus: "idle", idle: true },
        { agentId: "right-provider", role: "worker", provider: "opencode", sessionStatus: "idle", idle: true },
      ],
    })
    const providerActions = await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(providerState)
    expect(providerActions).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(providerActions[0]).toMatchObject({ agent_id: "right-provider" })

    const cappedActions = await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(
      baseState({
        graph: {
          ...baseState().graph,
          dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false, max_parallel_workers: 1 },
        },
        agents: providerState.agents,
      }),
    )
    expect(cappedActions).toEqual([])
  })

  it("builds a snapshot that maps Stoneforge ready ids back to XLOTYL taskCards", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-decision-state-"))
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(baseState().graph, root)
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      const adapter: StoneforgeAdapter = {
        listReadyTasks: async () => [{ id: "sf-task-A" }, { id: "unmapped" }],
        listAgents: async () => [{ id: "agent-codex", metadata: { agent: { agentRole: "worker" } } }],
        dispatchTask: async () => undefined,
        handoffTask: async () => undefined,
      }

      const state = await buildOrchestrationState(root, "run-decision-unit", adapter)

      expect(state.tasks.find((task) => task.taskCardId === "A")).toMatchObject({ ready: true })
      expect(state.tasks.find((task) => task.taskCardId === "B")).toMatchObject({ ready: false })
      expect(state.agents[0]).toMatchObject({ agentId: "agent-codex", role: "worker", idle: true })
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("classifies failed evaluations into replan, handoff, and noop actions", async () => {
    const replan = await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(
      baseState({
        tasks: [],
        agents: [],
        recentEvents: [
          { kind: "evaluation", task_card_id: "A", evaluation_status: "failed", requires_replan: true },
        ],
      }),
    )
    expect(replan[0]).toMatchObject({ action_type: "request_replan", task_card_id: "A", executed: false })

    const handoff = await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(
      baseState({
        tasks: [],
        agents: [],
        recentEvents: [
          { kind: "evaluation", task_card_id: "A", evaluation_status: "partial", requires_replan: false },
        ],
      }),
    )
    expect(handoff[0]).toMatchObject({ action_type: "handoff_task", task_card_id: "A", stoneforge_task_id: "sf-A" })

    const noop = await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(
      baseState({
        graph: {
          ...baseState().graph,
          tasks: [
            {
              ...baseState().graph.tasks[0]!,
              handoff_policy: { allow_handoff: false },
            },
          ],
        },
        taskMap: { A: "sf-A" },
        tasks: [],
        agents: [],
        recentEvents: [
          { kind: "evaluation", task_card_id: "A", evaluation_status: "failed", requires_replan: false },
        ],
      }),
    )
    expect(noop[0]).toMatchObject({ action_type: "noop", task_card_id: "A", executed: false })
  })

  it("builds deterministic decision log records and context bundles", async () => {
    const state = baseState()
    const action = (await new SimpleTaskRouter().decide(state))[0]!
    const record = decisionLogRecordFromAction(action, {
      ts: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
      executed: true,
    })
    expect(record).toEqual({
      schema_version: 1,
      ts: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
      decision_id: "run-decision-unit:dispatch_task:B:0",
      action_type: "dispatch_task",
      task_card_id: "B",
      stoneforge_task_id: "sf-B",
      agent_id: "agent-codex",
      reason: "Selected highest-priority ready taskCard B for idle worker agent-codex.",
      executed: true,
    })

    const bundle = buildContextBundle(state, "A")
    expect(bundle).toEqual({
      schema_version: 1,
      run_id: "run-decision-unit",
      task_card_id: "A",
      title: "Lower priority",
      source_goal: "Ship decision routing",
      dependencies: [],
      scope: undefined,
      tools: ["rg"],
      acceptance_criteria: ["done"],
      expected_artifacts: undefined,
      metrics: undefined,
    })
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_decision_cli_mcp.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4503 bytes

```ts
import { mkdtemp, readFile, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { runCli } from "../cli.js"
import { createMcpToolRegistry } from "../mcp.js"
import { decisionLogPath } from "../stoneforge/paths.js"
import { resolvedStoneforgeSfBin } from "./stoneforge_test_sf.js"

function graph(runId: string) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "wf",
    workflow_title: "Decision CLI",
    source_goal: "Dispatch one task",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "P" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Route me",
        task_card_type: "task",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["done"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge decision CLI and MCP", () => {
  it("runs xsf decide and appends decision-log.jsonl", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-decision-cli-"))
    const sfBin = resolvedStoneforgeSfBin()
    try {
      const graphPath = join(root, "graph.json")
      await import("node:fs/promises").then(({ writeFile }) =>
        writeFile(graphPath, `${JSON.stringify(graph("run-decision-cli"), null, 2)}\n`, "utf8"),
      )
      await runCli(["xsf", "import", "--graph", graphPath, "--workspace", root, "--binding", "sf-cli", "--sf-bin", sfBin])
      await runCli(["xsf", "activate", "--run", "run-decision-cli", "--workspace", root, "--binding", "sf-cli", "--sf-bin", sfBin])

      const out = await runCli(["xsf", "decide", "--run", "run-decision-cli", "--workspace", root, "--binding", "sf-cli", "--sf-bin", sfBin])
      const parsed = JSON.parse(out) as { ok: boolean; decisions: Array<{ action_type: string }>; executed: unknown[] }

      expect(parsed.ok).toBe(true)
      expect(parsed.decisions).toEqual([expect.objectContaining({ action_type: "dispatch_task" })])
      expect(parsed.executed).toHaveLength(1)
      const log = await readFile(decisionLogPath(root, "run-decision-cli"), "utf8")
      expect(log).toContain('"action_type":"dispatch_task"')
      expect(log).toContain('"executed":true')
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  }, 60000)

  it("exposes xlotyl_stoneforge_decide with matching behavior", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-decision-mcp-"))
    const sfBin = resolvedStoneforgeSfBin()
    const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()
    try {
      await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_import", {
        graph: graph("run-decision-mcp"),
        workspaceRoot: root,
        binding: "sf-cli",
        sfBinPath: sfBin,
      })
      await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_activate", {
        runId: "run-decision-mcp",
        workspaceRoot: root,
        binding: "sf-cli",
        sfBinPath: sfBin,
      })

      const result = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_decide", {
        runId: "run-decision-mcp",
        workspaceRoot: root,
        binding: "sf-cli",
        sfBinPath: sfBin,
      })
      const parsed = JSON.parse(result.content[0]?.text ?? "{}") as { ok: boolean; decisions: unknown[] }

      expect(parsed.ok).toBe(true)
      expect(parsed.decisions).toHaveLength(1)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  }, 60000)

  it("returns ok false for unsupported decide bindings and missing run artifacts", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-decision-invalid-"))
    try {
      const unsupported = JSON.parse(
        await runCli(["xsf", "decide", "--run", "missing", "--workspace", root, "--binding", "local-artifact"]),
      ) as { ok: boolean; error: string }
      expect(unsupported).toMatchObject({ ok: false })
      expect(unsupported.error).toContain("requires sf-cli")

      const missing = JSON.parse(
        await runCli([
          "xsf",
          "decide",
          "--run",
          "missing",
          "--workspace",
          root,
          "--binding",
          "sf-cli",
          "--sf-bin",
          resolvedStoneforgeSfBin(),
        ]),
      ) as { ok: boolean; error: string }
      expect(missing).toMatchObject({ ok: false })
      expect(missing.error).toContain("graph.json")
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_director_hook.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 1266 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { reportDirectorPlanningAttempt } from "../stoneforge/director-hook.js"

describe("Director planning hook", () => {
  it("rejects autonomous Director decomposition in strict xlotyl_stoneforge mode", () => {
    const raw = {
      run_id: "r1",
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "t",
      source_goal: "g",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      execution_mode: "xlotyl_stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "T1",
          phase_id: "P1",
          title: "one",
          task_card_type: "task",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
        },
      ],
    }
    const v = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(raw)
    expect(v.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!v.ok) {
      return
    }
    expect(() => reportDirectorPlanningAttempt(v.graph, true)).toThrow(
      "director_decomposition_forbidden_in_xlotyl_stoneforge_mode",
    )
    expect(() => reportDirectorPlanningAttempt(v.graph, false)).not.toThrow()
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_import.test.ts`

```ts
import { readFile, stat } from "node:fs/promises"
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { dirname, join, resolve } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { activateRun, validateAndImportRun, writeApproval } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"
import { sfCliJson } from "./stoneforge_sf_exec.js"
import { resolvedStoneforgeSfBin } from "./stoneforge_test_sf.js"

const mockSfBin = resolve(dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)), "..", "..", "fixtures", "mock-stoneforge-sf.mjs")

function validGraph(runId: string, requiresApproval = false) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    workflow_title: "Import test",
    source_goal: "Goal",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: requiresApproval },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "P1" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "A",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "First",
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["x"],
      },
      {
        id: "B",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Second",
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 2,
        dependencies: ["A"],
        acceptance_criteria: ["y"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge import run", () => {
  it("validates sf-cli imports in dry-run mode without mutating Stoneforge state", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-dry-run-"))
    try {
      const outcome = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-dry-run"), root, {
        binding: { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath: mockSfBin },
        dryRun: true,
      })
      expect(outcome.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!outcome.ok) {
        return
      }
      expect("dry_run" in outcome).toBe(true)
      if (!("dry_run" in outcome)) {
        return
      }
      expect(outcome.dry_run).toBe(true)
      expect(outcome.sf_cli.version).toMatch(/^\d+\.\d+\.\d+/)
      await expect(stat(join(root, ".stoneforge", "mock-stoneforge-state.json"))).rejects.toThrow()
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("writes graph, map, draft plan, and log", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-"))
    try {
      const outcome = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-1"), root)
      expect(outcome.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!outcome.ok) {
        return
      }
      const draft = JSON.parse(await readFile(outcome.result.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        tasks: Array<{ xlotyl_task_card_id: string; stoneforge_task_id: string }>
        dependencies: Array<{ blocked: string; blocker: string }>
      }
      expect(draft.tasks).toHaveLength(2)
      expect(draft.dependencies).toEqual([
        { blocked: "sf-task-B", blocker: "sf-task-A" },
      ])
      const log = await readFile(outcome.result.paths.log, "utf8")
      expect(log).toContain('"kind":"import"')
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("preserves recursive XLOTYL metadata in local draft tasks", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-generation-"))
    try {
      const graph = validGraph("run-import-generation-1") as any
      graph.dispatch_policy = {
        requires_human_approval_before_activation: false,
        max_generation_depth: 3,
        max_fan_out: 6,
      }
      graph.tasks = graph.tasks.map((task: any) => ({
        ...task,
        generation: 1,
        parent_run_id: "run-polynomial-root",
        parent_task_card_id: "taskCard-polynomial-root",
        decomposition_policy: "terminal",
      }))

      const outcome = await validateAndImportRun(graph, root)
      expect(outcome.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!outcome.ok) {
        return
      }
      const draft = JSON.parse(await readFile(outcome.result.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        tasks: Array<{
          xlotyl_task_card_id: string
          metadata?: {
            xlotyl?: {
              schema_version?: number
              generation?: number
              parent_run_id?: string
              parent_task_card_id?: string
              decomposition_policy?: string
            }
          }
        }>
      }

      expect(draft.tasks[0].metadata?.xlotyl).toMatchObject({
        schema_version: 1,
        generation: 1,
        parent_run_id: "run-polynomial-root",
        parent_task_card_id: "taskCard-polynomial-root",
        decomposition_policy: "terminal",
      })
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("imports via sf-cli (fixture mock sf unless STONEFORGE_SF_BIN) and blocks activation before approval", async () => {
    const sfBin = resolvedStoneforgeSfBin()
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-real-"))
    try {
      const outcome = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-real-1", true), root, {
        binding: { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath: sfBin },
      })
      expect(outcome.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!outcome.ok) {
        return
      }

      const draft = JSON.parse(await readFile(outcome.result.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        id: string
        status: string
        tasks: Array<{ stoneforge_task_id: string; xlotyl_task_card_id: string }>
        dependencies: Array<{ blocked: string; blocker: string }>
      }
      expect(draft.status).toBe("draft")
      expect(draft.id).toMatch(/^el-/)
      expect(draft.tasks).toHaveLength(2)
      expect(draft.dependencies).toHaveLength(1)

      const planShown = await sfCliJson<{ plan: { status: string; id: string } }>(root, sfBin, [
        "plan",
        "show",
        draft.id,
      ])
      expect(planShown.plan.status).toBe("draft")

      const readyBefore = await sfCliJson<Array<{ id: string }>>(root, sfBin, ["ready"])
      const readyIdsBefore = new Set(readyBefore.map((t) => t.id))
      for (const t of draft.tasks) {
        expect(readyIdsBefore.has(t.stoneforge_task_id)).toBe(false)
      }

      const firstActivation = await activateRun(root, "run-import-real-1", {
        binding: { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath: sfBin },
      })
      expect(firstActivation.ok).toBe(false)

      await writeApproval(root, "run-import-real-1", { approved: true, approved_by: "ci" })
      const secondActivation = await activateRun(root, "run-import-real-1", {
        approvedBy: "ci",
        binding: { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath: sfBin },
      })
      expect(secondActivation.ok).toBe(true)

      const draftAfter = JSON.parse(await readFile(outcome.result.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        tasks: Array<{ stoneforge_task_id: string; xlotyl_task_card_id: string }>
      }
      const idA = draftAfter.tasks.find((t) => t.xlotyl_task_card_id === "A")?.stoneforge_task_id
      const idB = draftAfter.tasks.find((t) => t.xlotyl_task_card_id === "B")?.stoneforge_task_id
      expect(idA).toBeTruthy()
      expect(idB).toBeTruthy()
      const readyAfter = await sfCliJson<Array<{ id: string }>>(root, sfBin, ["ready"])
      const readyIdsAfter = new Set(readyAfter.map((t) => t.id))
      expect(readyIdsAfter.has(idA!)).toBe(true)
      expect(readyIdsAfter.has(idB!)).toBe(false)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  }, 60000)

  it("tags sf-cli imported tasks with XLOTYL metadata", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-metadata-"))
    try {
      const outcome = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-metadata-1"), root, {
        binding: { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath: mockSfBin },
      })
      expect(outcome.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!outcome.ok) {
        return
      }

      const state = JSON.parse(
        await readFile(join(root, ".stoneforge", "mock-stoneforge-state.json"), "utf8"),
      ) as {
        tasks: Record<string, { metadata?: { xlotyl?: Record<string, unknown> } }>
      }
      const draftTask = outcome.result.draftPlan.tasks.find((task) => task.xlotyl_task_card_id === "A")
      expect(draftTask).toBeTruthy()
      expect(state.tasks[draftTask!.stoneforge_task_id]?.metadata?.xlotyl).toEqual({
        schema_version: 1,
        run_id: "run-import-metadata-1",
        task_card_id: "A",
        workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
        execution_mode: null,
        generation: 0,
        parent_run_id: null,
        parent_task_card_id: null,
        decomposition_policy: "auto",
      })
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  }, 60000)

  it("verifies task and plan metadata through the sf-cli binding after import", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-verify-metadata-"))
    try {
      const graph = {
        ...validGraph("run-import-verify-metadata"),
        execution_mode: "xlotyl_stoneforge" as const,
      }
      const outcome = await validateAndImportRun(graph, root, {
        binding: { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath: mockSfBin },
      })
      expect(outcome.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!outcome.ok) {
        return
      }

      const plan = await sfCliJson<{ metadata?: { xlotyl?: Record<string, unknown> } }>(root, mockSfBin, [
        "show",
        outcome.result.draftPlan.id,
      ])
      expect(plan.metadata?.xlotyl).toMatchObject({
        schema_version: 1,
        run_id: "run-import-verify-metadata",
        workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
        execution_mode: "xlotyl_stoneforge",
      })

      const taskA = outcome.result.draftPlan.tasks.find((task) => task.xlotyl_task_card_id === "A")
      expect(taskA).toBeTruthy()
      const shown = await sfCliJson<{ metadata?: { xlotyl?: Record<string, unknown> } }>(root, mockSfBin, [
        "show",
        taskA!.stoneforge_task_id,
      ])
      expect(shown.metadata?.xlotyl).toMatchObject({
        schema_version: 1,
        run_id: "run-import-verify-metadata",
        task_card_id: "A",
        execution_mode: "xlotyl_stoneforge",
      })
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("is idempotent when importing the same sf-cli run repeatedly", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-idempotent-"))
    try {
      const binding = { kind: "sf-cli" as const, sfBinPath: mockSfBin }
      const first = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-idempotent"), root, { binding })
      expect(first.ok).toBe(true)
      const second = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-idempotent"), root, { binding })
      expect(second.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!second.ok) {
        return
      }

      const state = JSON.parse(
        await readFile(join(root, ".stoneforge", "mock-stoneforge-state.json"), "utf8"),
      ) as {
        tasks: Record<string, unknown>
        plans: Record<string, { taskIds: string[] }>
      }
      expect(Object.keys(state.tasks)).toHaveLength(2)
      expect(state.plans[second.result.draftPlan.id]?.taskIds).toHaveLength(2)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("rejects corrupt imports with duplicate taskCard-to-task mapping", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-import-duplicate-map-"))
    try {
      const binding = { kind: "sf-cli" as const, sfBinPath: mockSfBin }
      const first = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-duplicate-map"), root, { binding })
      expect(first.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!first.ok) {
        return
      }
      await import("node:fs/promises").then(({ writeFile }) =>
        writeFile(
          join(root, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", "run-import-duplicate-map", "stoneforge-map.json"),
          `${JSON.stringify({ run_id: "run-import-duplicate-map", mapping: { A: "el-task-mock-1", B: "el-task-mock-1" } }, null, 2)}\n`,
          "utf8",
        ),
      )

      const second = await validateAndImportRun(validGraph("run-import-duplicate-map"), root, { binding })
      expect(second).toMatchObject({
        ok: false,
        errors: [expect.stringContaining("duplicate taskCard to Stoneforge task mapping")],
      })
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_m3_dispatch_integration.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3093 bytes

```ts
import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { aggregateRun } from "../stoneforge/aggregate-run.js"
import { appendSyncEvent, activateRun, validateAndImportRun, writeApproval } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"
import { sfCliJson } from "./stoneforge_sf_exec.js"
import { resolvedStoneforgeSfBin } from "./stoneforge_test_sf.js"

function oneTaskGraph(runId: string) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    workflow_title: "M3 dispatch",
    source_goal: "G",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: true },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "P" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Single",
        task_card_type: "task",
        priority: 2,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["done"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge M3 dispatch integration", () => {
  it("approve, activate, dispatch one ready task, then sync and aggregate", async () => {
    const sfBin = resolvedStoneforgeSfBin()
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-m3-"))
    const binding = { kind: "sf-cli" as const, sfBinPath: sfBin }
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(oneTaskGraph("run-m3-1"), root, { binding })
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      const draft = JSON.parse(await readFile(imported.result.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        id: string
        tasks: Array<{ stoneforge_task_id: string; xlotyl_task_card_id: string }>
      }
      const ready0 = await sfCliJson<Array<{ id: string }>>(root, sfBin, ["ready"])
      expect(ready0.some((t) => t.id === draft.tasks[0]!.stoneforge_task_id)).toBe(false)

      await writeApproval(root, "run-m3-1", { approved: true, approved_by: "ci" })
      const activated = await activateRun(root, "run-m3-1", { approvedBy: "ci", binding })
      expect(activated.ok).toBe(true)

      const ready1 = await sfCliJson<Array<{ id: string }>>(root, sfBin, ["ready"])
      expect(ready1.some((t) => t.id === draft.tasks[0]!.stoneforge_task_id)).toBe(true)

      const agents = await sfCliJson<Array<{ id: string; name?: string; metadata?: { agent?: { agentRole?: string } } }>>(
        root,
        sfBin,
        ["agent", "list"],
      )
      const worker = agents.find((a) => a.metadata?.agent?.agentRole === "worker")
      expect(worker?.id).toBeTruthy()

      await sfCliJson(root, sfBin, ["dispatch", draft.tasks[0]!.stoneforge_task_id, worker!.id])

      await appendSyncEvent(root, "run-m3-1", { task_card_id: "T1", status: "completed" })
      const agg = await aggregateRun(root, "run-m3-1")
      const report = await readFile(agg.reportPath, "utf8")
      expect(report).toContain("run-m3-1")
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  }, 60000)
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_m4_replan_sf_integration.test.ts`

```ts
import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { importRun, readGraphFromDisk, validateAndImportRun } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"
import { mergeGraphsForReplan } from "../stoneforge/replan.js"
import { resolvedStoneforgeSfBin } from "./stoneforge_test_sf.js"

function baseGraph(runId: string) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "wf",
    workflow_title: "Replan base",
    source_goal: "G",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "P" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "A",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "A",
        task_card_type: "task",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        tools: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["x"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge M4 replan with sf-cli", () => {
  it("merges delta and adds only new Stoneforge tasks on re-import", async () => {
    const sfBin = resolvedStoneforgeSfBin()
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-m4-"))
    const binding = { kind: "sf-cli" as const, sfBinPath: sfBin }
    try {
      const firstImport = await validateAndImportRun(baseGraph("run-m4-1"), root, { binding })
      expect(firstImport.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!firstImport.ok) {
        return
      }
      const first = firstImport.result
      const draft1 = JSON.parse(await readFile(first.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        tasks: Array<{ stoneforge_task_id: string; xlotyl_task_card_id: string }>
      }
      expect(draft1.tasks).toHaveLength(1)

      const base = await readGraphFromDisk(root, "run-m4-1")
      const merged = mergeGraphsForReplan(base, {
        ...base,
        tasks: [
          {
            id: "B",
            phase_id: "P1",
            title: "B",
            task_card_type: "task",
            priority: 2,
            dependencies: ["A"],
            tools: [],
            acceptance_criteria: ["y"],
          },
        ],
      })
      expect(merged.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!merged.ok) {
        return
      }
      const second = await importRun(merged.graph, root, { binding })
      const draft2 = JSON.parse(await readFile(second.paths.draftPlan, "utf8")) as {
        tasks: Array<{ stoneforge_task_id: string; xlotyl_task_card_id: string }>
      }
      expect(draft2.tasks).toHaveLength(2)
      const idsA = draft2.tasks.filter((t) => t.xlotyl_task_card_id === "A").map((t) => t.stoneforge_task_id)
      expect(idsA).toHaveLength(1)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  }, 60000)
})
```

```ts
import { mkdtemp, mkdir, readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import os from "node:os"
import path from "node:path"
import { describe, expect, test } from "vitest"

import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { markTerminal } from "../stoneforge/mark-terminal.js"
import { dispatchLogPath, runDirectory } from "../stoneforge/paths.js"

describe("stoneforge markTerminal", () => {
  test("marks one task terminal and keeps graph valid", async () => {
    const workspaceRoot = await mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "xlotyl-mark-terminal-"))
    const runId = "run-mark-terminal-fixture"

    const graph = {
      run_id: runId,
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "wf",
      source_goal: "goal",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "p1", name: "phase" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "task-a",
          title: "A",
          task_card_type: "test",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["ok"],
          tools: [],
          decomposition_policy: "auto",
        },
        {
          id: "task-b",
          title: "B",
          objective: "Execute task B as a terminal unit.",
          task_card_type: "test",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: ["task-a"],
          acceptance_criteria: ["ok"],
          tools: [],
          runtime_environment_id: "engineering_orchestration_stack",
          execution_adapter_id: "xlotyl_stoneforge_mark_terminal",
          expected_artifacts: ["VERIFICATION_REPORT"],
          decomposition_policy: "auto",
        },
      ],
    }

    const validated = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(validated.ok).toBe(true)

    await mkdir(runDirectory(workspaceRoot, runId), { recursive: true })
    const graphPath = path.join(workspaceRoot, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", runId, "graph.json")
    await writeFile(graphPath, `${JSON.stringify(graph, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")

    const result = await markTerminal(workspaceRoot, runId, {
      taskId: "task-b",
      markedBy: "ci-smoke",
      reason: "operator governance: make task terminal",
      evidenceRefs: ["artifact://evidence/task-terminal-governance"],
    })
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!result.ok) {
      return
    }
    expect(result.updated_task_ids).toEqual(["task-b"])
    expect(result.marked_by).toBe("ci-smoke")
    expect(result.reason).toBe("operator governance: make task terminal")
    expect(result.evidence_refs).toEqual(["artifact://evidence/task-terminal-governance"])

    const raw = JSON.parse(await readFile(graphPath, "utf8")) as unknown
    const revalidated = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(raw)
    expect(revalidated.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!revalidated.ok) {
      return
    }
    const updated = revalidated.graph.tasks.find((t) => t.id === "task-b")
    expect(updated?.decomposition_policy).toBe("terminal")

    const logPath = dispatchLogPath(workspaceRoot, runId)
    const logRaw = await readFile(logPath, "utf8")
    const lines = logRaw.split("\n").map((l) => l.trim()).filter(Boolean)
    const last = JSON.parse(lines[lines.length - 1]) as Record<string, unknown>
    expect(last.kind).toBe("mark_terminal")
    expect(last.status).toBe("ok")
    expect(last.updated_task_ids).toEqual(["task-b"])
    expect(last.marked_by).toBe("ci-smoke")
    expect(last.reason).toBe("operator governance: make task terminal")
    expect(last.evidence_refs).toEqual(["artifact://evidence/task-terminal-governance"])
  })

  test("idempotent markTerminal emits noop audit record", async () => {
    const workspaceRoot = await mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "xlotyl-mark-terminal-"))
    const runId = "run-mark-terminal-idempotent-fixture"

    const graph = {
      run_id: runId,
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "wf",
      source_goal: "goal",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "p1", name: "phase" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "task-terminal",
          title: "Already terminal",
          objective: "This is already a terminal unit.",
          task_card_type: "test",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["ok"],
          tools: [],
          runtime_environment_id: "engineering_orchestration_stack",
          execution_adapter_id: "xlotyl_stoneforge_mark_terminal",
          expected_artifacts: ["VERIFICATION_REPORT"],
          decomposition_policy: "terminal",
        },
      ],
    }

    const validated = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(validated.ok).toBe(true)

    await mkdir(runDirectory(workspaceRoot, runId), { recursive: true })
    const graphPath = path.join(workspaceRoot, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", runId, "graph.json")
    await writeFile(graphPath, `${JSON.stringify(graph, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")

    const result = await markTerminal(workspaceRoot, runId, {
      taskId: "task-terminal",
      markedBy: "ci-smoke",
      reason: "operator governance: reaffirm terminality",
      evidenceRefs: ["artifact://evidence/task-terminal-idempotent"],
    })
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!result.ok) {
      return
    }
    expect(result.updated_task_ids).toEqual([])
    expect(result.idempotent).toBe(true)

    const logPath = dispatchLogPath(workspaceRoot, runId)
    const logRaw = await readFile(logPath, "utf8")
    const lines = logRaw.split("\n").map((l) => l.trim()).filter(Boolean)
    const last = JSON.parse(lines[lines.length - 1]) as Record<string, unknown>
    expect(last.kind).toBe("mark_terminal")
    expect(last.status).toBe("noop")
    expect(last.idempotent).toBe(true)
    expect(last.updated_task_ids).toEqual([])
    expect(last.marked_by).toBe("ci-smoke")
    expect(last.reason).toBe("operator governance: reaffirm terminality")
    expect(last.evidence_refs).toEqual(["artifact://evidence/task-terminal-idempotent"])
  })

  test("rejects marking terminal when terminality requirements are missing", async () => {
    const workspaceRoot = await mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "xlotyl-mark-terminal-"))
    const runId = "run-mark-terminal-invalid"

    const graph = {
      run_id: runId,
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "wf",
      source_goal: "goal",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "p1", name: "phase" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "task-a",
          title: "A",
          task_card_type: "test",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["ok"],
          tools: [],
          decomposition_policy: "auto",
        },
      ],
    }

    const validated = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(validated.ok).toBe(true)

    await mkdir(runDirectory(workspaceRoot, runId), { recursive: true })
    const graphPath = path.join(workspaceRoot, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", runId, "graph.json")
    await writeFile(graphPath, `${JSON.stringify(graph, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")

    const result = await markTerminal(workspaceRoot, runId, { taskId: "task-a" })
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
    if (result.ok) return
    expect(result.errors.join("\n")).toContain("objective is required for terminal tasks")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_mode_guardrails.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2240 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { assertDirectorBypassAllowed, isStrictStoneforgeMode } from "../stoneforge/mode-guard.js"

describe("Stoneforge mode guardrails", () => {
  it("detects strict mode when execution_mode is set", () => {
    const raw = {
      run_id: "run-mode",
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "t",
      source_goal: "g",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      execution_mode: "xlotyl_stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "T1",
          phase_id: "P1",
          title: "t",
          task_card_type: "t",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
        },
      ],
    }
    const parsed = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(raw)
    expect(parsed.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!parsed.ok) {
      return
    }
    expect(isStrictStoneforgeMode(parsed.graph)).toBe(true)
    expect(() => assertDirectorBypassAllowed(parsed.graph, true)).toThrow(
      "director_decomposition_forbidden_in_xlotyl_stoneforge_mode",
    )
    expect(() => assertDirectorBypassAllowed(parsed.graph, false)).not.toThrow()
  })

  it("does not enforce strict mode when execution_mode is absent", () => {
    const raw = {
      run_id: "run-mode-2",
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "t",
      source_goal: "g",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "T1",
          phase_id: "P1",
          title: "t",
          task_card_type: "t",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
        },
      ],
    }
    const parsed = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(raw)
    expect(parsed.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!parsed.ok) {
      return
    }
    expect(isStrictStoneforgeMode(parsed.graph)).toBe(false)
    expect(() => assertDirectorBypassAllowed(parsed.graph, true)).not.toThrow()
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_replan.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5599 bytes

```ts
import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { importRun, readGraphFromDisk, validateAndImportRun } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { mergeGraphsForReplan } from "../stoneforge/replan.js"
import { runReplanMergeAndImport } from "../stoneforge/replan-pipeline.js"

function baseGraph(runId: string, opts: { max_replan_cycles?: number } = {}) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    workflow_title: "Replan base",
    source_goal: "g",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl" as const,
    runtime_target: "stoneforge" as const,
    dispatch_policy: {
      requires_human_approval_before_activation: false,
      ...(opts.max_replan_cycles !== undefined ? { max_replan_cycles: opts.max_replan_cycles } : {}),
    },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "first",
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [] as string[],
        acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

function deltaWithNewTask(runId: string, id: string, deps: string[]) {
  return {
    ...baseGraph(runId),
    tasks: [
      {
        id,
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: `task-${id}`,
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 2,
        dependencies: deps,
        acceptance_criteria: ["b"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge replan merge", () => {
  it("merges new taskCards only", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-replan-"))
    try {
      const first = await validateAndImportRun(baseGraph("run-replan-1"), root)
      expect(first.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!first.ok) {
        return
      }
      const base = await readGraphFromDisk(root, "run-replan-1")
      const delta = {
        ...baseGraph("run-replan-1"),
        tasks: [
          {
            id: "T2",
            phase_id: "P1",
            title: "follow-up",
            task_card_type: "t",
            priority: 2,
            dependencies: ["T1"],
            acceptance_criteria: ["b"],
          },
        ],
      }
      const merged = mergeGraphsForReplan(base, delta)
      expect(merged.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!merged.ok) {
        return
      }
      await importRun(merged.graph, root)
      const raw = await readFile(join(root, ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", "run-replan-1", "graph.json"), "utf8")
      const saved = JSON.parse(raw) as { tasks: Array<{ id: string }> }
      expect(saved.tasks.map((task) => task.id)).toEqual(["T1", "T2"])
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("rejects reuse of existing taskCard ids", () => {
    const baseResult = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(baseGraph("run-reuse"))
    expect(baseResult.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!baseResult.ok) {
      return
    }
    const delta = {
      ...baseGraph("run-reuse"),
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "T1",
          phase_id: "P1",
          title: "tampered",
          task_card_type: "t",
          priority: 9,
          dependencies: [] as string[],
          acceptance_criteria: ["changed"],
        },
      ],
    }
    const merged = mergeGraphsForReplan(baseResult.graph, delta)
    expect(merged.ok).toBe(false)
    if (!merged.ok) {
      expect(merged.errors.join(" ")).toContain("reuse")
    }
  })

  it("enforces max_replan_cycles on runReplanMergeAndImport", async () => {
    const runId = "run-cap-1"
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-replan-cap-"))
    try {
      const first = await validateAndImportRun(baseGraph(runId, { max_replan_cycles: 1 }), root)
      expect(first.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!first.ok) {
        return
      }
      const r1 = await runReplanMergeAndImport(root, runId, deltaWithNewTask(runId, "T2", ["T1"]), {
        binding: { kind: "local-artifact" },
      })
      expect(r1.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!r1.ok) {
        return
      }
      expect(r1.deduped).toBe(false)
      const r2 = await runReplanMergeAndImport(root, runId, deltaWithNewTask(runId, "T3", ["T2"]), {
        binding: { kind: "local-artifact" },
      })
      expect(r2.ok).toBe(false)
      if (r2.ok) {
        return
      }
      expect(r2.errors.join(" ")).toMatch(/max_replan_cycles/i)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("dedupes replan when idempotency key matches last success", async () => {
    const runId = "run-idem-1"
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-replan-idem-"))
    try {
      const first = await validateAndImportRun(baseGraph(runId), root)
      expect(first.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!first.ok) {
        return
      }
      const key = "idem-retry-1"
      const delta = deltaWithNewTask(runId, "T2", ["T1"])
      const a = await runReplanMergeAndImport(root, runId, delta, {
        binding: { kind: "local-artifact" },
        idempotencyKey: key,
      })
      expect(a.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!a.ok) {
        return
      }
      expect(a.deduped).toBe(false)
      const b = await runReplanMergeAndImport(root, runId, delta, {
        binding: { kind: "local-artifact" },
        idempotencyKey: key,
      })
      expect(b.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!b.ok) {
        return
      }
      expect(b.deduped).toBe(true)
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_sf_exec.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 847 bytes

```ts
import { execFile } from "node:child_process"
import { promisify } from "node:util"

const execFileAsync = promisify(execFile)

/**
 * Run the Stoneforge `sf` CLI built as `sf.js` under Node and parse JSON output.
 */
export async function sfCliJson<T>(cwd: string, sfBin: string, args: string[]): Promise<T> {
  const argv = args.includes("--json") ? args : [...args, "--json"]
  const { stdout, stderr } = await execFileAsync(process.execPath, [sfBin, ...argv], { cwd })
  const trimmed = stdout.trim()
  if (!trimmed) {
    throw new Error(`sf returned empty stdout: ${args.join(" ")}\n${stderr}`)
  }
  const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed) as { success?: boolean; data?: T; error?: { message?: string } }
  if (!parsed.success) {
    throw new Error(parsed.error?.message ?? stderr.trim() ?? "sf command failed")
  }
  return parsed.data as T
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_sync.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 1976 bytes

```ts
import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { mkdtemp, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { parseEvaluationPayload } from "../stoneforge/evaluation.js"
import { appendEvaluationEvent, appendSyncEvent, validateAndImportRun } from "../stoneforge/import-run.js"

function minimalGraph(runId: string) {
  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workflow_id: "wf",
    workflow_title: "t",
    source_goal: "g",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "one",
        task_card_type: "t",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("Stoneforge sync + evaluation", () => {
  it("appends sync and evaluation lines", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xsf-sync-"))
    try {
      const imported = await validateAndImportRun(minimalGraph("run-sync-1"), root)
      expect(imported.ok).toBe(true)
      if (!imported.ok) {
        return
      }
      await appendSyncEvent(root, "run-sync-1", { task_card_id: "T1", status: "completed", metrics: { files: 2 } })
      await appendEvaluationEvent(root, "run-sync-1", {
        task_card_id: "T1",
        evaluation_status: "passed",
        requires_replan: false,
      })
      const log = await readFile(imported.result.paths.log, "utf8")
      expect(log).toContain('"kind":"sync"')
      expect(log).toContain('"kind":"evaluation"')
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("rejects malformed evaluation payloads", () => {
    const parsed = parseEvaluationPayload({ task_card_id: "", evaluation_status: "passed" })
    expect(parsed.ok).toBe(false)
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/stoneforge_test_sf.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 612 bytes

```ts
import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url"
import path from "node:path"

/**
 * Path to the fake Stoneforge CLI used in tests when `STONEFORGE_SF_BIN` is unset.
 * Set `STONEFORGE_SF_BIN` to a real `sf.js` to exercise the live Stoneforge binary instead.
 */
export function resolvedStoneforgeSfBin(): string {
  const fromEnv = process.env.STONEFORGE_SF_BIN ?? process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN
  if (fromEnv && fromEnv.length > 0) {
    return path.resolve(fromEnv)
  }
  const here = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))
  return path.resolve(here, "..", "..", "fixtures", "mock-stoneforge-sf.mjs")
}
```

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import type { XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { renderTaskCardDescription } from "../stoneforge/task-card-renderer.js"

describe("renderTaskCardDescription", () => {
  it("includes acceptance criteria and run metadata", () => {
    const raw = {
      run_id: "run-render",
      workflow_id: "wf",
      workflow_title: "Title",
      source_goal: "Goal text",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "Phase" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "T1",
          phase_id: "P1",
          title: "Do work",
          task_card_type: "research",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          tools: ["git"],
          acceptance_criteria: ["Criterion A"],
        },
      ],
    }
    const parsed = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(raw)
    expect(parsed.ok).toBe(true)
    if (!parsed.ok) {
      return
    }
    const graph = parsed.graph as XlotylStoneforgeGraph
    const md = renderTaskCardDescription(graph, graph.tasks[0])
    expect(md).toContain("run-render")
    expect(md).toContain("Criterion A")
    expect(md).toContain("git")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/__tests__/xlotyl_stoneforge_contract.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5121 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"

function baseGraph() {
  return {
    run_id: "run-contract-1",
    workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    workflow_title: "Contract test",
    source_goal: "Ship a small change",
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
    phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "Discovery" }],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "T1",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Map codebase",
        task_card_type: "research_codebase",
        worker_role: "mapper",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["Map exists"],
      },
      {
        id: "T2",
        phase_id: "P1",
        title: "Implement",
        task_card_type: "implement",
        priority: 2,
        dependencies: ["T1"],
        acceptance_criteria: ["Tests pass"],
      },
    ],
  }
}

describe("validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph", () => {
  it("accepts a well-formed graph", () => {
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(baseGraph())
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (result.ok) {
      expect(result.graph.run_id).toBe("run-contract-1")
    }
  })

  it("rejects duplicate taskCard ids", () => {
    const graph = baseGraph() as ReturnType<typeof baseGraph>
    graph.tasks = [
      graph.tasks[0],
      { ...graph.tasks[1], id: "T1", dependencies: [] },
    ]
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
    if (!result.ok) {
      expect(result.errors.join(" ")).toContain("duplicate")
    }
  })

  it("rejects unknown dependency ids", () => {
    const graph = baseGraph() as ReturnType<typeof baseGraph>
    graph.tasks[1].dependencies = ["missing"]
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
    if (!result.ok) {
      expect(result.errors.some((line) => line.includes("unknown taskCard"))).toBe(true)
    }
  })

  it("rejects dependency cycles", () => {
    const graph = baseGraph() as ReturnType<typeof baseGraph>
    graph.tasks[0].dependencies = ["T2"]
    graph.tasks[1].dependencies = ["T1"]
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
    if (!result.ok) {
      expect(result.errors.join(" ")).toContain("cycle")
    }
  })

  it("rejects wrong planning_owner or runtime_target", () => {
    const bad = { ...baseGraph(), planning_owner: "stoneforge" }
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(bad)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
  })

  it("accepts optional dispatch_policy.max_replan_cycles", () => {
    const g = {
      ...baseGraph(),
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false, max_replan_cycles: 3 },
    }
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(g)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (result.ok) {
      expect(result.graph.dispatch_policy.max_replan_cycles).toBe(3)
    }
  })

  it("accepts recursive generation metadata for terminal child taskCards", () => {
    const graph = baseGraph() as any
    graph.dispatch_policy = {
      requires_human_approval_before_activation: false,
      max_generation_depth: 3,
      max_fan_out: 5,
    }
    graph.tasks[0] = {
      ...graph.tasks[0],
      generation: 1,
      parent_run_id: "run-polynomial-root",
      parent_task_card_id: "taskCard-polynomial-root",
      decomposition_policy: "terminal",
    }
    graph.tasks[1] = {
      ...graph.tasks[1],
      generation: 1,
      parent_run_id: "run-polynomial-root",
      parent_task_card_id: "taskCard-polynomial-root",
      decomposition_policy: "terminal",
    }

    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(true)
    if (result.ok) {
      expect(result.graph.tasks[0].generation).toBe(1)
      expect(result.graph.tasks[0].parent_task_card_id).toBe("taskCard-polynomial-root")
      expect(result.graph.tasks[0].decomposition_policy).toBe("terminal")
    }
  })

  it("rejects recursive taskCards without parent lineage", () => {
    const graph = baseGraph() as any
    graph.tasks[0] = {
      ...graph.tasks[0],
      generation: 1,
      decomposition_policy: "terminal",
    }

    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
    if (!result.ok) {
      expect(result.errors.join(" ")).toContain("parent_run_id is missing")
      expect(result.errors.join(" ")).toContain("parent_task_card_id is missing")
    }
  })

  it("requires orchestration-only tools for orchestrate taskCards", () => {
    const graph = baseGraph() as any
    graph.tasks[0] = {
      ...graph.tasks[0],
      decomposition_policy: "orchestrate",
      tools: ["xlotyl_orchestrate", "run_command"],
    }

    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
    expect(result.ok).toBe(false)
    if (!result.ok) {
      expect(result.errors.join(" ")).toContain("xlotyl_stoneforge_validate")
      expect(result.errors.join(" ")).toContain("forbids write tool 'run_command'")
    }
  })
})
```
