```ts
import path from "node:path"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { generateAdapters } from "./adapters.js"
import { defaultSourceRegistry } from "./manifest.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot, defaultWorkspaceRoot } from "./paths.js"
import { importPinnedSources } from "./registry.js"

describe("platform adapter generation", () => {
  it("generates native files for Codex, Claude Code, Cursor, and Antigravity", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"],
    })

    expect(files.map((file) => file.path)).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining([
        ".agents/plugins/marketplace.json",
        ".agents/skills/ce-plan/SKILL.md",
        ".agents/skills/ce-code-review/SKILL.md",
        ".agents/skills/ce-brainstorm/SKILL.md",
        "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.codex-plugin/plugin.json",
        "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.mcp.json",
        "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/ce-plan/SKILL.md",
        "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/ce-code-review/SKILL.md",
        ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.claude-plugin/plugin.json",
        ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.mcp.json",
        ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/commands/ce-code-review.md",
        ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/agents/review/ce-security-reviewer.md",
        ".cursor/rules/xlotyl-core-dev-services.mdc",
        ".cursor/rules/xlotyl-compound-engineering.mdc",
        ".cursor/mcp.json",
        ".agents/rules/xlotyl-core-dev-services.md",
        ".agents/workflows/ce-code-review.md",
        ".agents/workflows/xlotyl-orchestrate.md",
        ".gemini/antigravity/mcp_config.fragment.json",
      ]),
    )
  })

  it("excludes quarantined hooks and mutating MCP servers from generated adapters", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["claude", "codex"],
    })
    const allContent = files.map((file) => file.content).join("\n")

    expect(allContent).not.toContain("private-journal-mcp")
    expect(allContent).not.toContain("runlayer-block-env-hook")
    expect(allContent).toContain("smolagents:code-agent")
    expect(allContent).toContain("spectacular:spec-plan-execute")
    expect(allContent).toContain("xlotyl-dev-services")
  })

  it("emits callable compound engineering wrappers while keeping deferred utilities listed-only", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"],
    })
    const paths = files.map((file) => file.path)
    const codexPlugin = files.find(
      (file) => file.path === "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.codex-plugin/plugin.json",
    )

    expect(paths).toContain(".agents/skills/ce-code-review/SKILL.md")
    expect(paths).toContain(".agents/skills/ce-compound-refresh/SKILL.md")
    expect(paths).not.toContain(".agents/skills/ce-worktree/SKILL.md")
    expect(paths).not.toContain("plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/ce-commit/SKILL.md")
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-worktree")
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain("listedOnlyCapabilities")
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain("callableCapabilities")
  })

  it("emits Codex plugin metadata accepted by the local marketplace", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["codex"],
    })
    const marketplace = files.find((file) => file.path === ".agents/plugins/marketplace.json")
    const codexPlugin = files.find(
      (file) => file.path === "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.codex-plugin/plugin.json",
    )

    expect(marketplace?.content).toContain('"authentication": "ON_USE"')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"screenshots": []')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"developerName": "XLOTYL"')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"label": "Working for Codex"')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"id": "codex-supervised-swarm"')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"role": "adapter-pathway"')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"isDefaultPathway": false')
    expect(codexPlugin?.content).toContain('"sourceOfTruth": "xlotyl-core-dev-services"')
  })

  it("points Codex MCP launch config at the local workspace install instead of a global bin", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["codex"],
    })
    const mcpConfig = files.find((file) => file.path === "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.mcp.json")

    expect(mcpConfig?.content).toContain(`"command": "node"`)
    expect(mcpConfig?.content).toContain(
      path.join(defaultWorkspaceRoot(), "node_modules", "tsx", "dist", "cli.mjs"),
    )
    expect(mcpConfig?.content).toContain(path.join(defaultCoreDevServicesRoot(), "src", "cli.ts"))
    expect(mcpConfig?.content).not.toContain(`"command": "xlotyl-dev-services"`)
  })

  it("installs ce-plan as its own Codex skill wrapper", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["codex"],
    })
    const repoSkill = files.find((file) => file.path === ".agents/skills/ce-plan/SKILL.md")
    const pluginSkill = files.find((file) => file.path === "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/ce-plan/SKILL.md")

    expect(repoSkill?.content).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-plan")
    expect(pluginSkill?.content).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-plan")
    expect(repoSkill?.content).toContain("Call the `xlotyl_orchestrate` MCP tool")
    expect(repoSkill?.content).toContain("Codex pathway label: Working for Codex")
    expect(repoSkill?.content).toContain("This is a Codex adapter pathway, not the main XLOTYL execution pathway")
    expect(repoSkill?.content).toContain("If the user explicitly asks for Codex swarm agents")
    expect(repoSkill?.content).toContain("xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan")
  })

  it("does not leak the Codex swarm pathway as the default guidance for other adapters", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["claude", "cursor", "antigravity"],
    })
    const claudeSkill = files.find(
      (file) => file.path === ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/ce-plan/SKILL.md",
    )
    const claudePlugin = files.find(
      (file) => file.path === ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.claude-plugin/plugin.json",
    )
    const cursorRule = files.find((file) => file.path === ".cursor/rules/xlotyl-core-dev-services.mdc")
    const antigravityRule = files.find((file) => file.path === ".agents/rules/xlotyl-core-dev-services.md")

    expect(claudeSkill?.content).not.toContain("xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan")
    expect(claudeSkill?.content).not.toContain("Codex pathway label: Working for Codex")
    expect(claudeSkill?.content).toContain("Do not treat the Codex-supervised swarm pathway as the default")
    expect(claudePlugin?.content).toContain('"adapterPathways": []')
    expect(cursorRule?.content).toContain("not the default Cursor pathway")
    expect(antigravityRule?.content).toContain("not the default Antigravity pathway")
  })

  it("installs agent-native CE workflows as orchestration-backed Codex wrappers", () => {
    const files = generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      targets: ["codex"],
    })
    const repoAuditSkill = files.find((file) => file.path === ".agents/skills/ce-agent-native-audit/SKILL.md")
    const pluginAuditSkill = files.find(
      (file) => file.path === "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/ce-agent-native-audit/SKILL.md",
    )
    const repoArchitectureSkill = files.find(
      (file) => file.path === ".agents/skills/ce-agent-native-architecture/SKILL.md",
    )

    expect(repoAuditSkill?.content).toContain("Call the `xlotyl_orchestrate` MCP tool")
    expect(repoAuditSkill?.content).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit")
    expect(pluginAuditSkill?.content).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit")
    expect(repoArchitectureSkill?.content).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-architecture")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/adapters.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 18312 bytes

```ts
import path from "node:path"
import { capabilityEmissionMode, isCapabilityCallableForTarget, type Capability, type Target } from "./manifest.js"
import { CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY } from "./codex-swarm.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot, defaultWorkspaceRoot } from "./paths.js"
import type { ImportedInventory } from "./registry.js"

export interface VirtualFile {
  target: Target | "shared"
  path: string
  content: string
}

export interface AdapterOptions {
  targets: Target[]
}

function stableJson(value: unknown): string {
  return `${JSON.stringify(value, null, 2)}\n`
}

function mcpConfig(): Record<string, unknown> {
  const workspaceRoot = defaultWorkspaceRoot()
  const coreDevServicesRoot = defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()
  return {
    mcpServers: {
      "xlotyl-dev-services": {
        command: "node",
        args: [
          path.join(workspaceRoot, "node_modules", "tsx", "dist", "cli.mjs"),
          path.join(coreDevServicesRoot, "src", "cli.ts"),
          "mcp",
        ],
      },
    },
  }
}

function pathwayGuidance(target: Target): string[] {
  if (target === "codex") {
    return [
      `Codex pathway label: ${CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY.label} (${CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY.id}).`,
      "This is a Codex adapter pathway, not the main XLOTYL execution pathway.",
      "If the user explicitly asks for Codex swarm agents, call `xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan` and follow its dispatch phases.",
      "Keep final aggregation in the main Codex thread unless the returned pipeline says otherwise.",
    ]
  }

  return [
    "XLOTYL Core Dev Services remains the source of truth for tools, taskCards, and orchestration policy.",
    "Use platform-native dispatch only through an approved adapter pathway for this target.",
    "Do not treat the Codex-supervised swarm pathway as the default for this platform.",
  ]
}

function orchestrationSkill(target: Target): string {
  return [
    "---",
    "name: xlotyl-orchestrate",
    "description: Use when a task should be broken into governed XLOTYL swarm taskCards before execution.",
    "---",
    "",
    "Call the `xlotyl_orchestrate` MCP tool with the user's prompt and selected workflow.",
    "Use the returned task graph as the source of truth for agent taskCard scope, tools, metrics, and dependencies.",
    ...pathwayGuidance(target),
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}

function workflowSkillName(workflowId: string): string {
  const scoped = workflowId.includes(":") ? workflowId.split(":").at(-1) ?? workflowId : workflowId
  return scoped.toLowerCase()
}

function workflowSkill(workflowId: string, workflowIntent: string, target: Target): string {
  const skillName = workflowSkillName(workflowId)
  return [
    "---",
    `name: ${skillName}`,
    `description: Use when you need to ${workflowIntent.charAt(0).toLowerCase()}${workflowIntent.slice(1)}`,
    "---",
    "",
    `Call the \`xlotyl_orchestrate\` MCP tool with workflowId \`${workflowId}\` and the user's prompt.`,
    "Use the returned task graph as the source of truth for phases, taskCards, metrics, and acceptance criteria.",
    ...pathwayGuidance(target),
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}

function capabilityLocalId(capability: Capability): string {
  return capability.id.includes(":") ? capability.id.split(":").slice(1).join(":") : capability.id
}

function capabilitySkill(capability: Capability): string {
  const skillName = capabilityLocalId(capability).split("/").at(-1) ?? capability.id
  return [
    "---",
    `name: ${skillName}`,
    `description: ${capability.description ?? `Imported XLOTYL capability ${capability.id}.`}`,
    "---",
    "",
    `Use the imported XLOTYL capability \`${capability.id}\`.`,
    "Call `xlotyl_capability_get` when you need canonical metadata, aliases, target support, or execution responsibility.",
    "Keep any mutating, shell, network, or secret-bearing action inside the authority of the current XLOTYL taskCard.",
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}

function claudeCommand(capabilityOrWorkflowId: string, description: string): string {
  return [
    `Use XLOTYL Core Dev Services for \`${capabilityOrWorkflowId}\`.`,
    "",
    description,
    "",
    "If this is an orchestration workflow, call `xlotyl_orchestrate` first and execute only the returned taskCards.",
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}

function claudeAgent(capability: Capability): string {
  const localId = capabilityLocalId(capability)
  const name = localId.split("/").at(-1) ?? localId
  return [
    "---",
    `name: ${name}`,
    `description: ${capability.description ?? `Imported XLOTYL agent ${capability.id}.`}`,
    "tools: Read",
    "---",
    "",
    `You are a thin platform wrapper for \`${capability.id}\`.`,
    "Execute only the scoped XLOTYL taskCard you are given. Do not broaden scope or request unscoped shell authority.",
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}

function capabilitiesForTarget(inventory: ImportedInventory, target: Target) {
  return inventory.capabilities.filter(
    (capability) => capability.approval === "approved" && capability.targets.includes(target),
  )
}

function capabilityIdsByMode(inventory: ImportedInventory, target: Target, mode: "callable" | "listedOnly") {
  return capabilitiesForTarget(inventory, target)
    .filter((capability) => capabilityEmissionMode(capability, target) === mode)
    .map((capability) => capability.id)
}

function callableCapabilities(inventory: ImportedInventory, target: Target) {
  return capabilitiesForTarget(inventory, target).filter((capability) =>
    isCapabilityCallableForTarget(capability, target),
  )
}

function listedOnlyCapabilities(inventory: ImportedInventory, target: Target) {
  return capabilitiesForTarget(inventory, target).filter(
    (capability) => capabilityEmissionMode(capability, target) === "listedOnly",
  )
}

function approvedOrchestrationPlugins(inventory: ImportedInventory, target: Target) {
  return inventory.orchestrationPlugins.filter((plugin) => {
    const capability = inventory.capabilities.find((candidate) => candidate.id === plugin.id)
    return plugin.approval === "approved" && (!capability || isCapabilityCallableForTarget(capability, target))
  })
}

function codexFiles(inventory: ImportedInventory): VirtualFile[] {
  const approvedCapabilityIds = capabilitiesForTarget(inventory, "codex").map((capability) => capability.id)
  const workflowSkills = approvedOrchestrationPlugins(inventory, "codex").flatMap((plugin): VirtualFile[] => {
    const skillName = workflowSkillName(plugin.id)
    const content = workflowSkill(plugin.id, plugin.workflowIntent, "codex")
    return [
      {
        target: "codex",
        path: `.agents/skills/${skillName}/SKILL.md`,
        content,
      },
      {
        target: "codex",
        path: `plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/${skillName}/SKILL.md`,
        content,
      },
    ]
  })
  const importedSkillFiles = callableCapabilities(inventory, "codex")
    .filter((capability) => capability.sourceId === "compound-engineering" && capability.kind === "skill")
    .flatMap((capability): VirtualFile[] => {
      const skillName = capabilityLocalId(capability)
      const content = capabilitySkill(capability)
      return [
        {
          target: "codex",
          path: `.agents/skills/${skillName}/SKILL.md`,
          content,
        },
        {
          target: "codex",
          path: `plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/${skillName}/SKILL.md`,
          content,
        },
      ]
    })

  return [
    {
      target: "codex",
      path: ".agents/skills/xlotyl-orchestrate/SKILL.md",
      content: orchestrationSkill("codex"),
    },
    {
      target: "codex",
      path: ".agents/plugins/marketplace.json",
      content: stableJson({
        name: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
        interface: { displayName: "XLOTYL Core Dev Services" },
        plugins: [
          {
            name: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
            source: { source: "local", path: "./plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services" },
            policy: { installation: "AVAILABLE", authentication: "ON_USE" },
            category: "Developer Tools",
          },
        ],
      }),
    },
    {
      target: "codex",
      path: "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.codex-plugin/plugin.json",
      content: stableJson({
        name: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
        version: "0.1.0",
        description: "Portable XLOTYL skills, tools, MCP, and orchestration adapters.",
        skills: "./skills/",
        mcpServers: "./.mcp.json",
        interface: {
          displayName: "XLOTYL Core Dev Services",
          shortDescription: "Portable dev services and swarm orchestration.",
          longDescription:
            "Portable XLOTYL development services for Codex, including CE workflow skills and the xlotyl-dev-services MCP tools.",
          developerName: "XLOTYL",
          category: "Developer Tools",
          capabilities: ["Read", "Write"],
          defaultPrompt: [
            "Plan this with CE workflow taskCards",
            "Search XLOTYL capabilities",
            "Run an agent-native audit",
          ],
          brandColor: "#2563EB",
          screenshots: [],
        },
        xlotyl: {
          sourceOfTruth: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
          defaultPathwayPolicy:
            "Core Dev Services is canonical. Platform pathways are labeled adapter bridges and must not become the default cross-platform route by accident.",
          adapterPathways: [CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY],
          approvedCapabilities: approvedCapabilityIds,
          callableCapabilities: capabilityIdsByMode(inventory, "codex", "callable"),
          listedOnlyCapabilities: capabilityIdsByMode(inventory, "codex", "listedOnly"),
        },
      }),
    },
    {
      target: "codex",
      path: "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/xlotyl-orchestrate/SKILL.md",
      content: orchestrationSkill("codex"),
    },
    {
      target: "codex",
      path: "plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.mcp.json",
      content: stableJson(mcpConfig()),
    },
    ...workflowSkills,
    ...importedSkillFiles,
  ]
}

function claudeFiles(inventory: ImportedInventory): VirtualFile[] {
  const approvedCapabilityIds = capabilitiesForTarget(inventory, "claude").map((capability) => capability.id)
  const ceCallableSkills = callableCapabilities(inventory, "claude").filter(
    (capability) => capability.sourceId === "compound-engineering" && capability.kind === "skill",
  )
  const ceAgents = callableCapabilities(inventory, "claude").filter(
    (capability) => capability.sourceId === "compound-engineering" && capability.kind === "agent",
  )
  const workflowPlugins = approvedOrchestrationPlugins(inventory, "claude")

  return [
    {
      target: "claude",
      path: ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.claude-plugin/plugin.json",
      content: stableJson({
        name: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
        version: "0.1.0",
        description: "Portable XLOTYL skills, tools, MCP, and orchestration adapters.",
        skills: "./skills/",
        commands: "./commands/",
        agents: "./agents/",
        mcpServers: "./.mcp.json",
        xlotyl: {
          sourceOfTruth: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
          defaultPathwayPolicy:
            "Core Dev Services is canonical. Platform pathways are labeled adapter bridges and must not become the default cross-platform route by accident.",
          adapterPathways: [],
          approvedCapabilities: approvedCapabilityIds,
          callableCapabilities: capabilityIdsByMode(inventory, "claude", "callable"),
          listedOnlyCapabilities: capabilityIdsByMode(inventory, "claude", "listedOnly"),
        },
      }),
    },
    {
      target: "claude",
      path: ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/xlotyl-orchestrate/SKILL.md",
      content: orchestrationSkill("claude"),
    },
    {
      target: "claude",
      path: ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/commands/xlotyl-orchestrate.md",
      content: "Use XLOTYL Core Dev Services to compile this prompt into governed swarm taskCards.\n",
    },
    {
      target: "claude",
      path: ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/agents/xlotyl-swarm-worker.md",
      content: [
        "---",
        "name: xlotyl-swarm-worker",
        "description: Executes a single scoped XLOTYL taskCard.",
        "tools: Read, Edit, Bash",
        "---",
        "Execute only the taskCard provided by XLOTYL. Do not broaden scope.",
        "",
      ].join("\n"),
    },
    {
      target: "claude",
      path: ".claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/.mcp.json",
      content: stableJson(mcpConfig()),
    },
    ...workflowPlugins.flatMap((plugin): VirtualFile[] => {
      const name = workflowSkillName(plugin.id)
      const content = workflowSkill(plugin.id, plugin.workflowIntent, "claude")
      return [
        {
          target: "claude",
          path: `.claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/${name}/SKILL.md`,
          content,
        },
        {
          target: "claude",
          path: `.claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/commands/${name}.md`,
          content: claudeCommand(plugin.id, plugin.workflowIntent),
        },
      ]
    }),
    ...ceCallableSkills.flatMap((capability): VirtualFile[] => {
      const localId = capabilityLocalId(capability)
      return [
        {
          target: "claude",
          path: `.claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/skills/${localId}/SKILL.md`,
          content: capabilitySkill(capability),
        },
        {
          target: "claude",
          path: `.claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/commands/${localId}.md`,
          content: claudeCommand(capability.id, capability.description ?? ""),
        },
      ]
    }),
    ...ceAgents.map((capability): VirtualFile => ({
      target: "claude",
      path: `.claude/plugins/xlotyl-core-dev-services/agents/${capabilityLocalId(capability)}.md`,
      content: claudeAgent(capability),
    })),
  ]
}

function cursorFiles(inventory: ImportedInventory): VirtualFile[] {
  const workflows = approvedOrchestrationPlugins(inventory, "cursor").map((plugin) => plugin.id)
  const deferred = listedOnlyCapabilities(inventory, "cursor")
    .filter((capability) => capability.sourceId === "compound-engineering")
    .map((capability) => capability.id)

  return [
    {
      target: "cursor",
      path: ".cursor/rules/xlotyl-core-dev-services.mdc",
      content: [
        "---",
        "description: Invoke XLOTYL Core Dev Services for portable skills, MCP tools, and governed swarm orchestration.",
        "alwaysApply: true",
        "---",
        "",
        "For orchestration or breakout-task workflows, call the `xlotyl_orchestrate` MCP tool before implementation.",
        "Use XLOTYL taskCards as the source of truth for scope, metrics, tools, and dependencies.",
        "The Codex-supervised swarm pathway is labeled Working for Codex and is not the default Cursor pathway.",
        "",
      ].join("\n"),
    },
    {
      target: "cursor",
      path: ".cursor/rules/xlotyl-compound-engineering.mdc",
      content: [
        "---",
        "description: Invoke XLOTYL for Compound Engineering workflows and respect listed-only CE utilities.",
        "alwaysApply: true",
        "---",
        "",
        "Callable Compound Engineering workflows:",
        ...workflows.map((workflow) => `- \`${workflow}\``),
        "",
        "Listed-only Compound Engineering utilities are visible features, but direct shell or mutating execution waits for the XLOTYL permission broker:",
        ...deferred.map((capability) => `- \`${capability}\``),
        "",
      ].join("\n"),
    },
    {
      target: "cursor",
      path: ".cursor/mcp.json",
      content: stableJson(mcpConfig()),
    },
  ]
}

function antigravityFiles(inventory: ImportedInventory): VirtualFile[] {
  const workflows = approvedOrchestrationPlugins(inventory, "antigravity")
  const deferred = listedOnlyCapabilities(inventory, "antigravity")
    .filter((capability) => capability.sourceId === "compound-engineering")
    .map((capability) => capability.id)

  return [
    {
      target: "antigravity",
      path: ".agents/rules/xlotyl-core-dev-services.md",
      content: [
        "# XLOTYL Core Dev Services",
        "",
        "Use XLOTYL orchestration for workflows that need swarm task breakout.",
        "Platform-native agents are wrappers; XLOTYL owns task delineation and metrics.",
        "The Codex-supervised swarm pathway is labeled Working for Codex and is not the default Antigravity pathway.",
        "",
      ].join("\n"),
    },
    {
      target: "antigravity",
      path: ".agents/workflows/xlotyl-orchestrate.md",
      content: "Call `xlotyl_orchestrate` with the user prompt, then follow the returned task graph.\n",
    },
    {
      target: "antigravity",
      path: ".agents/rules/xlotyl-compound-engineering.md",
      content: [
        "# Compound Engineering Through XLOTYL",
        "",
        "Use XLOTYL orchestration for callable Compound Engineering workflows.",
        "Listed-only CE utilities are visible features; direct shell, hook, or mutating authority is deferred.",
        "",
        ...deferred.map((capability) => `- ${capability}`),
        "",
      ].join("\n"),
    },
    ...workflows.map((plugin): VirtualFile => ({
      target: "antigravity",
      path: `.agents/workflows/${workflowSkillName(plugin.id)}.md`,
      content: `Call \`xlotyl_orchestrate\` with workflowId \`${plugin.id}\`, then follow the returned task graph.\n`,
    })),
    {
      target: "antigravity",
      path: ".gemini/antigravity/mcp_config.fragment.json",
      content: stableJson(mcpConfig()),
    },
  ]
}

export function generateAdapters(
  inventory: ImportedInventory,
  options: AdapterOptions = { targets: ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"] },
): VirtualFile[] {
  const files: VirtualFile[] = []
  for (const target of options.targets) {
    if (target === "codex") {
      files.push(...codexFiles(inventory))
    } else if (target === "claude") {
      files.push(...claudeFiles(inventory))
    } else if (target === "cursor") {
      files.push(...cursorFiles(inventory))
    } else if (target === "antigravity") {
      files.push(...antigravityFiles(inventory))
    }
  }
  return files
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/agent-runtime.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 1439 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { createAgentRunStore } from "./agent-runtime.js"

describe("agent taskCard runtime queue", () => {
  it("queues taskCards, exposes status, and records results", () => {
    const store = createAgentRunStore({ now: () => "2026-04-21T17:30:00.000Z" })

    const queued = store.queueRun({
      taskId: "task-002",
      runtime: "codex-supervised",
      task: { id: "task-002", expectedOutput: "Implementation handoff." },
    })

    expect(queued).toMatchObject({
      runId: "run-0001-task-002",
      taskId: "task-002",
      status: "queued",
      coordinator: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
    })
    expect(store.status({ runId: queued.runId })).toMatchObject({ runId: queued.runId, status: "queued" })
    expect(store.result({ runId: queued.runId })).toMatchObject({ runId: queued.runId, status: "queued", result: null })

    const completed = store.completeRun({
      runId: queued.runId,
      result: { summary: "Implemented bounded taskCard." },
      artifacts: [{ type: "handoff", path: "reports/task-002.md" }],
    })

    expect(completed).toMatchObject({ runId: queued.runId, status: "completed" })
    expect(store.result({ runId: queued.runId })).toMatchObject({
      runId: queued.runId,
      status: "completed",
      result: { summary: "Implemented bounded taskCard." },
      artifacts: [{ type: "handoff", path: "reports/task-002.md" }],
    })
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/agent-runtime.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4067 bytes

```ts
export type AgentRunStatus = "queued" | "running" | "completed" | "failed"

export interface AgentRunArtifact {
  type?: string
  path?: string
  url?: string
  [key: string]: unknown
}

export interface AgentRunRecord {
  runId: string
  taskId: string
  status: AgentRunStatus
  runtime: string
  task: Record<string, unknown>
  result: unknown | null
  artifacts: AgentRunArtifact[]
  queuedAt: string
  updatedAt: string
  completedAt?: string
  error?: string
  coordinator: "xlotyl-core-dev-services"
  nextAction: string
  /** Optional correlation when this run is tied to a Stoneforge-backed XLOTYL import. */
  stoneforge?: { xlotylRunId?: string; taskCardId?: string }
}

export interface AgentRunStoreOptions {
  now?: () => string
}

export interface QueueRunInput {
  taskId?: string
  runtime?: string
  task?: Record<string, unknown>
  stoneforge?: { xlotylRunId?: string; taskCardId?: string }
}

export interface AgentRunQuery {
  runId?: string
  taskId?: string
}

export interface CompleteRunInput {
  runId: string
  result?: unknown
  artifacts?: AgentRunArtifact[]
  error?: string
  status?: Extract<AgentRunStatus, "completed" | "failed">
}

function safeId(value: string): string {
  return value.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-").replace(/^-|-$/g, "") || "task"
}

function taskIdFor(input: QueueRunInput): string {
  const taskId = input.taskId ?? (typeof input.task?.id === "string" ? input.task.id : undefined)
  return taskId ?? "task-ad-hoc"
}

export function createAgentRunStore(options: AgentRunStoreOptions = {}) {
  const now = options.now ?? (() => new Date().toISOString())
  const runs = new Map<string, AgentRunRecord>()
  let nextRunNumber = 1

  function queueRun(input: QueueRunInput): AgentRunRecord {
    const taskId = taskIdFor(input)
    const timestamp = now()
    const record: AgentRunRecord = {
      runId: `run-${String(nextRunNumber).padStart(4, "0")}-${safeId(taskId)}`,
      taskId,
      status: "queued",
      runtime: input.runtime ?? "codex-supervised",
      task: input.task ?? {},
      result: null,
      artifacts: [],
      queuedAt: timestamp,
      updatedAt: timestamp,
      coordinator: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
      nextAction:
        "Dispatch this taskCard through the supervising client, then call xlotyl_agent_complete with the handoff result.",
      stoneforge: input.stoneforge,
    }
    nextRunNumber += 1
    runs.set(record.runId, record)
    return record
  }

  function status(query: AgentRunQuery = {}): AgentRunRecord | { runs: AgentRunRecord[] } | null {
    if (query.runId) {
      return runs.get(query.runId) ?? null
    }
    const allRuns = Array.from(runs.values())
    if (query.taskId) {
      return { runs: allRuns.filter((run) => run.taskId === query.taskId) }
    }
    return { runs: allRuns }
  }

  function completeRun(input: CompleteRunInput): AgentRunRecord {
    const existing = runs.get(input.runId)
    if (!existing) {
      throw new Error(`Unknown agent run: ${input.runId}`)
    }
    const timestamp = now()
    const updated: AgentRunRecord = {
      ...existing,
      status: input.status ?? (input.error ? "failed" : "completed"),
      result: input.result ?? null,
      artifacts: input.artifacts ?? [],
      error: input.error,
      updatedAt: timestamp,
      completedAt: timestamp,
      nextAction: input.error
        ? "Review the failed taskCard and decide whether to retry or rescope."
        : "Review this taskCard handoff before aggregation.",
    }
    runs.set(updated.runId, updated)
    return updated
  }

  function result(query: Required<Pick<AgentRunQuery, "runId">>) {
    const record = runs.get(query.runId)
    if (!record) {
      return null
    }
    return {
      runId: record.runId,
      taskId: record.taskId,
      status: record.status,
      result: record.result,
      artifacts: record.artifacts,
      error: record.error,
      completedAt: record.completedAt,
      nextAction: record.nextAction,
    }
  }

  return {
    queueRun,
    status,
    completeRun,
    result,
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/capability-package/graph-compiler.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4290 bytes

```ts
import { z } from "zod"

import type { XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "../stoneforge/contract.js"
import { getCapabilityPackage } from "./index.js"

/**
 * Package-aware graph compiler (skeleton).
 *
 * This is the deterministic bridge between:
 * - capability package (manifest constraints)
 * - a source goal/prompt
 * - and a Stoneforge-target XLOTYL graph payload.
 *
 * Non-goals (in this pass):
 * - model calls
 * - dynamic decomposition
 * - routing policy decisions
 *
 * The intent is to make capability packages become *compiler inputs* without coupling
 * the compiler to dispatch or to any provider models.
 */

export const terminalityPolicySchema = z.enum(["require_terminal", "allow_auto"])
export type TerminalityPolicy = z.infer<typeof terminalityPolicySchema>

export interface CompileCapabilityPackageGraphInput {
  packageId: string
  sourceGoal: string
  workflowId?: string
  workflowTitle?: string
  context?: Record<string, unknown>
  terminalityPolicy?: TerminalityPolicy
}

export interface CompileCapabilityPackageGraphSuccess {
  ok: true
  graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph
}

export interface CompileCapabilityPackageGraphFailure {
  ok: false
  errors: string[]
}

export type CompileCapabilityPackageGraphResult = CompileCapabilityPackageGraphSuccess | CompileCapabilityPackageGraphFailure

function nowRunId(prefix: string): string {
  return `${prefix}-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, "-")}`
}

/**
 * Compile a minimal, deterministic graph for a capability package.
 *
 * Today: creates a single task that is either terminal (require_terminal) or auto.
 * Later: can expand into a multi-task template and attach validators/adapters based on package constraints.
 */
export async function compileCapabilityPackageGraph(
  input: CompileCapabilityPackageGraphInput,
): Promise<CompileCapabilityPackageGraphResult> {
  const pkg = await getCapabilityPackage(input.packageId)
  if (!pkg) {
    return { ok: false, errors: [`unknown capability package: ${input.packageId}`] }
  }

  const terminality = input.terminalityPolicy ?? "allow_auto"
  const decomposition_policy = terminality === "require_terminal" ? "terminal" : "auto"

  const runtimeEnv = pkg.runtime_environments[0]?.id
  const adapter = pkg.execution_adapters[0]?.id
  const validatorIds = pkg.validators.map((v) => v.id)
  const isTerminal = decomposition_policy === "terminal"

  const graph: unknown = {
    run_id: nowRunId(`run-${pkg.package_id}`),
    workflow_id: input.workflowId ?? `capability-package:${pkg.package_id}`,
    workflow_title: input.workflowTitle ?? pkg.label,
    source_goal: input.sourceGoal,
    planning_owner: "xlotyl",
    runtime_target: "stoneforge",
    execution_mode: "xlotyl_stoneforge",
    dispatch_policy: {
      requires_human_approval_before_activation: true,
    },
    phases: [
      { id: "p1", name: "compile", purpose: "Deterministic graph compile from capability package constraints." },
    ],
    tasks: [
      {
        id: "task-001",
        phase_id: "p1",
        title: `${pkg.label}: ${input.sourceGoal}`,
        task_card_type: "capability_package_task",
        priority: 1,
        dependencies: [],
        tools: [],
        acceptance_criteria: ["Meets acceptance criteria declared in task card."],
        objective: input.sourceGoal,
        runtime_environment_id: runtimeEnv,
        execution_adapter_id: adapter,
        validator_ids: validatorIds.length > 0 ? validatorIds : undefined,
        expected_artifacts: isTerminal ? ["VERIFICATION_REPORT"] : undefined,
        decomposition_policy,
        orchestration_state: {
          ambiguity_level: "none",
          terminality: isTerminal ? "terminal" : "needs_decomposition",
          missing_information: [],
          recommended_next_step: isTerminal ? "execute" : "decompose",
          allowed_executor_tiers: ["deterministic_validator", "local_general_model", "coding_model", "strategic_reviewer"],
          required_contracts: ["verification_report:1.0.0"],
        },
      },
    ],
  }

  const validated = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph)
  if (!validated.ok) {
    return { ok: false, errors: validated.errors }
  }
  return { ok: true, graph: validated.graph }
}

```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/capability-package/index.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2141 bytes

```ts
import { loadCapabilityPackageManifests, type CapabilityPackageManifest } from "./loader.js"

/**
 * Capability package index.
 *
 * The index is used for observability (docs/operator UI/audits/routing diagnostics).
 * It is intentionally not a dispatch controller in this pass.
 */

export interface CapabilityPackageIndex {
  manifests: CapabilityPackageManifest[]
  byId: Map<string, CapabilityPackageManifest>
}

export async function buildCapabilityPackageIndex(): Promise<CapabilityPackageIndex> {
  const manifests = await loadCapabilityPackageManifests()
  const byId = new Map<string, CapabilityPackageManifest>()
  for (const manifest of manifests) {
    byId.set(manifest.package_id, manifest)
  }
  return { manifests, byId }
}

export async function getCapabilityPackage(package_id: string): Promise<CapabilityPackageManifest | undefined> {
  const index = await buildCapabilityPackageIndex()
  return index.byId.get(package_id)
}

export async function findPackagesByDomain(domain: string): Promise<CapabilityPackageManifest[]> {
  const index = await buildCapabilityPackageIndex()
  return index.manifests.filter((manifest) => manifest.domain === domain)
}

export async function findPackagesByRuntimeEnvironment(runtime_environment_id: string): Promise<CapabilityPackageManifest[]> {
  const index = await buildCapabilityPackageIndex()
  return index.manifests.filter((manifest) =>
    manifest.runtime_environments.some((env) => env.id === runtime_environment_id),
  )
}

export async function findPackagesByExecutionAdapter(execution_adapter_id: string): Promise<CapabilityPackageManifest[]> {
  const index = await buildCapabilityPackageIndex()
  return index.manifests.filter((manifest) =>
    manifest.execution_adapters.some((adapter) => adapter.id === execution_adapter_id),
  )
}

export async function findPackagesByDomainKnowledgePackage(
  domain_knowledge_package_artifact_ref: string,
): Promise<CapabilityPackageManifest[]> {
  const index = await buildCapabilityPackageIndex()
  return index.manifests.filter((manifest) => manifest.domain_knowledge_packages.includes(domain_knowledge_package_artifact_ref))
}

```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/capability-package/loader.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3600 bytes

```ts
import fs from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import { z } from "zod"

import { defaultWorkspaceRoot } from "../paths.js"
import { capabilityPackagesRoot } from "./resolve.js"

/**
 * Capability package manifest loader.
 *
 * This module is intentionally read-only and \"observable-first\":
 * - it loads and validates manifests for docs/UI/audit use
 * - it does NOT control runtime dispatch in this pass
 */

export const capabilityPackageStatusSchema = z.enum(["experimental", "active", "deprecated", "reserved"])

export const capabilityPackageRuntimeEnvironmentSchema = z
  .object({
    id: z.string().min(1),
    status: capabilityPackageStatusSchema,
    summary: z.string().min(1).max(240).optional(),
    implementation_path: z.string().min(1).optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export const capabilityPackageExecutionAdapterSchema = z
  .object({
    id: z.string().min(1),
    summary: z.string().min(1).max(240).optional(),
    implementation_path: z.string().min(1).optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export const capabilityPackageValidatorSchema = z
  .object({
    id: z.string().min(1),
    summary: z.string().min(1).max(240).optional(),
    path: z.string().min(1).optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export const capabilityPackageSmokeSchema = z
  .object({
    required: z.boolean(),
    mode: z.enum(["local-artifact", "sf-cli"]).optional(),
    example_task_card: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    source_goal: z.string().min(1).max(280).optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export const capabilityPackageManifestSchema = z
  .object({
    schema_version: z.literal("1.0.0"),
    package_id: z.string().min(1),
    label: z.string().min(1),
    domain: z.string().min(1),
    summary: z.string().min(1),
    status: capabilityPackageStatusSchema,
    owners: z.array(z.string().min(1)).min(1),
    domain_knowledge_packages: z.array(z.string().min(1)).min(1),
    runtime_environments: z.array(capabilityPackageRuntimeEnvironmentSchema).min(1),
    execution_adapters: z.array(capabilityPackageExecutionAdapterSchema).min(1),
    validators: z.array(capabilityPackageValidatorSchema).min(1),
    techniques: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    theory: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    schemas: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    artifacts: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    failure_modes: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    escalation_rules: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    verification_reports: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    smoke: capabilityPackageSmokeSchema.optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export type CapabilityPackageManifest = z.infer<typeof capabilityPackageManifestSchema>

export interface LoadCapabilityPackageOptions {
  workspaceRoot?: string
}

export async function loadCapabilityPackageManifests(
  options: LoadCapabilityPackageOptions = {},
): Promise<CapabilityPackageManifest[]> {
  const workspaceRoot = options.workspaceRoot ?? defaultWorkspaceRoot()
  const root = capabilityPackagesRoot(workspaceRoot)
  const entries = await fs.readdir(root, { withFileTypes: true }).catch(() => [])
  const manifests: CapabilityPackageManifest[] = []

  for (const entry of entries) {
    if (!entry.isDirectory()) {
      continue
    }
    const manifestPath = path.join(root, entry.name, "capability.manifest.json")
    const rawText = await fs.readFile(manifestPath, "utf-8").catch(() => null)
    if (!rawText) {
      continue
    }
    const rawJson = JSON.parse(rawText) as unknown
    const parsed = capabilityPackageManifestSchema.parse(rawJson)
    manifests.push(parsed)
  }

  return manifests
}

```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/capability-package/resolve.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 1122 bytes

```ts
import path from "node:path"

/**
 * Capability package resolution utilities.
 *
 * These helpers are intentionally small and deterministic. They exist to make
 * capability packages observable (docs/UI/audits) without coupling to dispatch.
 */

export type CapabilityArtifactKind = "domain-knowledge-package" | "runtime-environment" | "technique-card" | "theory-card"

export interface ParsedArtifactRef {
  scheme: "artifact"
  kind: CapabilityArtifactKind
  key: string
  raw: string
}

const artifactRefPattern =
  /^artifact:\/\/(?<kind>domain-knowledge-package|runtime-environment|technique-card|theory-card)\/(?<key>[A-Za-z0-9_\-]+)$/

export function parseArtifactRef(raw: string): ParsedArtifactRef | null {
  const trimmed = raw.trim()
  const match = trimmed.match(artifactRefPattern)
  if (!match?.groups) {
    return null
  }
  const kind = match.groups.kind as CapabilityArtifactKind
  const key = match.groups.key
  return { scheme: "artifact", kind, key, raw: trimmed }
}

export function capabilityPackagesRoot(workspaceRoot: string): string {
  return path.join(workspaceRoot, "capability-packages")
}

```

```ts
describe("xlotyl-dev-services CLI", () => {
  it("prints inventory, doctor, sync plan, and orchestration output", async () => {
    await expect(runCli(["inventory"])).resolves.toContain("compound-engineering")

              phase_id: "P1",
              title: "one",
              task_card_type: "t",
              priority: 1,
              dependencies: [],
              acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
            },
          ],
        }),
        "utf8",
      )
      process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_BINDING = "sf-cli"
      delete process.env.STONEFORGE_SF_BIN
      delete process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN

        "xsf binding sf-cli requires --sf-bin <path>",

      if (previousXlotylSfBin === undefined) {
        delete process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN
      } else {
        process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN = previousXlotylSfBin
      }
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/cli.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4777 bytes

```ts
#!/usr/bin/env node
import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url"
import { generateAdapters } from "./adapters.js"
import { approvalSchema, defaultSourceRegistry, targetSchema, type Target } from "./manifest.js"
import { runMcpStdio } from "./mcp.js"
import { orchestratePrompt } from "./orchestrator.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot } from "./paths.js"
import { approveCapability, importPinnedSources } from "./registry.js"
import { startHttpServer } from "./server.js"
import { createSyncPlan, writeSyncPlan } from "./sync.js"
import { runXsfCli } from "./stoneforge/xsf-cli.js"

function valueAfter(args: string[], flag: string): string | undefined {
  const index = args.indexOf(flag)
  return index >= 0 ? args[index + 1] : undefined
}

function hasFlag(args: string[], flag: string): boolean {
  return args.includes(flag)
}

function targetsFromArgs(args: string[]): Target[] {
  const requested = args.flatMap((arg, index) => (arg === "--target" ? [args[index + 1]] : []))
  const parsed = requested
    .filter((target): target is string => Boolean(target))
    .map((target) => targetSchema.parse(target))
  return parsed.length > 0 ? parsed : ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"]
}

export async function runCli(args: string[]): Promise<string> {
  const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
  const [command, subcommand] = args

  if (command === "xsf") {
    return runXsfCli(args.slice(1))
  }

  if (command === "inventory" || command === "import") {
    return `${JSON.stringify({ sources: inventory.sources, capabilities: inventory.capabilities }, null, 2)}\n`
  }
  if (command === "doctor") {
    return [
      "core-dev-services: ok",
      `sources: ${inventory.sources.length}`,
      `capabilities: ${inventory.capabilities.length}`,
      `orchestrationPlugins: ${inventory.orchestrationPlugins.length}`,
      "",
    ].join("\n")
  }
  if (command === "approve") {
    const capabilityId = args[1]
    if (!capabilityId) {
      throw new Error("approve requires a capability id")
    }
    const approval = approvalSchema.parse(valueAfter(args, "--approval") ?? "approved")
    const result = approveCapability(inventory, capabilityId, approval)
    return `${JSON.stringify({ capability: result.capability }, null, 2)}\n`
  }
  if (command === "sync" && subcommand === "plan") {
    const repoRoot = valueAfter(args, "--repo-root") ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()
    const plan = createSyncPlan(generateAdapters(inventory, { targets: targetsFromArgs(args) }), {
      repoRoot,
      global: hasFlag(args, "--global"),
      homeDir: valueAfter(args, "--home-dir"),
    })
    return `${JSON.stringify(plan, null, 2)}\n`
  }
  if (command === "sync" && subcommand === "apply") {
    const repoRoot = valueAfter(args, "--repo-root") ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()
    const plan = createSyncPlan(generateAdapters(inventory, { targets: targetsFromArgs(args) }), {
      repoRoot,
      global: hasFlag(args, "--global"),
      homeDir: valueAfter(args, "--home-dir"),
    })
    const result = await writeSyncPlan(plan)
    return `${JSON.stringify({ plannedWrites: plan.operations.length, ...result }, null, 2)}\n`
  }
  if (command === "orchestrate") {
    const workflowId = valueAfter(args, "--workflow") ?? "compound-engineering:ce-work"
    const prompt = valueAfter(args, "--prompt") ?? args.slice(1).join(" ")
    return `${JSON.stringify(orchestratePrompt(inventory, { workflowId, prompt }), null, 2)}\n`
  }
  if (command === "serve") {
    return "Starting xlotyl-core-dev-services HTTP server on 127.0.0.1:8765\n"
  }
  if (command === "mcp") {
    return "Starting xlotyl-dev-services MCP stdio server\n"
  }
  return [
    "Usage: xlotyl-dev-services <inventory|import|approve|doctor|serve|mcp|orchestrate|sync|xsf>",
    "Examples:",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services xsf validate --graph graph.json",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services xsf import --graph graph.json --workspace /repo",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services xsf replay --run <run_id> --workspace /repo",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services inventory",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services approve private-journal-mcp:server --approval approved",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services sync plan --target codex --repo-root /repo",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services sync apply --target antigravity --repo-root /repo --global --home-dir /Users/me",
    "  xlotyl-dev-services orchestrate --workflow compound-engineering:ce-work --prompt \"Ship adapters\"",
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}

async function main() {
  const args = process.argv.slice(2)
  if (args[0] === "serve") {
    await startHttpServer()
    return
  }
  if (args[0] === "mcp") {
    await runMcpStdio()
    return
  }
  process.stdout.write(await runCli(args))
}

if (process.argv[1] === fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)) {
  await main()
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/codex-swarm.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 1923 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { createCodexSwarmPipeline } from "./codex-swarm.js"
import { defaultSourceRegistry } from "./manifest.js"
import { orchestratePrompt } from "./orchestrator.js"
import { importPinnedSources } from "./registry.js"

describe("Codex swarm promotion pipeline", () => {
  it("turns a governed XLOTYL task graph into explicit Codex sub-agent dispatch phases", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
    const taskGraph = orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
      prompt: "Audit this app for agent-native architecture.",
    })

    const pipeline = createCodexSwarmPipeline({ taskGraph })

    expect(pipeline.pathway).toMatchObject({
      id: "codex-supervised-swarm",
      label: "Working for Codex",
      target: "codex",
      role: "adapter-pathway",
      sourceOfTruth: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
      isDefaultPathway: false,
    })
    expect(pipeline.dispatchMode).toBe("codex-subagents")
    expect(pipeline.requiresExplicitUserDelegation).toBe(true)
    expect(pipeline.taskGraphId).toBe(taskGraph.id)
    expect(pipeline.spawnQueue.map((taskCard) => [taskCard.taskId, taskCard.codexAgentType])).toEqual([
      ["task-001", "explorer"],
      ["task-002", "worker"],
      ["task-003", "explorer"],
    ])
    expect(pipeline.mainThreadTasks).toEqual(["task-004"])
    expect(pipeline.dispatchPhases.map((phase) => phase.taskIds)).toEqual([
      ["task-001"],
      ["task-002", "task-003"],
      ["task-004"],
    ])
    expect(pipeline.dispatchPhases[1]?.parallel).toBe(true)
    expect(pipeline.supervisorInstructions.join("\n")).toContain("Aggregate task-004 in the main Codex thread")
    expect(pipeline.activationPrompt).toContain("explicitly asked")
    expect(pipeline.spawnQueue[1]?.spawnPrompt).toContain("You are not alone in the codebase")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/codex-swarm.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 6137 bytes

```ts
import type { TaskGraph, TaskCard } from "./orchestrator.js"

export type CodexAgentType = "default" | "explorer" | "worker"

export interface PlatformPathwayLabel {
  id: string
  label: string
  target: "codex"
  status: "working"
  role: "adapter-pathway"
  sourceOfTruth: "xlotyl-core-dev-services"
  isDefaultPathway: false
  notes: string
}

export const CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY: PlatformPathwayLabel = {
  id: "codex-supervised-swarm",
  label: "Working for Codex",
  target: "codex",
  status: "working",
  role: "adapter-pathway",
  sourceOfTruth: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
  isDefaultPathway: false,
  notes:
    "Codex can supervise sub-agent dispatch for XLOTYL taskCards, but this is not the canonical cross-platform execution path.",
}

export interface CodexSpawnTaskCard {
  taskId: string
  title: string
  codexAgentType: CodexAgentType
  dependsOn: string[]
  canRunInParallel: boolean
  ownership: string
  allowedTools: string[]
  allowedMcpServers: string[]
  expectedOutput: string
  spawnPrompt: string
}

export interface CodexDispatchPhase {
  id: string
  taskIds: string[]
  parallel: boolean
  executor: "codex-subagents" | "main-thread"
  description: string
}

export interface CodexSwarmPipeline {
  id: string
  pathway: PlatformPathwayLabel
  dispatchMode: "codex-subagents"
  status: "ready-for-codex-supervision"
  requiresExplicitUserDelegation: true
  taskGraphId: string
  workflowId: string
  sourcePrompt: string
  activationPrompt: string
  spawnQueue: CodexSpawnTaskCard[]
  mainThreadTasks: string[]
  dispatchPhases: CodexDispatchPhase[]
  supervisorInstructions: string[]
  integrationChecklist: string[]
}

export interface CodexSwarmPipelineInput {
  taskGraph: TaskGraph
}

function codexAgentTypeFor(task: TaskCard): CodexAgentType {
  if (task.agentDomain === "implementer") {
    return "worker"
  }
  if (task.agentDomain === "planner" || task.agentDomain === "verifier") {
    return "explorer"
  }
  return "default"
}

function shouldDelegate(task: TaskCard): boolean {
  return task.agentDomain !== "aggregator"
}

function spawnPromptFor(taskGraph: TaskGraph, task: TaskCard): string {
  return [
    `You are a Codex ${codexAgentTypeFor(task)} sub-agent for XLOTYL taskCard ${task.id}.`,
    "You are not alone in the codebase; do not revert edits made by others, and adapt to concurrent work.",
    `Workflow: ${taskGraph.workflowId}`,
    `Source prompt: ${taskGraph.sourcePrompt}`,
    `Task title: ${task.title}`,
    `Scope: ${task.scope}`,
    `Dependencies: ${task.dependsOn.length > 0 ? task.dependsOn.join(", ") : "none"}`,
    `Allowed tools: ${task.authority.allowedTools.join(", ")}`,
    `Allowed MCP servers: ${task.authority.allowedMcpServers.join(", ")}`,
    `Expected output: ${task.expectedOutput}`,
    `Acceptance criteria: ${task.acceptanceCriteria.join(" | ")}`,
    "Return a concise handoff with changed files, findings, verification evidence, and any blockers.",
  ].join("\n")
}

function dispatchPhaseFor(taskGraph: TaskGraph, taskIds: string[], index: number): CodexDispatchPhase {
  const tasks = taskIds.flatMap((taskId) => taskGraph.tasks.find((task) => task.id === taskId) ?? [])
  const delegates = tasks.filter(shouldDelegate)
  const executor = delegates.length === tasks.length ? "codex-subagents" : "main-thread"
  return {
    id: `phase-${String(index + 1).padStart(3, "0")}`,
    taskIds,
    parallel: taskIds.length > 1 && executor === "codex-subagents",
    executor,
    description:
      executor === "codex-subagents"
        ? "Dispatch these taskCards through Codex sub-agents after their dependencies are satisfied."
        : "Keep these taskCards in the supervising Codex thread for integration and final synthesis.",
  }
}

export function createCodexSwarmPipeline(input: CodexSwarmPipelineInput): CodexSwarmPipeline {
  const { taskGraph } = input
  const delegatedTaskIds = new Set(taskGraph.tasks.filter(shouldDelegate).map((task) => task.id))
  const spawnQueue = taskGraph.tasks
    .filter((task) => delegatedTaskIds.has(task.id))
    .map((task): CodexSpawnTaskCard => ({
      taskId: task.id,
      title: task.title,
      codexAgentType: codexAgentTypeFor(task),
      dependsOn: task.dependsOn,
      canRunInParallel: taskGraph.coordination.parallelGroups.some(
        (group) => group.length > 1 && group.includes(task.id),
      ),
      ownership: `${task.agentDomain}: ${task.scope}`,
      allowedTools: task.authority.allowedTools,
      allowedMcpServers: task.authority.allowedMcpServers,
      expectedOutput: task.expectedOutput,
      spawnPrompt: spawnPromptFor(taskGraph, task),
    }))
  const mainThreadTasks = taskGraph.tasks.filter((task) => !delegatedTaskIds.has(task.id)).map((task) => task.id)

  return {
    id: `codex-swarm-${taskGraph.id}`,
    pathway: CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY,
    dispatchMode: "codex-subagents",
    status: "ready-for-codex-supervision",
    requiresExplicitUserDelegation: true,
    taskGraphId: taskGraph.id,
    workflowId: taskGraph.workflowId,
    sourcePrompt: taskGraph.sourcePrompt,
    activationPrompt:
      "Use this pipeline only when the user explicitly asked for Codex swarm agents, parallel agents, delegation, or sub-agents.",
    spawnQueue,
    mainThreadTasks,
    dispatchPhases: taskGraph.coordination.parallelGroups.map((taskIds, index) =>
      dispatchPhaseFor(taskGraph, taskIds, index),
    ),
    supervisorInstructions: [
      "Start only phases whose dependencies are satisfied.",
      "Use the listed Codex agent type as a recommendation; keep urgent blocking work in the main thread when needed.",
      `Aggregate ${mainThreadTasks.join(", ") || "the final task"} in the main Codex thread before reporting completion.`,
      "Review every sub-agent handoff before integrating or claiming the workflow is complete.",
    ],
    integrationChecklist: [
      "Every delegated taskCard returned expected output or a blocker.",
      "Verifier evidence is reconciled with implementation results.",
      "Main-thread aggregation preserves the XLOTYL done state.",
      "No task broadened its authority beyond the taskCard.",
    ],
  }
}
```

```ts
export function compoundEngineeringDisplayName(name: string): string {
  return name
    .split(/[-/]/)
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((part) => part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.slice(1))
    .join(" ")
}

export function isCompoundEngineeringWorkflow(name: string): boolean {
  return (compoundEngineeringWorkflowNames as readonly string[]).includes(name)
}

export function isCompoundEngineeringListedOnlySkill(name: string): boolean {
  return compoundEngineeringListedOnlySkillNames.has(name)
}
```

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { defaultSourceRegistry } from "./manifest.js"
import { importPinnedSources } from "./registry.js"

describe("pinned source importer", () => {
  it("imports the full compound engineering surface plus the other initial upstreams", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())

    expect(inventory.capabilities.map((capability) => capability.sourceId)).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining([
        "compound-engineering",
        "superpowers",
        "runlayer-plugins",
        "smolagents",
        "spectacular",
        "private-journal-mcp",
        "smallest-agent",
      ]),
    )
    expect(inventory.orchestrationPlugins.map((plugin) => plugin.id)).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining([
        "compound-engineering:ce-ideate",
        "compound-engineering:ce-brainstorm",
        "compound-engineering:ce-plan",
        "compound-engineering:ce-work",
        "compound-engineering:ce-code-review",
        "compound-engineering:ce-compound",
        "compound-engineering:ce-debug",
        "compound-engineering:ce-optimize",
        "compound-engineering:ce-compound-refresh",
      ]),
    )
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "superpowers:writing-plans")?.kind,
    ).toBe("skill")
    expect(inventory.capabilities.map((capability) => capability.id)).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining([
        "compound-engineering:ce-plan",
        "compound-engineering:ce-code-review",
        "compound-engineering:ce-worktree",
        "compound-engineering:ce-setup",
        "compound-engineering:review/ce-security-reviewer",
      ]),
    )
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "compound-engineering:ce-code-review")
        ?.aliases,
    ).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-review")
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "compound-engineering:ce-work")
        ?.aliases,
    ).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining(["compound-engineering:swarm", "compound-engineering:ce-swarm", "xlotyl:codex-swarm"]),
    )
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "compound-engineering:ce-work")
        ?.description,
    ).toContain("swarm")
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "compound-engineering:ce-code-review")
        ?.targets,
    ).toEqual(["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"])
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.filter((capability) => capability.sourceId === "compound-engineering").length,
    ).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(90)
    expect(inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "smolagents:code-agent")?.kind).toBe(
      "agent",
    )
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities.find((capability) => capability.id === "spectacular:spec-plan-execute")
        ?.kind,
    ).toBe("workflow")
    expect(inventory.orchestrationPlugins.map((plugin) => plugin.id)).toContain(
      "spectacular:spec-plan-execute",
    )
  })

  it("treats smolagents and spectacular as approved tool features instead of warnings", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
    const added = inventory.capabilities.filter((capability) =>
      ["smolagents", "spectacular"].includes(capability.sourceId),
    )

    expect(added.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(added.every((capability) => capability.approval === "approved")).toBe(true)
    expect(added.every((capability) => !capability.permissions?.shell && !capability.permissions?.secrets)).toBe(
      true,
    )
  })

  it("keeps candidate sources quarantined until explicitly approved", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())

    expect(
      inventory.capabilities
        .filter((capability) => capability.sourceId === "private-journal-mcp")
        .every((capability) => capability.approval === "quarantined"),
    ).toBe(true)
    expect(
      inventory.capabilities
        .filter((capability) => capability.sourceId === "smallest-agent")
        .every((capability) => capability.approval === "quarantined"),
    ).toBe(true)
  })

  it("marks shell-backed compound engineering utilities as approved but listed-only", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
    const listedOnlyIds = [
      "compound-engineering:ce-worktree",
      "compound-engineering:ce-setup",
      "compound-engineering:ce-commit",
      "compound-engineering:ce-commit-push-pr",
    ]

    for (const id of listedOnlyIds) {
      const capability = inventory.capabilities.find((candidate) => candidate.id === id)
      expect(capability?.approval).toBe("approved")
      expect(capability?.targetModes.every((mode) => mode.mode === "listedOnly")).toBe(true)
      expect(capability?.executionResponsibility?.owner).toBe("deferred")
    }
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/manifest.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3240 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import {
  classifyCapabilityPermissions,
  defaultSourceRegistry,
  manifestSchema,
  validateManifest,
} from "./manifest.js"

describe("core dev services manifest", () => {
  it("declares the neutral v1 schema and pinned upstream sources", () => {
    const manifest = validateManifest(defaultSourceRegistry())

    expect(manifest.schemaVersion).toBe("xlotyl-core-dev-services/v1")
    expect(manifest.sources.map((source) => source.id)).toEqual([
      "compound-engineering",
      "superpowers",
      "runlayer-plugins",
      "smolagents",
      "spectacular",
      "private-journal-mcp",
      "smallest-agent",
    ])
    expect(manifest.sources.every((source) => /^[a-f0-9]{40}$/.test(source.ref))).toBe(true)
    expect(manifest.sources.find((source) => source.id === "private-journal-mcp")?.approval).toBe(
      "quarantined",
    )
    expect(manifest.sources.find((source) => source.id === "smolagents")).toMatchObject({
      approval: "approved",
      license: "Apache-2.0",
    })
    expect(manifest.sources.find((source) => source.id === "spectacular")).toMatchObject({
      approval: "approved",
      license: "MIT",
    })
  })

  it("rejects unpinned source refs", () => {
    const candidate = defaultSourceRegistry()
    candidate.sources[0] = { ...candidate.sources[0]!, ref: "main" }

    expect(() => manifestSchema.parse(candidate)).toThrow()
  })

  it("classifies shell, secret, and mutating capabilities before approval", () => {
    expect(
      classifyCapabilityPermissions({
        id: "hook-format",
        name: "Format Hook",
        kind: "hook",
        sourceId: "runlayer-plugins",
        approval: "quarantined",
        targets: ["claude"],
        command: "npm run format",
      }),
    ).toMatchObject({ shell: true, mutating: true })

    expect(
      classifyCapabilityPermissions({
        id: "journal-mcp",
        name: "Private Journal MCP",
        kind: "mcpServer",
        sourceId: "private-journal-mcp",
        approval: "quarantined",
        targets: ["codex"],
        tools: ["read_entries", "write_entry"],
        env: { JOURNAL_TOKEN: "${JOURNAL_TOKEN}" },
      }),
    ).toMatchObject({ secrets: true, mutating: true })
  })

  it("supports aliases, target emission modes, and execution responsibility metadata", () => {
    const manifest = validateManifest({
      ...defaultSourceRegistry(),
      capabilities: [
        {
          id: "compound-engineering:ce-code-review",
          name: "CE Code Review",
          kind: "workflow",
          sourceId: "compound-engineering",
          approval: "approved",
          aliases: ["compound-engineering:ce-review"],
          targets: ["codex"],
          targetModes: [{ target: "codex", mode: "callable" }],
          executionResponsibility: {
            owner: "xlotyl",
            notes: "Compiled into governed taskCards.",
          },
        },
      ],
    })

    expect(manifest.capabilities[0]?.aliases).toEqual(["compound-engineering:ce-review"])
    expect(manifest.capabilities[0]?.targetModes).toEqual([{ target: "codex", mode: "callable" }])
    expect(manifest.capabilities[0]?.executionResponsibility?.owner).toBe("xlotyl")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/manifest.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 8545 bytes

```ts
import { z } from "zod"

export const targetSchema = z.enum(["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"])
export const approvalSchema = z.enum(["quarantined", "approved", "disabled"])
export const targetEmissionModeSchema = z.enum(["callable", "listedOnly"])
export const capabilityKindSchema = z.enum([
  "skill",
  "agent",
  "workflow",
  "rule",
  "command",
  "mcpServer",
  "hook",
])

export const permissionsSchema = z.object({
  read: z.boolean().default(false),
  write: z.boolean().default(false),
  network: z.boolean().default(false),
  shell: z.boolean().default(false),
  secrets: z.boolean().default(false),
  mutating: z.boolean().default(false),
})

export const targetModeSchema = z.object({
  target: targetSchema,
  mode: targetEmissionModeSchema,
})

export const executionResponsibilitySchema = z.object({
  owner: z.enum(["xlotyl", "deferred"]).default("xlotyl"),
  notes: z.string().optional(),
})

export const sourceSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().min(1),
  name: z.string().min(1),
  repo: z.string().url(),
  ref: z.string().regex(/^[a-f0-9]{40}$/),
  license: z.string().min(1),
  importPath: z.string().min(1),
  approval: approvalSchema.default("quarantined"),
  enabledComponents: z.array(capabilityKindSchema).default([]),
})

export const capabilitySchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().min(1),
  name: z.string().min(1),
  kind: capabilityKindSchema,
  sourceId: z.string().min(1),
  approval: approvalSchema.default("quarantined"),
  aliases: z.array(z.string().min(1)).default([]),
  targets: z.array(targetSchema).default([]),
  targetModes: z.array(targetModeSchema).default([]),
  description: z.string().optional(),
  content: z.string().optional(),
  command: z.string().optional(),
  tools: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
  env: z.record(z.string()).optional(),
  permissions: permissionsSchema.optional(),
  executionResponsibility: executionResponsibilitySchema.optional(),
})

export const orchestrationAgentSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().min(1),
  domain: z.string().min(1),
  scope: z.string().min(1),
  allowedTools: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
  allowedMcpServers: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
  expectedOutput: z.string().min(1),
})

export const orchestrationPluginSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().min(1),
  name: z.string().min(1),
  sourceId: z.string().min(1),
  approval: approvalSchema.default("quarantined"),
  aliases: z.array(z.string().min(1)).default([]),
  workflowIntent: z.string().min(1),
  promptTemplate: z.string().min(1),
  agents: z.array(orchestrationAgentSchema).min(1),
  breakoutRules: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
  reviewExpectations: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
  contextPreferences: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
  metricPolicy: z.object({
    successCriteria: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
    risk: z.enum(["low", "medium", "high"]).default("medium"),
    confidence: z.number().min(0).max(1).default(0.7),
    evidence: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
    doneState: z.string().min(1),
  }),
})

export const manifestSchema = z.object({
  schemaVersion: z.literal("xlotyl-core-dev-services/v1"),
  sources: z.array(sourceSchema).min(1),
  capabilities: z.array(capabilitySchema).default([]),
  orchestrationPlugins: z.array(orchestrationPluginSchema).default([]),
})

export type Target = z.infer<typeof targetSchema>
export type Approval = z.infer<typeof approvalSchema>
export type TargetEmissionMode = z.infer<typeof targetEmissionModeSchema>
export type Permissions = z.infer<typeof permissionsSchema>
export type TargetMode = z.infer<typeof targetModeSchema>
export type ExecutionResponsibility = z.infer<typeof executionResponsibilitySchema>
export type SourceDefinition = z.infer<typeof sourceSchema>
export type Capability = z.infer<typeof capabilitySchema>
export type CapabilityInput = z.input<typeof capabilitySchema>
export type OrchestrationPlugin = z.infer<typeof orchestrationPluginSchema>
export type CoreDevServicesManifest = z.infer<typeof manifestSchema>

export const allTargets: Target[] = ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"]

export function defaultSourceRegistry(): CoreDevServicesManifest {
  return {
    schemaVersion: "xlotyl-core-dev-services/v1",
    sources: [
      {
        id: "compound-engineering",

        importPath: ".",
        approval: "approved",
        enabledComponents: ["skill", "agent", "workflow"],

        repo: "https://github.com/arittr/spectacular",
        ref: "0e495f8fd05d9bffc682589dfa86c6390799fb90",
        license: "MIT",
        importPath: ".",
        approval: "approved",
        enabledComponents: ["skill", "workflow", "command"],
      },
      {
        id: "private-journal-mcp",
        name: "Private Journal MCP",
        repo: "https://github.com/obra/private-journal-mcp",
        ref: "65b182875389288782063ac058248d70e71640a8",
        license: "MIT",
        importPath: ".",
        approval: "quarantined",
        enabledComponents: ["mcpServer"],
      },
      {
        id: "smallest-agent",
        name: "Smallest Agent",
        repo: "https://github.com/obra/smallest-agent",
        ref: "d42ba035040c64aa59ba235d8cf8da8cf0129944",
        license: "MIT",
        importPath: ".",
        approval: "quarantined",
        enabledComponents: ["agent", "workflow"],
      },
    ],
    capabilities: [],
    orchestrationPlugins: [],
  }
}

export function validateManifest(manifest: unknown): CoreDevServicesManifest {
  const parsed = manifestSchema.parse(manifest)
  return {
    ...parsed,
    capabilities: parsed.capabilities.map((capability) => ({
      ...capability,
      permissions: capability.permissions ?? classifyCapabilityPermissions(capability),
    })),
  }
}

export function targetModesFor(targets: Target[], mode: TargetEmissionMode): TargetMode[] {
  return targets.map((target) => ({ target, mode }))
}

export function capabilityEmissionMode(
  capability: Pick<Capability, "targets" | "targetModes">,
  target: Target,
): TargetEmissionMode | undefined {
  if (!capability.targets.includes(target)) {
    return undefined
  }
  return capability.targetModes.find((candidate) => candidate.target === target)?.mode ?? "callable"
}

export function isCapabilityCallableForTarget(
  capability: Pick<Capability, "approval" | "targets" | "targetModes">,
  target: Target,
): boolean {
  return capability.approval === "approved" && capabilityEmissionMode(capability, target) === "callable"
}

export function classifyCapabilityPermissions(
  capability: Partial<Capability> & Pick<Capability, "kind">,
): Permissions {
  const text = [
    capability.kind,
    capability.command ?? "",
    ...(capability.tools ?? []),
    ...Object.keys(capability.env ?? {}),
    ...Object.values(capability.env ?? {}),
  ]
    .join(" ")
    .toLowerCase()

  const shell = capability.kind === "hook" || Boolean(capability.command)
  const secrets = /(token|secret|password|api[_-]?key|authorization)/i.test(text)
  const mutating =
    capability.kind === "hook" ||
    /(write|create|update|delete|set_|mutat|format|apply|push|deploy|run)/i.test(text)
  const network = capability.kind === "mcpServer"

  return {
    read: true,
    write: mutating,
    network,
    shell,
    secrets,
    mutating,
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/mcp.test.ts`
