```ts
import { mkdtemp, readFile, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { createMcpToolRegistry, handleMcpRequest } from "./mcp.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot } from "./paths.js"

describe("xlotyl-dev-services MCP tools", () => {
  it("lists the expected tool surface and calls representative tools", async () => {
    const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()

    expect(registry.listTools().map((tool) => tool.name)).toEqual([
      "xlotyl_capability_search",
      "xlotyl_capability_get",
      "xlotyl_adapter_status",
      "xlotyl_sync_plan",
      "xlotyl_sync_apply",
      "xlotyl_orchestrate",
      "xlotyl_workflow_orchestrate",
      "xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan",
      "xlotyl_workflow_codex_swarm_plan",
      "xlotyl_agent_run",
      "xlotyl_agent_status",
      "xlotyl_agent_result",
      "xlotyl_agent_complete",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_validate",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_import",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_approve",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_activate",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_mark_terminal",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_sync",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_evaluate",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_replan",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_replay",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_decide",
      "xlotyl_stoneforge_aggregate",
    ])

    const search = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_capability_search", { query: "superpowers" })
    expect(search.content[0]?.text).toContain("superpowers:writing-plans")

    const swarmSearch = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_capability_search", { query: "swarm" })
    expect(swarmSearch.content[0]?.text).toContain("xlotyl:codex-swarm")

    const orchestration = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_orchestrate", {
      workflowId: "xlotyl:swarm",
      prompt: "Break this work into taskCards.",
    })
    expect(orchestration.content[0]?.text).toContain("task-001")
    expect(orchestration.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"workflowId\": \"compound-engineering:ce-work\"")

    const swarmPlan = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan", {
      workflowId: "xlotyl:swarm",
      prompt: "Audit this app for agent-native architecture.",
    })
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"workflowId\": \"compound-engineering:ce-work\"")
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"label\": \"Working for Codex\"")
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"role\": \"adapter-pathway\"")
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"isDefaultPathway\": false")
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"dispatchMode\": \"codex-subagents\"")
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"requiresExplicitUserDelegation\": true")
    expect(swarmPlan.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"codexAgentType\": \"worker\"")

    const promotedRun = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_agent_run", {
      runtime: "codex-swarm",
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
      prompt: "Break this work into Codex swarm taskCards.",
    })
    // No implicit promotion: codex-swarm is treated as a queued run unless the caller
    // explicitly invokes a promotion tool (e.g. xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan).
    expect(promotedRun.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"status\": \"queued\"")
    expect(promotedRun.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"runtime\": \"codex-swarm\"")

    const queuedRun = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_agent_run", {
      taskId: "task-002",
      task: { id: "task-002", expectedOutput: "Implementation handoff." },
    })
    const queued = JSON.parse(queuedRun.content[0]?.text ?? "{}") as { runId: string }
    expect(queued.runId).toMatch(/^run-\d+-task-002$/)

    const queuedStatus = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_agent_status", { runId: queued.runId })
    expect(queuedStatus.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"status\": \"queued\"")

    const completedRun = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_agent_complete", {
      runId: queued.runId,
      result: { summary: "Implemented bounded taskCard." },
      artifacts: [{ type: "handoff", path: "reports/task-002.md" }],
    })
    expect(completedRun.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"status\": \"completed\"")

    const runResult = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_agent_result", { runId: queued.runId })
    expect(runResult.content[0]?.text).toContain("Implemented bounded taskCard.")

    const aliasedCapability = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_capability_get", {
      id: "compound-engineering:ce-review",
    })
    expect(aliasedCapability.content[0]?.text).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-code-review")

    const swarmCapability = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_capability_get", {
      id: "xlotyl:codex-swarm",
    })
    expect(swarmCapability.content[0]?.text).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-work")

    const stoneforgeGraph = {
      run_id: "run-mcp-stoneforge",
      workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
      workflow_title: "MCP stoneforge",
      source_goal: "g",
      planning_owner: "xlotyl",
      runtime_target: "stoneforge",
      dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
      phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
      tasks: [
        {
          id: "T1",
          phase_id: "P1",
          title: "one",
          task_card_type: "t",
          priority: 1,
          dependencies: [],
          acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
        },
      ],
    }
    const stoneforgeValidate = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_validate", { graph: stoneforgeGraph })
    expect(stoneforgeValidate.content[0]?.text).toContain('"ok": true')

    const listedOnlyCapability = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_capability_get", {
      id: "compound-engineering:ce-worktree",
    })
    expect(listedOnlyCapability.content[0]?.text).toContain("listedOnly")

    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xlotyl-mcp-"))
    try {
      const syncPlan = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_sync_plan", { repoRoot: root })
      const plan = JSON.parse(syncPlan.content[0]?.text ?? "{}") as Record<string, unknown>
      const syncApply = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_sync_apply", { plan })
      expect(syncApply.content[0]?.text).toContain("\"writes\"")
      expect(syncApply.content[0]?.text).toContain(".cursor/mcp.json")
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("defaults sync planning to the core-dev-services root", async () => {
    const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()
    const syncPlan = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_sync_plan")
    const parsed = JSON.parse(syncPlan.content[0]?.text ?? "{}") as {
      operations: Array<{ destination: string }>
    }

    expect(parsed.operations.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(parsed.operations.every((operation) => operation.destination.startsWith(defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()))).toBe(
      true,
    )
  })

  it("calls xlotyl_stoneforge_replay after import", async () => {
    const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xlotyl-mcp-replay-"))
    try {
      const graph = {
        run_id: "run-mcp-replay",
        workflow_id: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
        workflow_title: "replay",
        source_goal: "g",
        planning_owner: "xlotyl",
        runtime_target: "stoneforge",
        dispatch_policy: { requires_human_approval_before_activation: false },
        phases: [{ id: "P1", name: "p" }],
        tasks: [
          {
            id: "T1",
            phase_id: "P1",
            title: "one",
            task_card_type: "t",
            priority: 1,
            dependencies: [],
            acceptance_criteria: ["a"],
          },
        ],
      }
      await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_import", { graph, workspaceRoot: root })
      await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_sync", {
        runId: "run-mcp-replay",
        workspaceRoot: root,
        event: { task_card_id: "T1", status: "synced" },
      })
      const replay = await registry.callTool("xlotyl_stoneforge_replay", { runId: "run-mcp-replay", workspaceRoot: root })
      const replayParsed = JSON.parse(replay.content[0]?.text ?? "{}") as { draftPlan: string }
      const draftBody = await readFile(replayParsed.draftPlan, "utf8")
      expect(draftBody).toContain("draft-plan-run-mcp-replay-replay")
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })

  it("answers MCP JSON-RPC initialize, tools/list, and tools/call requests", async () => {
    const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()

    await expect(
      handleMcpRequest(registry, { method: "notifications/initialized" }),
    ).resolves.toBeNull()

    await expect(
      handleMcpRequest(registry, {
        jsonrpc: "2.0",
        id: 1,
        method: "initialize",
        params: { protocolVersion: "2024-11-05" },
      }),
    ).resolves.toMatchObject({
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 1,
      result: {
        capabilities: { tools: {} },
        serverInfo: { name: "xlotyl-dev-services" },
      },
    })

    const toolsList = await handleMcpRequest(registry, { jsonrpc: "2.0", id: 2, method: "tools/list" })
    expect(JSON.stringify(toolsList)).toContain("xlotyl_orchestrate")

    const toolCall = await handleMcpRequest(registry, {
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 3,
      method: "tools/call",
      params: { name: "xlotyl_capability_search", arguments: { query: "agent-native" } },
    })
    expect(JSON.stringify(toolCall)).toContain("ce-agent-native-audit")

    const orchestrationCall = await handleMcpRequest(registry, {
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 4,
      method: "tools/call",
      params: {
        name: "xlotyl_orchestrate",
        arguments: {
          workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
          prompt: "Audit this app for agent-native architecture.",
        },
      },
    })
    expect(JSON.stringify(orchestrationCall)).toContain("compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit")

    const swarmCall = await handleMcpRequest(registry, {
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 5,
      method: "tools/call",
      params: {
        name: "xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan",
        arguments: {
          workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
          prompt: "Audit this app for agent-native architecture.",
        },
      },
    })
    expect(JSON.stringify(swarmCall)).toContain("codex-subagents")
  })

  it("returns JSON-RPC tool errors without poisoning later calls", async () => {
    const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()

    const failingCall = await handleMcpRequest(registry, {
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 10,
      method: "tools/call",
      params: {
        name: "xlotyl_orchestrate",
        arguments: { workflowId: "compound-engineering:not-real", prompt: "Try a bad workflow." },
      },
    })

    expect(failingCall).toMatchObject({
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 10,
      error: {
        code: -32000,
      },
    })
    expect(JSON.stringify(failingCall)).toContain("Unknown orchestration workflow")

    const healthyCall = await handleMcpRequest(registry, {
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: 11,
      method: "tools/call",
      params: { name: "xlotyl_adapter_status", arguments: {} },
    })
    const healthyResult = healthyCall as { result?: { content?: Array<{ text?: string }> } }

    expect(healthyResult.result?.content?.[0]?.text).toContain('"status": "ready"')
    expect(healthyResult.result?.content?.[0]?.text).toContain('"label": "Working for Codex"')
  })
})

### `services/core-dev-services/src/mcp.ts`

```ts
import { createInterface } from "node:readline/promises"
import { stdin as input, stdout as output } from "node:process"
import { createAgentRunStore, type AgentRunArtifact } from "./agent-runtime.js"
import { generateAdapters } from "./adapters.js"
import { CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY, createCodexSwarmPipeline } from "./codex-swarm.js"
import { defaultSourceRegistry } from "./manifest.js"
import { orchestratePrompt, type TaskGraph } from "./orchestrator.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot } from "./paths.js"
import { importPinnedSources, resolveCapability } from "./registry.js"
import { createSyncPlan, writeSyncPlan, type SyncPlan } from "./sync.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./stoneforge/contract.js"
import { parseEvaluationPayload } from "./stoneforge/evaluation.js"
import {
  activateRun,
  appendEvaluationEvent,
  appendSyncEvent,
  validateAndImportRun,
  writeApproval,
} from "./stoneforge/import-run.js"
import { aggregateRun } from "./stoneforge/aggregate-run.js"
import { resolveStoneforgeBindingFromMcpArgs } from "./stoneforge/binding.js"
import { replayRun } from "./stoneforge/replay-run.js"
import { runReplanMergeAndImport } from "./stoneforge/replan-pipeline.js"
import { runDecisionCycle } from "./stoneforge/decision/index.js"
import { markTerminal } from "./stoneforge/mark-terminal.js"

export interface McpTool {
  name: string
  description: string
  inputSchema: Record<string, unknown>
}

export interface McpToolResult {
  content: Array<{ type: "text"; text: string }>
}

interface McpRequest {
  jsonrpc?: string
  id?: unknown
  method?: string
  params?: Record<string, unknown>
}

function errorMessage(error: unknown): string {
  return error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
}

function jsonRpcError(id: unknown, code: number, message: string): Record<string, unknown> {
  return {
    jsonrpc: "2.0",
    id,
    error: {
      code,
      message,
    },
  }
}

function textResult(value: unknown): McpToolResult {
  return {
    content: [{ type: "text", text: typeof value === "string" ? value : JSON.stringify(value, null, 2) }],
  }
}

function taskGraphFromArgs(inventory: ReturnType<typeof importPinnedSources>, args: Record<string, unknown>): TaskGraph {
  if (args.taskGraph && typeof args.taskGraph === "object" && !Array.isArray(args.taskGraph)) {
    return args.taskGraph as TaskGraph
  }
  return orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
    workflowId: String(args.workflowId ?? "compound-engineering:ce-work"),
    prompt: String(args.prompt ?? ""),
    context:
      args.context && typeof args.context === "object" && !Array.isArray(args.context)
        ? args.context as Record<string, unknown>
        : undefined,
  })
}

function optionalString(value: unknown): string | undefined {
  return typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0 ? value : undefined
}

function optionalRecord(value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> | undefined {
  return value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value) ? value as Record<string, unknown> : undefined
}

function artifactsFrom(value: unknown): AgentRunArtifact[] | undefined {
  return Array.isArray(value)
    ? value.flatMap((item): AgentRunArtifact[] => {
        const record = optionalRecord(item)
        return record ? [record as AgentRunArtifact] : []
      })
    : undefined
}

export function createMcpToolRegistry() {
  const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
  const agentRuns = createAgentRunStore()
  const tools: McpTool[] = [
    {
      name: "xlotyl_capability_search",
      description: "Search imported XLOTYL dev-service capabilities.",
      inputSchema: { type: "object", properties: { query: { type: "string" } } },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_capability_get",
      description: "Get one imported XLOTYL dev-service capability by id.",
      inputSchema: { type: "object", properties: { id: { type: "string" } }, required: ["id"] },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_adapter_status",
      description: "Report adapter generation status for supported front ends.",
      inputSchema: { type: "object", properties: {} },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_sync_plan",
      description: "Plan adapter sync operations without writing files.",
      inputSchema: { type: "object", properties: { repoRoot: { type: "string" } } },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_sync_apply",
      description:
        "Write an approved adapter sync plan to disk (no implicit replanning). Requires `plan` from xlotyl_sync_plan.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { plan: { type: "object" } },
        required: ["plan"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_orchestrate",
      description: "Compile a prompt and orchestration plugin workflow into a governed task graph.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { workflowId: { type: "string" }, prompt: { type: "string" } },
        required: ["workflowId", "prompt"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_workflow_orchestrate",
      description:
        "Workflow: compile a prompt and orchestration plugin workflow into a governed task graph. (Alias of xlotyl_orchestrate; explicit workflow namespace.)",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { workflowId: { type: "string" }, prompt: { type: "string" } },
        required: ["workflowId", "prompt"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan",
      description:
        "Promote a governed XLOTYL task graph into the Working for Codex adapter pathway for Codex sub-agent dispatch. This is not the canonical cross-platform pathway.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",

    {
      name: "xlotyl_workflow_codex_swarm_plan",

        "Workflow: promote a governed XLOTYL task graph into the Working for Codex adapter pathway for Codex sub-agent dispatch. (Alias of xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan; explicit workflow namespace.)",
      inputSchema: {

      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: {
          taskId: { type: "string" },
          task: { type: "object" },
          workflowId: { type: "string" },
          prompt: { type: "string" },

      },

    {
      name: "xlotyl_agent_status",
      description: "Inspect queued or completed XLOTYL agent taskCard run status.",

      },
    },

      name: "xlotyl_agent_result",

      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",

        required: ["runId"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_agent_complete",
      description: "Attach a supervised execution result to a queued XLOTYL agent taskCard run.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: {
          runId: { type: "string" },
          result: {},
          artifacts: { type: "array", items: { type: "object" } },
          error: { type: "string" },
          status: { type: "string" },
        },
        required: ["runId"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_validate",

      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_mark_terminal",
      description: "Mark one or all taskCards terminal by updating the imported graph.json for a run.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: {
          runId: { type: "string" },
          workspaceRoot: { type: "string" },
          taskId: { type: "string" },
          all: { type: "boolean" },
          markedBy: { type: "string" },
          reason: { type: "string" },
          evidenceRefs: { type: "array", items: { type: "string" } },
        },
        required: ["runId"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_sync",
      description: "Append a normalized sync event to dispatch-log.jsonl for a run.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { runId: { type: "string" }, workspaceRoot: { type: "string" }, event: { type: "object" } },
        required: ["runId", "event"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_evaluate",
      description: "Append a steward evaluation record to dispatch-log.jsonl for a run.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { runId: { type: "string" }, workspaceRoot: { type: "string" }, evaluation: { type: "object" } },
        required: ["runId", "evaluation"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_replan",
      description:
        "Merge a replan delta graph into an existing imported run and re-import artifacts. Honors dispatch_policy.max_replan_cycles and optional idempotencyKey.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: {
          runId: { type: "string" },
          workspaceRoot: { type: "string" },
          deltaGraph: { type: "object" },
          idempotencyKey: { type: "string" },
          binding: { type: "string", enum: ["local-artifact", "sf-cli"] },
          sfBinPath: { type: "string" },
        },
        required: ["runId", "deltaGraph"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_replay",
      description: "Regenerate draft-plan.json, stoneforge-map.json, final-report.md, and dataset.jsonl from graph + log.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { runId: { type: "string" }, workspaceRoot: { type: "string" } },
        required: ["runId"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_decide",
      description:
        "Observe a Stoneforge run through sf-cli, make XLOTYL decision-module routing/recovery decisions, execute supported actions, and write decision artifacts.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: {
          runId: { type: "string" },
          workspaceRoot: { type: "string" },
          binding: { type: "string", enum: ["sf-cli", "local-artifact"] },
          sfBinPath: { type: "string" },
        },
        required: ["runId"],
      },
    },
    {
      name: "xlotyl_stoneforge_aggregate",
      description: "Write final-report.md and dataset.jsonl for a run from graph + dispatch log.",
      inputSchema: {
        type: "object",
        properties: { runId: { type: "string" }, workspaceRoot: { type: "string" } },
        required: ["runId"],
      },
    },
  ]

  return {
    listTools: () => tools,
    callTool: async (name: string, args: Record<string, unknown> = {}): Promise<McpToolResult> => {
      if (name === "xlotyl_capability_search") {
        const query = String(args.query ?? "").toLowerCase()
        return textResult(
          inventory.capabilities.filter((capability) =>
            [
              capability.id,
              capability.name,
              capability.description ?? "",
              capability.sourceId,
              ...capability.aliases,
              ...capability.targetModes.map((mode) => mode.mode),
              capability.executionResponsibility?.owner ?? "",
            ]
              .join(" ")
              .toLowerCase()
              .includes(query),
          ),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_capability_get") {
        return textResult(resolveCapability(inventory, String(args.id ?? "")) ?? null)
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_adapter_status") {
        return textResult({
          targets: ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"],
          status: "ready",
          sourceOfTruth: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
          defaultPathwayPolicy:
            "Core Dev Services is canonical. Platform pathways are labeled adapter bridges and must not become the default cross-platform route by accident.",
          adapterPathways: [CODEX_SWARM_PATHWAY],
        })
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_sync_plan") {
        const repoRoot = String(args.repoRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        return textResult(
          createSyncPlan(
            generateAdapters(inventory, { targets: ["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"] }),
            { repoRoot },
          ),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_sync_apply") {
        const plan = optionalRecord(args.plan)
        if (!plan) {
          return textResult({
            status: "rejected",
            error_code: "missing_plan",
            message: "xlotyl_sync_apply requires an explicit `plan` (from xlotyl_sync_plan).",
          })
        }
        return textResult(await writeSyncPlan(plan as unknown as SyncPlan))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_orchestrate") {
        return textResult(
          taskGraphFromArgs(inventory, args),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_workflow_orchestrate") {
        return textResult(
          taskGraphFromArgs(inventory, args),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_codex_swarm_plan") {
        return textResult(createCodexSwarmPipeline({ taskGraph: taskGraphFromArgs(inventory, args) }))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_workflow_codex_swarm_plan") {
        return textResult(createCodexSwarmPipeline({ taskGraph: taskGraphFromArgs(inventory, args) }))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_agent_run") {
        return textResult(
          agentRuns.queueRun({
            taskId: optionalString(args.taskId),
            runtime: optionalString(args.runtime),
            task: optionalRecord(args.task),
          }),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_agent_status") {
        return textResult(agentRuns.status({ runId: optionalString(args.runId), taskId: optionalString(args.taskId) }))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_agent_result") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_agent_result requires runId")
        }
        return textResult(agentRuns.result({ runId }))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_agent_complete") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_agent_complete requires runId")
        }
        return textResult(
          agentRuns.completeRun({
            runId,
            result: args.result,
            artifacts: artifactsFrom(args.artifacts),
            error: optionalString(args.error),
            status: args.status === "failed" ? "failed" : "completed",
          }),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_validate") {
        const graph = optionalRecord(args.graph)
        if (!graph) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_validate requires graph")
        }
        return textResult(validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(graph))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_import") {
        const graph = optionalRecord(args.graph)
        if (!graph) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_import requires graph")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        const binding = resolveStoneforgeBindingFromMcpArgs(args)
        const result = args.dryRun === true
          ? await validateAndImportRun(graph, workspaceRoot, { binding, dryRun: true })
          : await validateAndImportRun(graph, workspaceRoot, { binding })
        return textResult(result)
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_approve") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_approve requires runId")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        await writeApproval(workspaceRoot, runId, {
          approved: true,
          approved_by: optionalString(args.approvedBy) ?? "operator",
        })
        return textResult({ ok: true, runId })
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_activate") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_activate requires runId")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        const binding = resolveStoneforgeBindingFromMcpArgs(args)
        return textResult(
          await activateRun(workspaceRoot, runId, {
            force: Boolean(args.force),
            approvedBy: optionalString(args.approvedBy),
            binding,
          }),
        )
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_sync") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        const event = optionalRecord(args.event)
        if (!runId || !event) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_sync requires runId and event")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        await appendSyncEvent(workspaceRoot, runId, {
          task_card_id: String(event.task_card_id ?? ""),
          status: String(event.status ?? "unknown"),
          message: typeof event.message === "string" ? event.message : undefined,
          metrics: event.metrics as Record<string, number> | undefined,
          artifacts: Array.isArray(event.artifacts) ? (event.artifacts as string[]) : undefined,
        })
        return textResult({ ok: true })
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_mark_terminal") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_mark_terminal requires runId")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        const taskId = optionalString(args.taskId)
        const all = args.all === true
        const markedBy = optionalString(args.markedBy)
        const reason = optionalString(args.reason)
        const evidenceRefs = Array.isArray(args.evidenceRefs)
          ? (args.evidenceRefs as unknown[]).map((v) => String(v))
          : undefined
        return textResult(await markTerminal(workspaceRoot, runId, { taskId, all, markedBy, reason, evidenceRefs }))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_evaluate") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        const evaluation = args.evaluation
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_evaluate requires runId")
        }
        const parsed = parseEvaluationPayload(evaluation)
        if (!parsed.ok) {
          return textResult({ ok: false, errors: parsed.errors })
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        await appendEvaluationEvent(workspaceRoot, runId, parsed.value)
        return textResult({ ok: true })
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_replan") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        const deltaGraph = optionalRecord(args.deltaGraph)
        if (!runId || !deltaGraph) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_replan requires runId and deltaGraph")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        const binding = resolveStoneforgeBindingFromMcpArgs(args)
        const idempotencyKey = optionalString(args.idempotencyKey)
        const result = await runReplanMergeAndImport(workspaceRoot, runId, deltaGraph, {
          binding,
          idempotencyKey,
        })
        if (result.ok) {
          if (result.deduped) {
            return textResult({ ok: true, deduped: true, replan_cycles_completed: result.replan_cycles_completed })
          }
          return textResult({ ok: true, import: result.import, replan_cycles_completed: result.replan_cycles_completed })
        }
        return textResult({ ok: false, errors: result.errors })
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_replay") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_replay requires runId")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        return textResult(await replayRun(workspaceRoot, runId))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_decide") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_decide requires runId")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        const binding = resolveStoneforgeBindingFromMcpArgs(args)
        return textResult(await runDecisionCycle({ workspaceRoot, runId, binding }))
      }
      if (name === "xlotyl_stoneforge_aggregate") {
        const runId = optionalString(args.runId)
        if (!runId) {
          throw new Error("xlotyl_stoneforge_aggregate requires runId")
        }
        const workspaceRoot = String(args.workspaceRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot())
        return textResult(await aggregateRun(workspaceRoot, runId))
      }
      throw new Error(`Unknown MCP tool: ${name}`)
    },
  }
}

export async function handleMcpRequest(
  registry: ReturnType<typeof createMcpToolRegistry>,
  request: McpRequest,
): Promise<Record<string, unknown> | null> {
  if (!request.id && (request.method === "notifications/initialized" || request.method === "initialized")) {
    return null
  }

  if (request.method === "initialize") {
    return {
      jsonrpc: "2.0",
      id: request.id,
      result: {
        protocolVersion: String(request.params?.protocolVersion ?? "2024-11-05"),
        capabilities: {
          tools: {},
          resources: {},
        },
        serverInfo: {
          name: "xlotyl-dev-services",
          version: "0.1.0",
        },
      },
    }
  }

  if (request.method === "tools/list") {
    return { jsonrpc: "2.0", id: request.id, result: { tools: registry.listTools() } }
  }

  if (request.method === "tools/call") {
    const params = request.params ?? {}
    try {
      const result = await registry.callTool(String(params.name), params.arguments as Record<string, unknown>)
      return { jsonrpc: "2.0", id: request.id, result }
    } catch (error) {
      return jsonRpcError(request.id, -32000, errorMessage(error))
    }
  }

  if (request.method === "resources/list") {
    return { jsonrpc: "2.0", id: request.id, result: { resources: [] } }
  }

  if (request.method === "resources/templates/list") {
    return { jsonrpc: "2.0", id: request.id, result: { resourceTemplates: [] } }
  }

  if (request.method === "ping") {
    return { jsonrpc: "2.0", id: request.id, result: {} }
  }

  return jsonRpcError(request.id, -32601, `Unknown MCP method: ${request.method ?? "unknown"}`)
}

export async function runMcpStdio() {
  const registry = createMcpToolRegistry()
  const rl = createInterface({ input, output })
  for await (const line of rl) {
    if (!line.trim()) {
      continue
    }
    try {
      const request = JSON.parse(line) as McpRequest
      const response = await handleMcpRequest(registry, request)
      if (response) {
        output.write(`${JSON.stringify(response)}\n`)
      }
    } catch (error) {
      output.write(`${JSON.stringify(jsonRpcError(null, -32700, errorMessage(error)))}\n`)
    }
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/orchestrator.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5047 bytes

```ts
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { defaultSourceRegistry } from "./manifest.js"
import { orchestratePrompt } from "./orchestrator.js"
import { importPinnedSources } from "./registry.js"

describe("swarm orchestration", () => {
  it("compiles plugin workflow policy and a user prompt into a governed task graph", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
    const graph = orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
      prompt: "Port shared skills and MCP tools into all IDE fronts.",
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
      context: { repo: "xlotyl" },
    })

    expect(graph.workflowId).toBe("compound-engineering:ce-work")
    expect(graph.tasks).toHaveLength(4)
    expect(graph.tasks[0]).toMatchObject({
      id: "task-001",
      agentDomain: "planner",
      status: "ready",
      dependsOn: [],
    })
    expect(graph.tasks[1]?.dependsOn).toEqual(["task-001"])
    expect(graph.tasks.every((task) => task.authority.allowedTools.length > 0)).toBe(true)
    expect(graph.metrics.doneState).toContain("All taskCards satisfy")
    expect(graph.coordination.parallelGroups).toEqual([["task-001"], ["task-002", "task-003"], ["task-004"]])
  })

  it("scopes each swarm agent taskCard to its declared domain instead of passing the full workflow", () => {
    const graph = orchestratePrompt(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      prompt: "Review and implement adapter generation.",
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    })

    const implementerTaskCard = graph.tasks.find((task) => task.agentDomain === "implementer")
    expect(implementerTaskCard?.prompt).toContain("Review and implement adapter generation.")
    expect(implementerTaskCard?.scope).toContain("implementation")
    expect(implementerTaskCard?.scope).not.toContain("final aggregation")
  })

  it("supports compound engineering planning as a callable orchestration workflow", () => {
    const graph = orchestratePrompt(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry()), {
      prompt: "Plan the Codex adapter rollout.",
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-plan",
      context: { repo: "xlotyl" },
    })

    expect(graph.workflowId).toBe("compound-engineering:ce-plan")
    expect(graph.tasks).toHaveLength(4)
    expect(graph.tasks[0]?.title).toContain("planning")
    expect(graph.tasks[0]?.expectedOutput).toContain("Implementation plan")
    expect(graph.coordination.parallelGroups).toEqual([["task-001"], ["task-002", "task-003"], ["task-004"]])
  })

  it("supports every callable compound engineering workflow and normalizes aliases", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())

    for (const workflowId of [
      "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-architecture",
      "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
      "compound-engineering:ce-ideate",
      "compound-engineering:ce-brainstorm",
      "compound-engineering:ce-plan",
      "compound-engineering:ce-work",
      "compound-engineering:ce-code-review",
      "compound-engineering:ce-compound",
      "compound-engineering:ce-debug",
      "compound-engineering:ce-optimize",
      "compound-engineering:ce-compound-refresh",
    ]) {
      const graph = orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
        prompt: "Wire the Compound Engineering adapters.",
        workflowId,
      })
      expect(graph.workflowId).toBe(workflowId)
      expect(graph.tasks).toHaveLength(4)
      expect(graph.tasks.every((task) => task.acceptanceCriteria.length > 0)).toBe(true)
    }

    const aliased = orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
      prompt: "Review the adapter changes.",
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-review",
    })

    expect(aliased.workflowId).toBe("compound-engineering:ce-code-review")

    for (const workflowId of [
      "compound-engineering:swarm",
      "compound-engineering:ce-swarm",
      "xlotyl:codex-swarm",
      "xlotyl:swarm",
    ]) {
      const swarm = orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
        prompt: "Run this through the supervised swarm lifecycle.",
        workflowId,
      })
      expect(swarm.workflowId).toBe("compound-engineering:ce-work")
      expect(swarm.tasks).toHaveLength(4)
    }
  })

  it("registers agent-native CE audit as a governed orchestration workflow", () => {
    const inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
    const workflowIds = inventory.orchestrationPlugins.map((plugin) => plugin.id)

    expect(workflowIds).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining([
        "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-architecture",
        "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
      ]),
    )

    const graph = orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
      prompt: "Audit this app for agent-native architecture.",
      workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
    })

    expect(graph.workflowId).toBe("compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit")
    expect(graph.tasks).toHaveLength(4)
    expect(graph.metrics.successCriteria).toContain("The canonical CE workflow is preserved.")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/orchestrator.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3459 bytes

```ts
import type { ImportedInventory } from "./registry.js"

export interface OrchestrationInput {
  prompt: string
  workflowId: string
  context?: Record<string, unknown>
}

export interface TaskCard {
  id: string
  title: string
  prompt: string
  agentDomain: string
  scope: string
  status: "ready"
  dependsOn: string[]
  authority: {
    allowedTools: string[]
    allowedMcpServers: string[]
  }
  expectedOutput: string
  acceptanceCriteria: string[]
  metrics: {
    risk: "low" | "medium" | "high"
    confidenceTarget: number
    evidenceRequired: string[]
  }
}

export interface TaskGraph {
  id: string
  workflowId: string
  sourcePrompt: string
  context: Record<string, unknown>
  tasks: TaskCard[]
  metrics: {
    successCriteria: string[]
    risk: "low" | "medium" | "high"
    confidenceTarget: number
    evidenceRequired: string[]
    doneState: string
  }
  coordination: {
    parallelGroups: string[][]
    checkpoints: string[]
  }
}

function resolveWorkflow(inventory: ImportedInventory, workflowId: string) {
  return inventory.orchestrationPlugins.find(
    (candidate) => candidate.id === workflowId || candidate.aliases.includes(workflowId),
  )
}

const dependencyByDomain: Record<string, string[]> = {
  planner: [],
  implementer: ["task-001"],
  verifier: ["task-001"],
  aggregator: ["task-002", "task-003"],
}

export function orchestratePrompt(inventory: ImportedInventory, input: OrchestrationInput): TaskGraph {
  const workflow = resolveWorkflow(inventory, input.workflowId)
  if (!workflow) {
    throw new Error(`Unknown orchestration workflow: ${input.workflowId}`)
  }
  if (workflow.approval !== "approved") {
    throw new Error(`Workflow is not approved: ${input.workflowId}`)
  }

  const tasks = workflow.agents.map((agent, index): TaskCard => {
    const id = `task-${String(index + 1).padStart(3, "0")}`
    return {
      id,
      title: `${agent.domain}: ${workflow.workflowIntent}`,
      prompt: `${workflow.promptTemplate.replace("{{prompt}}", input.prompt)}\n\nAgent domain: ${agent.domain}\nScope: ${agent.scope}`,
      agentDomain: agent.domain,
      scope: agent.scope,
      status: "ready",
      dependsOn: dependencyByDomain[agent.domain] ?? (index === 0 ? [] : ["task-001"]),
      authority: {
        allowedTools: [...agent.allowedTools].sort(),
        allowedMcpServers: [...agent.allowedMcpServers].sort(),
      },
      expectedOutput: agent.expectedOutput,
      acceptanceCriteria: [
        ...workflow.metricPolicy.successCriteria,
        `Return ${agent.expectedOutput}`,
      ],
      metrics: {
        risk: workflow.metricPolicy.risk,
        confidenceTarget: workflow.metricPolicy.confidence,
        evidenceRequired: workflow.metricPolicy.evidence,
      },
    }
  })

  return {
    id: `task-graph-${input.workflowId.replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/gi, "-").toLowerCase()}`,
    workflowId: workflow.id,
    sourcePrompt: input.prompt,
    context: input.context ?? {},
    tasks,
    metrics: {
      successCriteria: workflow.metricPolicy.successCriteria,
      risk: workflow.metricPolicy.risk,
      confidenceTarget: workflow.metricPolicy.confidence,
      evidenceRequired: workflow.metricPolicy.evidence,
      doneState: workflow.metricPolicy.doneState,
    },
    coordination: {
      parallelGroups: [["task-001"], ["task-002", "task-003"], ["task-004"]],
      checkpoints: ["planning-approved", "taskCard-results-reviewed", "aggregation-complete"],
    },
  }
}
```

```ts
import path from "node:path"
import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url"

export function defaultCoreDevServicesRoot(importMetaUrl = import.meta.url): string {
  const moduleDir = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(importMetaUrl))
  const dirName = path.basename(moduleDir)
  if (dirName === "src" || dirName === "dist") {
    return path.dirname(moduleDir)
  }
  return moduleDir
}

export function defaultWorkspaceRoot(importMetaUrl = import.meta.url): string {
  return path.dirname(path.dirname(defaultCoreDevServicesRoot(importMetaUrl)))
}

### `services/core-dev-services/src/registry.ts`

```ts
import {
  allTargets,
  classifyCapabilityPermissions,
  type Capability,
  type CoreDevServicesManifest,
  type OrchestrationPlugin,
  type Permissions,
  type SourceDefinition,
  type TargetEmissionMode,
  targetModesFor,
  validateManifest,
} from "./manifest.js"
import {
  compoundEngineeringAgentSnapshots,
  compoundEngineeringDisplayName,
  compoundEngineeringSkillSnapshots,
  isCompoundEngineeringListedOnlySkill,
  isCompoundEngineeringWorkflow,
} from "./compound-engineering.js"

export interface ImportedInventory extends CoreDevServicesManifest {
  importedAt: string
}

function approvalFor(source: SourceDefinition, capability: Pick<Capability, "kind" | "command" | "tools" | "env">) {
  const permissions = classifyCapabilityPermissions(capability)
  if (source.approval !== "approved") {
    return source.approval
  }
  if (permissions.shell || permissions.secrets || (permissions.mutating && capability.kind !== "command")) {
    return "quarantined"
  }
  return "approved"
}

type CapabilityEntry = Omit<
  Capability,
  "approval" | "aliases" | "executionResponsibility" | "permissions" | "sourceId" | "targetModes"
> & {
  approval?: Capability["approval"]
  aliases?: string[]
  executionResponsibility?: Capability["executionResponsibility"]
  permissions?: Permissions
  targetMode?: TargetEmissionMode
  targetModes?: Capability["targetModes"]
}

function capability(
  source: SourceDefinition,
  entry: CapabilityEntry,
): Capability {
  const { targetMode, ...capabilityEntry } = entry
  const base = {
    aliases: entry.aliases ?? [],
    targetModes: entry.targetModes ?? targetModesFor(entry.targets, targetMode ?? "callable"),
    executionResponsibility: entry.executionResponsibility ?? { owner: "xlotyl" as const },
    ...capabilityEntry,
    sourceId: source.id,
    approval: entry.approval ?? "quarantined",
  }
  const permissions = entry.permissions ?? classifyCapabilityPermissions(base)
  return {
    ...base,
    approval: entry.approval ?? approvalFor(source, base),
    permissions,
  }
}

function sourceById(sources: SourceDefinition[], id: string): SourceDefinition {
  const source = sources.find((candidate) => candidate.id === id)
  if (!source) {
    throw new Error(`Missing built-in source: ${id}`)
  }
  return source
}

function compoundEngineeringAliases(skillName: string): string[] {
  if (skillName === "ce-code-review") {
    return ["compound-engineering:ce-review"]
  }
  if (skillName === "ce-work") {
    return ["compound-engineering:swarm", "compound-engineering:ce-swarm", "xlotyl:codex-swarm", "xlotyl:swarm"]
  }
  return []
}

function compoundEngineeringDescription(skillName: string, description: string | undefined): string {
  if (skillName === "ce-work") {
    return `${description ?? "Execute work efficiently while maintaining quality and finishing features."} Produces governed swarm taskCards for Codex-supervised dispatch.`
  }
  return description ?? `Imported Compound Engineering skill: ${skillName}.`
}

function compoundEngineeringCapabilities(source: SourceDefinition): Capability[] {
  const skillCapabilities = compoundEngineeringSkillSnapshots.map((skill) => {
    const listedOnly = isCompoundEngineeringListedOnlySkill(skill.name)
    const kind = isCompoundEngineeringWorkflow(skill.name) ? "workflow" : "skill"
    const permissions: Permissions = listedOnly
      ? {
          read: true,
          write: true,
          network: /slack|proof|gemini|release|pr|browser|xcode/i.test(skill.name),
          shell: Boolean(skill.hasScripts) || /setup|worktree|commit|branch|deploy|update/i.test(skill.name),
          secrets: /slack|proof|gemini/i.test(skill.name),
          mutating: true,
        }
      : {
          read: true,
          write: false,
          network: false,
          shell: false,
          secrets: false,
          mutating: false,
        }

    return capability(source, {
      id: `${source.id}:${skill.name}`,
      name: compoundEngineeringDisplayName(skill.name),
      kind,
      aliases: compoundEngineeringAliases(skill.name),
      targets: allTargets,
      targetMode: listedOnly ? "listedOnly" : "callable",
      description: compoundEngineeringDescription(skill.name, skill.description),
      approval: "approved",
      permissions,
      executionResponsibility: listedOnly
        ? {
            owner: "deferred",
            notes: "Imported as a visible Compound Engineering utility; direct shell, hook, or mutating execution waits for the XLOTYL permission broker.",
          }
        : {
            owner: "xlotyl",
            notes: isCompoundEngineeringWorkflow(skill.name)
              ? "Compiled into governed XLOTYL taskCards before agent dispatch."
              : "Callable as an imported helper skill under XLOTYL capability policy.",
          },
    })
  })

  const agentCapabilities = compoundEngineeringAgentSnapshots.map((agent) =>
    capability(source, {
      id: `${source.id}:${agent.path}`,
      name: compoundEngineeringDisplayName(agent.path),
      kind: "agent",
      targets: allTargets,
      targetMode: "callable",
      description:
        agent.description ??
        `Imported Compound Engineering agent persona from ${agent.path}. Platform adapters wrap this agent in scoped XLOTYL taskCards.`,
      approval: "approved",
      permissions: {
        read: true,
        write: false,
        network: /web|slack|issue/i.test(agent.path),
        shell: false,
        secrets: /slack/i.test(agent.path),
        mutating: false,
      },
      executionResponsibility: {
        owner: "xlotyl",
        notes: "Thin platform-native wrapper around scoped XLOTYL taskCards.",
      },
    }),
  )

  return [...skillCapabilities, ...agentCapabilities]
}

function workflowIntent(workflowName: string): string {
  const intents: Record<string, string> = {
    "ce-agent-native-architecture": "Build applications where agents are first-class citizens.",
    "ce-agent-native-audit": "Run comprehensive agent-native architecture review with scored principles.",
    "ce-ideate": "Generate and rank grounded improvement ideas before requirements work.",
    "ce-brainstorm": "Explore requirements and approaches before implementation planning.",
    "ce-plan": "Turn an engineering prompt into a decision-complete implementation planning workflow.",
    "ce-work": "Turn an engineering prompt into scoped swarm taskCards.",
    "ce-code-review": "Review code changes with confidence-gated reviewer taskCards and merge-ready findings.",
    "ce-compound": "Capture solved problems as durable team learning artifacts.",
    "ce-debug": "Investigate bugs systematically before fixing or dispatching implementation taskCards.",
    "ce-optimize": "Run metric-driven optimization planning with experiment taskCards and verification gates.",
    "ce-compound-refresh": "Refresh stale learning docs through scoped review and update taskCards.",
  }
  return intents[workflowName] ?? `Run the Compound Engineering ${workflowName} workflow.`
}

function compoundEngineeringWorkflowPlugin(source: SourceDefinition, workflowName: string): OrchestrationPlugin {
  const intent = workflowIntent(workflowName)
  return {
    id: `${source.id}:${workflowName}`,
    name: compoundEngineeringDisplayName(workflowName),
    sourceId: source.id,
    approval: "approved",
    aliases: compoundEngineeringAliases(workflowName),
    workflowIntent: intent,
    promptTemplate: `Use Compound Engineering ${workflowName} mode for: {{prompt}}`,
    agents: [
      {
        id: "workflow-planner",
        domain: "planner",
        scope: "requirements, constraints, context boundaries, and dependency mapping for this CE workflow",
        allowedTools: ["xlotyl_capability_search", "workspace_file_read"],
        allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
        expectedOutput:
          workflowName === "ce-plan"
            ? "Implementation plan with scope, constraints, and acceptance criteria."
            : "Workflow plan with scope, dependencies, and acceptance criteria.",
      },
      {
        id: "domain-specialist",
        domain: "implementer",
        scope: "workflow-specific implementation shaping and bounded taskCard recommendations only",
        allowedTools: ["workspace_file_read", "workspace_git_status"],
        allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
        expectedOutput: "Scoped taskCard recommendations with file/context boundaries.",
      },
      {
        id: "quality-reviewer",
        domain: "verifier",
        scope: "risk review, evidence requirements, acceptance checks, and escalation triggers",
        allowedTools: ["workspace_file_read", "xlotyl_capability_get"],
        allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
        expectedOutput: "Verification expectations, risk notes, and confidence assessment.",
      },
      {
        id: "workflow-aggregator",
        domain: "aggregator",
        scope: "merge workflow findings into a final XLOTYL-coordinated handoff",
        allowedTools: ["workspace_file_read", "workspace_git_status"],
        allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
        expectedOutput: "Final workflow handoff with taskCards, dependencies, and done-state evidence.",
      },
    ],
    breakoutRules: [
      "Treat the Compound Engineering workflow as prompt-shaping policy; XLOTYL owns final task delineation.",
      "Create bounded taskCards before any platform-native agent receives work.",
      "Keep deferred shell or mutating utilities as capability metadata until permission brokering exists.",
    ],
    reviewExpectations: [
      "Every taskCard must include acceptance criteria and evidence requirements.",
      "Aliases normalize to canonical upstream workflow names in returned task graphs.",
    ],
    contextPreferences: ["repo guidance", "approved capabilities", "CE source provenance", "acceptance criteria"],
    metricPolicy: {
      successCriteria: [
        "The canonical CE workflow is preserved.",
        "Task taskCards have scoped authority and clear expected outputs.",
        "Deferred utilities are visible but not directly executable.",
      ],
      risk: workflowName === "ce-code-review" || workflowName === "ce-debug" ? "medium" : "low",
      confidence: 0.82,
      evidence: ["task_graph", "agent_taskCard", "verification_report"],
      doneState: "All taskCards satisfy CE-derived acceptance criteria and XLOTYL aggregation has no blocking gaps.",
    },
  }
}

export function importPinnedSources(registry: CoreDevServicesManifest): ImportedInventory {
  const manifest = validateManifest(registry)
  const compound = sourceById(manifest.sources, "compound-engineering")

  const capabilities: Capability[] = [

    capability(spectacular, {

      description: "Expose Spectacular plan execution as a XLOTYL-governed Codex command capability.",
    }),

        {
          id: "spec-writer",
          domain: "planner",

          allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
          expectedOutput: "Spec summary with anchored requirements and acceptance criteria.",
        },
        {
          id: "task-decomposer",
          domain: "implementer",
          scope: "task decomposition, file ownership, dependency analysis, and phase grouping",
          allowedTools: ["workspace_file_read", "workspace_git_status"],
          allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
          expectedOutput: "Task plan with sequential and parallel phase boundaries.",
        },
        {
          id: "phase-executor",
          domain: "implementer",
          scope: "execute only assigned taskCards in isolated worktrees when parallelism is allowed",
          allowedTools: ["workspace_file_read", "workspace_file_edit", "workspace_bash"],
          allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
          expectedOutput: "Per-taskCard implementation report with branch/worktree and verification evidence.",
        },
        {
          id: "reviewer",
          domain: "verifier",
          scope: "quality gates, acceptance review, stack readiness, and escalation decisions",
          allowedTools: ["workspace_file_read", "workspace_bash", "workspace_git_status"],
          allowedMcpServers: ["xlotyl-dev-services"],
          expectedOutput: "Quality-gate report with residual risk and ready/not-ready status.",
        },
      ],
      breakoutRules: [
        "Treat Spectacular as task-shaping policy; XLOTYL remains the task graph authority.",
        "Create parallel phases only when task file ownership does not conflict.",
        "Keep git-spice and worktree operations behind scoped taskCard authority.",
      ],
      reviewExpectations: [
        "Every phase has acceptance criteria.",
        "Quality gates run before stack or merge recommendations.",
      ],
      contextPreferences: ["spec", "plan", "constitutions", "CLAUDE.md development commands", "git status"],
      metricPolicy: {
        successCriteria: [
          "Specs and plans remain attached to every taskCard.",
          "Parallel phases include non-overlap evidence.",
          "Execution reports include branch/worktree and verification evidence.",
        ],
        risk: "medium",
        confidence: 0.82,
        evidence: ["spec_summary", "phase_plan", "quality_gate_report"],
        doneState: "All Spectacular-derived taskCards pass quality gates and are ready for aggregation.",
      },
    },
  ]

  return {
    ...manifest,
    capabilities,
    orchestrationPlugins,
    importedAt: new Date(0).toISOString(),
  }
}

export function resolveCapability(inventory: ImportedInventory, capabilityId: string): Capability | undefined {
  return inventory.capabilities.find(
    (candidate) => candidate.id === capabilityId || candidate.aliases.includes(capabilityId),
  )
}

export function approveCapability(inventory: ImportedInventory, capabilityId: string, approval: Capability["approval"]) {
  const resolved = resolveCapability(inventory, capabilityId)
  const capabilities = inventory.capabilities.map((candidate) =>
    candidate.id === resolved?.id ? { ...candidate, approval } : candidate,
  )
  const capability = capabilities.find((candidate) => candidate.id === resolved?.id)
  if (!capability) {
    throw new Error(`Unknown capability: ${capabilityId}`)
  }
  return {
    inventory: { ...inventory, capabilities },
    capability,
  }
}

### `services/core-dev-services/src/server.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5238 bytes

```ts
import { mkdtemp, readFile, rm } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { buildServer } from "./server.js"

describe("core dev services HTTP API", () => {
  it("exposes health, sources, capabilities, sync planning, and orchestration routes", async () => {
    const app = buildServer()

    const health = await app.inject({ method: "GET", url: "/health" })
    expect(health.statusCode).toBe(200)

    const sources = await app.inject({ method: "GET", url: "/v1/dev-services/sources" })
    expect(sources.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(sources.body).sources).toHaveLength(7)

    const capabilities = await app.inject({ method: "GET", url: "/v1/dev-services/capabilities" })
    expect(capabilities.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(capabilities.body).capabilities.length).toBeGreaterThan(5)

    const syncPlan = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/sync/plan",
      payload: { targets: ["codex", "cursor"], repoRoot: "/repo" },
    })
    expect(syncPlan.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(syncPlan.body).operations.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)

    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xlotyl-api-"))
    try {
      const syncApply = await app.inject({
        method: "POST",
        url: "/v1/dev-services/sync/apply",
        payload: { targets: ["cursor"], repoRoot: root },
      })
      expect(syncApply.statusCode).toBe(200)
      expect(JSON.parse(syncApply.body).writes).toHaveLength(3)
      await expect(readFile(join(root, ".cursor/mcp.json"), "utf8")).resolves.toContain(
        "xlotyl-dev-services",
      )
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }

    const orchestration = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/orchestrations",
      payload: {
        workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-review",
        prompt: "Create portable adapter outputs.",
      },
    })
    expect(orchestration.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(orchestration.body).taskGraph.tasks).toHaveLength(4)
    expect(JSON.parse(orchestration.body).taskGraph.workflowId).toBe("compound-engineering:ce-code-review")

    const swarmPlan = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/codex/swarm-plan",
      payload: {
        workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-agent-native-audit",
        prompt: "Audit this app for agent-native architecture.",
      },
    })
    expect(swarmPlan.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(swarmPlan.body).pipeline.dispatchMode).toBe("codex-subagents")
    expect(JSON.parse(swarmPlan.body).pipeline.pathway.label).toBe("Working for Codex")
    expect(JSON.parse(swarmPlan.body).pipeline.pathway.isDefaultPathway).toBe(false)
    expect(JSON.parse(swarmPlan.body).pipeline.requiresExplicitUserDelegation).toBe(true)

    const importResult = await app.inject({ method: "POST", url: "/v1/dev-services/sources/import" })
    expect(importResult.statusCode).toBe(200)

    const agentRun = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/agents/run",
      payload: { taskId: "task-002", task: { id: "task-002" } },
    })
    expect(agentRun.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(agentRun.body).coordinator).toBe("xlotyl-core-dev-services")
    expect(JSON.parse(agentRun.body).runId).toBe("run-0001-task-002")

    const agentStatus = await app.inject({
      method: "GET",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/agents/runs/run-0001-task-002",
    })
    expect(agentStatus.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(agentStatus.body).status).toBe("queued")

    const agentComplete = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/agents/runs/run-0001-task-002/result",
      payload: { result: { summary: "Implemented bounded taskCard." } },
    })
    expect(agentComplete.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(agentComplete.body).status).toBe("completed")

    const agentResult = await app.inject({
      method: "GET",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/agents/runs/run-0001-task-002/result",
    })
    expect(agentResult.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(agentResult.body).result.summary).toBe("Implemented bounded taskCard.")

    const promotedAgentRun = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/agents/run",
      payload: {
        runtime: "codex-swarm",
        workflowId: "compound-engineering:ce-work",
        prompt: "Break this work into Codex swarm taskCards.",
      },
    })
    expect(promotedAgentRun.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(promotedAgentRun.body).status).toBe("promoted")
    expect(JSON.parse(promotedAgentRun.body).pipeline.dispatchMode).toBe("codex-subagents")
  })

  it("can approve a quarantined capability for future generated inventories", async () => {
    const app = buildServer()
    const res = await app.inject({
      method: "POST",
      url: "/v1/dev-services/capabilities/private-journal-mcp:server/approval",
      payload: { approval: "approved" },
    })

    expect(res.statusCode).toBe(200)
    expect(JSON.parse(res.body).capability.approval).toBe("approved")
  })
})
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/server.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 6657 bytes

```ts
import Fastify from "fastify"
import { z } from "zod"
import { createAgentRunStore, type AgentRunArtifact } from "./agent-runtime.js"
import { generateAdapters } from "./adapters.js"
import { createCodexSwarmPipeline } from "./codex-swarm.js"
import { defaultSourceRegistry, targetSchema } from "./manifest.js"
import { orchestratePrompt, type TaskGraph } from "./orchestrator.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot } from "./paths.js"
import { approveCapability, importPinnedSources, type ImportedInventory } from "./registry.js"
import { createSyncPlan, writeSyncPlan } from "./sync.js"

const targetListSchema = z.array(targetSchema).default(["codex", "claude", "cursor", "antigravity"])
const orchestrationBodySchema = z.object({
  workflowId: z.string(),
  prompt: z.string(),
  context: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
})
const codexSwarmBodySchema = z.object({
  workflowId: z.string().optional(),
  prompt: z.string().optional(),
  context: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
  taskGraph: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
})
const runIdParamsSchema = z.object({ runId: z.string() })
const agentRunBodySchema = z.object({
  task: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
  taskId: z.string().optional(),
  runtime: z.string().optional(),
  workflowId: z.string().optional(),
  prompt: z.string().optional(),
  context: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
  taskGraph: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
})
const agentResultBodySchema = z.object({
  result: z.unknown().optional(),
  artifacts: z.array(z.record(z.unknown())).optional(),
  error: z.string().optional(),
  status: z.enum(["completed", "failed"]).optional(),
})

function taskGraphFromBody(inventory: ImportedInventory, body: z.infer<typeof codexSwarmBodySchema>): TaskGraph {
  if (body.taskGraph) {
    return body.taskGraph as unknown as TaskGraph
  }
  return orchestratePrompt(inventory, {
    workflowId: body.workflowId ?? "compound-engineering:ce-work",
    prompt: body.prompt ?? "",
    context: body.context,
  })
}

export function buildServer(initialInventory: ImportedInventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())) {
  let inventory = initialInventory
  const agentRuns = createAgentRunStore()
  const app = Fastify({ logger: false })

  app.get("/health", async () => ({
    status: "healthy",
    service: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
    schemaVersion: inventory.schemaVersion,
  }))

  app.get("/v1/dev-services/sources", async () => ({ sources: inventory.sources }))

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/sources/import", async () => {
    inventory = importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())
    return { inventory }
  })

  app.get("/v1/dev-services/capabilities", async () => ({
    capabilities: inventory.capabilities,
    orchestrationPlugins: inventory.orchestrationPlugins,
  }))

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/capabilities/:id/approval", async (request, reply) => {
    const params = z.object({ id: z.string() }).parse(request.params)
    const body = z.object({ approval: z.enum(["quarantined", "approved", "disabled"]) }).parse(request.body)
    try {
      const result = approveCapability(inventory, params.id, body.approval)
      inventory = result.inventory
      return { capability: result.capability }
    } catch (error) {
      await reply.code(404).send({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown capability" })
    }
  })

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/sync/plan", async (request) => {
    const body = z.object({
      targets: targetListSchema,
      repoRoot: z.string().default(defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()),
      homeDir: z.string().optional(),
      global: z.boolean().default(false),
    }).parse(request.body ?? {})
    const files = generateAdapters(inventory, { targets: body.targets })
    return createSyncPlan(files, body)
  })

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/sync/apply", async (request) => {
    const body = z.object({
      targets: targetListSchema,
      repoRoot: z.string().default(defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()),
      homeDir: z.string().optional(),
      global: z.boolean().default(false),
    }).parse(request.body ?? {})
    const files = generateAdapters(inventory, { targets: body.targets })
    return writeSyncPlan(createSyncPlan(files, body))
  })

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/orchestrations", async (request) => {
    const body = orchestrationBodySchema.parse(request.body)
    return { taskGraph: orchestratePrompt(inventory, body) }
  })

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/codex/swarm-plan", async (request) => {
    const body = codexSwarmBodySchema.parse(request.body ?? {})
    return { pipeline: createCodexSwarmPipeline({ taskGraph: taskGraphFromBody(inventory, body) }) }
  })

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/agents/run", async (request) => {
    const body = agentRunBodySchema.parse(request.body ?? {})
    if (body.runtime === "codex-swarm") {
      return {
        status: "promoted",
        coordinator: "xlotyl-core-dev-services",
        pipeline: createCodexSwarmPipeline({ taskGraph: taskGraphFromBody(inventory, body) }),
      }
    }
    return agentRuns.queueRun({ taskId: body.taskId, runtime: body.runtime, task: body.task })
  })

  app.get("/v1/dev-services/agents/runs/:runId", async (request, reply) => {
    const params = runIdParamsSchema.parse(request.params)
    const status = agentRuns.status({ runId: params.runId })
    if (!status) {
      return reply.code(404).send({ error: `Unknown agent run: ${params.runId}` })
    }
    return status
  })

  app.get("/v1/dev-services/agents/runs/:runId/result", async (request, reply) => {
    const params = runIdParamsSchema.parse(request.params)
    const result = agentRuns.result({ runId: params.runId })
    if (!result) {
      return reply.code(404).send({ error: `Unknown agent run: ${params.runId}` })
    }
    return result
  })

  app.post("/v1/dev-services/agents/runs/:runId/result", async (request, reply) => {
    const params = runIdParamsSchema.parse(request.params)
    const body = agentResultBodySchema.parse(request.body ?? {})
    try {
      return agentRuns.completeRun({
        runId: params.runId,
        result: body.result,
        artifacts: body.artifacts as AgentRunArtifact[] | undefined,
        error: body.error,
        status: body.status,
      })
    } catch (error) {
      return reply.code(404).send({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown agent run" })
    }
  })

  return app
}

export async function startHttpServer(port = Number(process.env.XLOTYL_DEV_SERVICES_PORT ?? 8765)) {
  const app = buildServer()
  await app.listen({ port, host: "127.0.0.1" })
  return app
}

if (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}`) {
  await startHttpServer()
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/aggregate-run.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4729 bytes

````ts
import { readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import type { XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { serializeDatasetRows } from "./dataset.js"
import { readGraphFromDisk } from "./import-run.js"
import { datasetPath, dispatchLogPath, finalReportPath } from "./paths.js"

interface DispatchRecord {
  ts?: string
  kind?: string
  task_card_id?: string
  status?: string
  evaluation_status?: string
  requires_replan?: boolean
  message?: string
  /** Present on evaluation log lines */
  reason?: string
}

async function readJsonlRecords(filePath: string): Promise<DispatchRecord[]> {
  const text = await readFile(filePath, "utf8")
  const records: DispatchRecord[] = []
  for (const line of text.split("\n")) {
    const trimmed = line.trim()
    if (!trimmed) {
      continue
    }
    try {
      records.push(JSON.parse(trimmed) as DispatchRecord)
    } catch {
      records.push({ kind: "error", message: "malformed_jsonl_line" })
    }
  }
  return records
}

/**
 * Build `final-report.md` and `dataset.jsonl` from graph + dispatch log.
 */
export async function aggregateRun(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string): Promise<{ reportPath: string; datasetPath: string }> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  const graph = await readGraphFromDisk(root, runId)
  const logPath = dispatchLogPath(root, runId)
  let records: DispatchRecord[] = []
  try {
    records = await readJsonlRecords(logPath)
  } catch {
    records = []
  }

  const syncByTaskCard = new Map<string, DispatchRecord[]>()
  const evalByTaskCard = new Map<string, DispatchRecord[]>()
  for (const record of records) {
    if (!record.task_card_id) {
      continue
    }
    if (record.kind === "sync") {
      const bucket = syncByTaskCard.get(record.task_card_id) ?? []
      bucket.push(record)
      syncByTaskCard.set(record.task_card_id, bucket)
    }
    if (record.kind === "evaluation") {
      const bucket = evalByTaskCard.get(record.task_card_id) ?? []
      bucket.push(record)
      evalByTaskCard.set(record.task_card_id, bucket)
    }
  }

  const lines: string[] = []
  lines.push("# XLOTYL Run Report", "")
  lines.push("## Run metadata", "")
  lines.push(`- run_id: \`${graph.run_id}\``)
  lines.push(`- workflow_id: \`${graph.workflow_id}\``)
  lines.push(`- runtime_target: \`${graph.runtime_target}\``)
  lines.push(`- planning_owner: \`${graph.planning_owner}\``)
  lines.push("")

  lines.push("## Goal", "", graph.source_goal, "")

  lines.push("## Phase summary", "")
  for (const phase of graph.phases) {
    lines.push(`- **${phase.id}** — ${phase.name}`)
  }
  lines.push("")

  lines.push("## Task taskCard results", "")
  lines.push("| TaskCard | Last sync status | Last evaluation |", "| --- | --- | --- |")
  for (const task of graph.tasks) {
    const syncs = syncByTaskCard.get(task.id) ?? []
    const evals = evalByTaskCard.get(task.id) ?? []
    const lastSync = syncs.at(-1)?.status ?? "—"
    const lastEval = evals.at(-1)?.evaluation_status ?? "—"
    lines.push(`| \`${task.id}\` | ${lastSync} | ${lastEval} |`)
  }
  lines.push("")

  lines.push("## Dispatch log excerpt", "")
  lines.push("```json")
  lines.push(JSON.stringify(records.slice(-20), null, 2))
  lines.push("```")
  lines.push("")

  const reportBody = `${lines.join("\n")}\n`
  const reportFile = finalReportPath(root, runId)
  await writeFile(reportFile, reportBody, "utf8")

  const datasetRows = buildDatasetRows(graph, records)
  const datasetFile = datasetPath(root, runId)
  await writeFile(datasetFile, serializeDatasetRows(datasetRows), "utf8")

  return { reportPath: reportFile, datasetPath: datasetFile }
}

function buildDatasetRows(graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph, records: DispatchRecord[]): Record<string, unknown>[] {
  const rows: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
  rows.push({
    row_type: "run",
    run_id: graph.run_id,
    workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
    task_count: graph.tasks.length,
    log_events: records.length,
  })
  for (const task of graph.tasks) {
    rows.push({
      row_type: "taskCard",
      run_id: graph.run_id,
      task_card_id: task.id,
      task_card_type: task.task_card_type,
      priority: task.priority,
    })
  }
  for (const record of records) {
    if (record.kind === "evaluation" && record.task_card_id) {
      rows.push({
        row_type: "evaluation",
        run_id: graph.run_id,
        task_card_id: record.task_card_id,
        evaluation_status: record.evaluation_status,
        requires_replan: record.requires_replan,
      })
    }
  }
  rows.push({
    row_type: "aggregate",
    run_id: graph.run_id,
    workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
    task_card_count: graph.tasks.length,
  })
  return rows
}
````

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/binding.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2895 bytes

```ts
/**
 * Stoneforge runtime binding: local adapter artifacts vs real `sf` CLI.
 */

/**
 * - `local-artifact` / `sf-cli`: supported today (`sf` is Node `sf.js`).
 * - `http`: reserved for a future `StoneforgeHttpBinding` (native API client); not implemented yet.
 */
export type StoneforgeBinding =
  | { kind: "local-artifact" }
  | { kind: "sf-cli"; sfBinPath: string }
  | { kind: "http"; baseUrl: string }

export interface StoneforgeBindingOptions {
  binding?: StoneforgeBinding
}

function valueAfter(args: string[], flag: string): string | undefined {
  const index = args.indexOf(flag)
  return index >= 0 ? args[index + 1] : undefined
}

/**
 * Resolve binding from `xsf`-style argv plus process env.
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * args : string[]
 *     CLI tokens after the `xsf` subcommand (e.g. `import`, `--binding`, `sf-cli`).
 *
 * Returns
 * -------
 * StoneforgeBinding
 *     Resolved binding mode.
 */
export function resolveStoneforgeBindingFromXsfArgs(args: string[]): StoneforgeBinding {
  const selected = valueAfter(args, "--binding") ?? process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_BINDING ?? "local-artifact"
  if (selected === "local-artifact") {
    return { kind: "local-artifact" }
  }
  if (selected === "sf-cli") {
    const sfBinPath = valueAfter(args, "--sf-bin") ?? process.env.STONEFORGE_SF_BIN ?? process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN
    if (!sfBinPath) {
      throw new Error("xsf binding sf-cli requires --sf-bin <path> or STONEFORGE_SF_BIN/XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN")
    }
    return { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath }
  }
  if (selected === "http") {
    throw new Error(
      "Stoneforge HTTP/native API binding is not implemented; use local-artifact or sf-cli (Node sf.js) until StoneforgeHttpBinding ships.",
    )
  }
  throw new Error(`Unknown xsf binding: ${selected}. Expected local-artifact, sf-cli, or http (http is reserved / not implemented).`)
}

/**
 * Resolve binding from MCP tool arguments (optional `binding`, `sfBinPath`).
 */
export function resolveStoneforgeBindingFromMcpArgs(args: Record<string, unknown>): StoneforgeBinding {
  const mode = typeof args.binding === "string" ? args.binding : "local-artifact"
  if (mode === "local-artifact") {
    return { kind: "local-artifact" }
  }
  if (mode === "sf-cli") {
    const sfBinPath =
      typeof args.sfBinPath === "string" && args.sfBinPath.length > 0
        ? args.sfBinPath
        : process.env.STONEFORGE_SF_BIN ?? process.env.XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN
    if (!sfBinPath) {
      throw new Error("MCP binding sf-cli requires sfBinPath or STONEFORGE_SF_BIN/XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN")
    }
    return { kind: "sf-cli", sfBinPath }
  }
  if (mode === "http") {
    throw new Error(
      "MCP binding http is not implemented; use local-artifact or sf-cli until StoneforgeHttpBinding exists.",
    )
  }
  throw new Error(`Unknown MCP binding: ${mode}. Expected local-artifact or sf-cli.`)
}
```
