### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/contract.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 11337 bytes

```ts
import { z } from "zod"

/** Whether a taskCard should spawn another orchestration generation or execute directly. */
export const decompositionPolicySchema = z.enum(["orchestrate", "terminal", "auto"])
export type DecompositionPolicy = z.infer<typeof decompositionPolicySchema>

export const ambiguityLevelSchema = z.enum(["none", "low", "medium", "high"])
export type AmbiguityLevel = z.infer<typeof ambiguityLevelSchema>

export const orchestrationTerminalitySchema = z.enum(["terminal", "needs_decomposition", "needs_clarification"])
export type OrchestrationTerminality = z.infer<typeof orchestrationTerminalitySchema>

export const orchestrationNextStepSchema = z.enum(["execute", "decompose", "clarify", "escalate", "reject"])
export type OrchestrationNextStep = z.infer<typeof orchestrationNextStepSchema>

/**
 * Orchestration state contract: bridge between graph compilation and routing/dispatch policy.
 *
 * This is intentionally task-local and strictly typed:
 * - compiler emits it deterministically
 * - routers / harnesses consume it for executor selection and escalation policy
 */
export const orchestrationStateSchema = z
  .object({
    ambiguity_level: ambiguityLevelSchema,
    terminality: orchestrationTerminalitySchema,
    missing_information: z.array(z.string()),
    recommended_next_step: orchestrationNextStepSchema,
    allowed_executor_tiers: z.array(z.string()),
    required_contracts: z.array(z.string()),
    blocking_reasons: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export type OrchestrationState = z.infer<typeof orchestrationStateSchema>

/** Single taskCard in a Stoneforge-targeted XLOTYL graph. */
export const stoneforgeTaskCardSchema = z
  .object({
    id: z.string().min(1),
    phase_id: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    title: z.string().min(1),
    /**
     * Concrete objective statement for execution.
     *
     * Optional at the schema layer for backward compatibility, but required by
     * terminality governance when `decomposition_policy` is `terminal`.
     */
    objective: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    task_card_type: z.string().min(1),
    worker_role: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    priority: z.number().int(),
    /** Blocker taskCard ids that must complete before this taskCard may run. */
    dependencies: z.array(z.string()),
    scope: z
      .object({
        include_paths: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
        exclude_paths: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
      })
      .strict()
      .optional(),
    tools: z.array(z.string()).default([]),
    /**
     * Selected runtime environment id for this task (capability-package scoped).
     * Optional at schema layer; required for terminal tasks.
     */
    runtime_environment_id: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    /**
     * Selected execution adapter id / tool surface for this task.
     * Optional at schema layer; required for terminal tasks.
     */
    execution_adapter_id: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    acceptance_criteria: z.array(z.string()).min(1),
    metrics: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
    expected_artifacts: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
    /**
     * Validator ids that must be satisfied for execution to be considered successful.
     * Optional at schema layer; required (or equivalent verification artifact requirement)
     * for terminal tasks.
     */
    validator_ids: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    /**
     * If present and non-empty, the task is waiting on human clarification and must not
     * be treated as terminal execution-ready work.
     */
    clarification_dependencies: z.array(z.string().min(1)).optional(),
    handoff_policy: z.record(z.unknown()).optional(),
    /** Generation depth for recursive orchestration (0 = root graph). */
    generation: z.number().int().nonnegative().default(0),
    /** Run id of the parent graph that spawned this taskCard. Required when generation > 0. */
    parent_run_id: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    /** TaskCard id from the parent graph that this task decomposes. Required when generation > 0. */
    parent_task_card_id: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    /** Agent behavior for the next step in the orchestration ladder. */
    decomposition_policy: decompositionPolicySchema.default("auto"),
    orchestration_state: orchestrationStateSchema.optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export const xlotylStoneforgeGraphSchema = z
  .object({
    run_id: z.string().min(1),
    workflow_id: z.string().min(1),
    workflow_title: z.string().min(1),
    source_goal: z.string().min(1),
    planning_owner: z.literal("xlotyl"),
    runtime_target: z.literal("stoneforge"),
    execution_mode: z.literal("xlotyl_stoneforge").optional(),
    dispatch_policy: z
      .object({
        requires_human_approval_before_activation: z.boolean(),
        max_parallel_workers: z.number().int().positive().optional(),
        default_worker_provider: z.string().optional(),
        allowed_worker_providers: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
        /**
         * Cap successful replan → re-import cycles for this run (excludes the initial `import`).
         * Omitted = unlimited. Enforced in `replan-pipeline` / `xsf replan` / `xlotyl_stoneforge_replan`.
         */
        max_replan_cycles: z.number().int().nonnegative().optional(),
        /**
         * Safety cap for recursive decomposition depth. Defaults to 4 generations.
         */
        max_generation_depth: z.number().int().positive().max(10).default(4),
        /**
         * Safety cap for how many siblings a single parent taskCard can spawn.
         */
        max_fan_out: z.number().int().positive().max(50).default(10),
      })
      .strict(),
    phases: z
      .array(
        z
          .object({
            id: z.string().min(1),
            name: z.string().min(1),
            purpose: z.string().optional(),
          })
          .strict(),
      )
      .min(1),
    tasks: z.array(stoneforgeTaskCardSchema).min(1),
    aggregation: z
      .object({
        owner: z.literal("xlotyl").optional(),
        final_artifact: z.string().optional(),
        include_task_metrics: z.boolean().optional(),
      })
      .strict()
      .optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export type XlotylStoneforgeGraph = z.infer<typeof xlotylStoneforgeGraphSchema>
export type StoneforgeTaskCard = z.infer<typeof stoneforgeTaskCardSchema>

export interface GraphValidationSuccess {
  ok: true
  graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph
}

export interface GraphValidationFailure {
  ok: false
  errors: string[]
}

export type GraphValidationResult = GraphValidationSuccess | GraphValidationFailure

/** Parse and validate a Stoneforge-target XLOTYL graph (schema + DAG + id references). */
export function validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(input: unknown): GraphValidationResult {
  const parsed = xlotylStoneforgeGraphSchema.safeParse(input)
  if (!parsed.success) {
    return { ok: false, errors: parsed.error.errors.map((issue) => `${issue.path.join(".")}: ${issue.message}`) }
  }
  const graph = parsed.data
  const errors: string[] = []

  const ids = new Set(graph.tasks.map((task) => task.id))
  if (ids.size !== graph.tasks.length) {
    errors.push("tasks: duplicate taskCard ids")
  }

  const phaseIds = new Set(graph.phases.map((phase) => phase.id))
  for (const task of graph.tasks) {
    if (task.phase_id && !phaseIds.has(task.phase_id)) {
      errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: unknown phase_id "${task.phase_id}"`)
    }
    for (const blocker of task.dependencies) {
      if (!ids.has(blocker)) {
        errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: dependency references unknown taskCard id "${blocker}"`)
      }
      if (blocker === task.id) {
        errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: self-dependency is not allowed`)
      }
    }
  }

  const cycle = detectDependencyCycle(graph.tasks)
  if (cycle) {
    errors.push(`tasks: dependency cycle detected (${cycle.join(" -> ")})`)
  }

  const maxGenerationDepth = graph.dispatch_policy.max_generation_depth
  const maxFanOut = graph.dispatch_policy.max_fan_out
  for (const task of graph.tasks) {
    if (task.generation > maxGenerationDepth) {
      errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: generation ${task.generation} exceeds max_generation_depth ${maxGenerationDepth}`)
    }
    if (task.generation > 0 && !task.parent_run_id) {
      errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: generation ${task.generation} > 0 but parent_run_id is missing`)
    }
    if (task.generation > 0 && !task.parent_task_card_id) {
      errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: generation ${task.generation} > 0 but parent_task_card_id is missing`)
    }
    if (task.generation === 0 && task.parent_run_id) {
      errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: generation 0 must not have parent_run_id`)
    }
    if (task.generation === 0 && task.parent_task_card_id) {
      errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: generation 0 must not have parent_task_card_id`)
    }

    if (task.decomposition_policy === "orchestrate") {
      const requiredTools = [
        "xlotyl_orchestrate",
        "xlotyl_stoneforge_validate",
        "xlotyl_stoneforge_import",
        "xlotyl_stoneforge_activate",
      ]
      for (const requiredTool of requiredTools) {
        if (!task.tools.includes(requiredTool)) {
          errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: decomposition_policy 'orchestrate' requires tool '${requiredTool}'`)
        }
      }
      const writeTools = [
        "workspace_file_edit",
        "write_to_file",
        "replace_file_content",
        "multi_replace_file_content",
        "run_command",
        "git_commit",
      ]
      for (const writeTool of writeTools) {
        if (task.tools.includes(writeTool)) {
          errors.push(`tasks.${task.id}: decomposition_policy 'orchestrate' forbids write tool '${writeTool}'`)
        }
      }
    }
  }

  const fanOutCounts = new Map<string, number>()
  for (const task of graph.tasks) {
    if (!task.parent_task_card_id) {
      continue
    }
    const key = `${task.parent_run_id ?? ""}:${task.parent_task_card_id}`
    fanOutCounts.set(key, (fanOutCounts.get(key) ?? 0) + 1)
  }
  for (const [key, count] of fanOutCounts) {
    if (count > maxFanOut) {
      errors.push(`tasks: parent ${key} has ${count} children, exceeding max_fan_out ${maxFanOut}`)
    }
  }

  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return { ok: false, errors }
  }
  return { ok: true, graph }
}

function detectDependencyCycle(tasks: StoneforgeTaskCard[]): string[] | null {
  const idSet = new Set(tasks.map((task) => task.id))
  const adj = new Map<string, string[]>()
  for (const task of tasks) {
    adj.set(task.id, task.dependencies.filter((dep) => idSet.has(dep)))
  }

  const visiting = new Set<string>()
  const visited = new Set<string>()
  const stack: string[] = []

  function dfs(node: string): string[] | null {
    if (visiting.has(node)) {
      const cycleStart = stack.indexOf(node)
      return cycleStart >= 0 ? [...stack.slice(cycleStart), node] : [node]
    }
    if (visited.has(node)) {
      return null
    }
    visiting.add(node)
    stack.push(node)
    for (const next of adj.get(node) ?? []) {
      const found = dfs(next)
      if (found) {
        return found
      }
    }
    stack.pop()
    visiting.delete(node)
    visited.add(node)
    return null
  }

  for (const task of tasks) {
    const found = dfs(task.id)
    if (found) {
      return found
    }
  }
  return null
}
```

```ts
import { appendFile, mkdir } from "node:fs/promises"
import { createHash } from "node:crypto"
import path from "node:path"

export interface StoneforgeDaemonDispatchPolicy {
  max_parallel_workers?: number
  allowed_worker_providers?: string[]
  default_worker_provider?: string
}

export interface StoneforgeDaemonReadyTask {
  stoneforge_task_id: string
  title: string
  priority: number
  ready_order: number
  assignee?: string | null
  assignee_id?: string | null
  status?: string
  metadata?: Record<string, unknown>
}

export interface StoneforgeDaemonAgent {
  agent_id: string
  name?: string
  role?: string
  provider?: string
  active_session_id?: string | null
  session_status?: string | null
  metadata?: Record<string, unknown>
}

export interface StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest {
  workspace_root: string
  poll_id: string
  dispatch_policy?: StoneforgeDaemonDispatchPolicy
  ready_tasks: StoneforgeDaemonReadyTask[]
  agents: StoneforgeDaemonAgent[]
  busy_worker_count: number
  max_parallel_workers?: number
}

export type StoneforgeDaemonDecisionAction =
  | {
      action_type: "dispatch_task"
      decision_provider: "xlotyl"
      decision_class: string
      decision_id: string
      input_snapshot_hash: string
      stoneforge_task_id: string
      task_card_id: string
      xlotyl_run_id?: string
      agent_id: string
      provider?: string
      reason: string
    }
  | {
      action_type: "noop"
      decision_provider: "xlotyl"
      decision_class: string
      decision_id: string
      input_snapshot_hash: string
      task_card_id?: string
      stoneforge_task_id?: string
      xlotyl_run_id?: string
      agent_id?: string
      reason: string
    }

export interface StoneforgeDaemonDecisionResult {
  ok: boolean
  decisions: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionAction[]
  decision_log?: string
  error?: string
}

export interface StoneforgeDaemonDecisionOutcome {
  workspace_root: string
  poll_id: string
  decision: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionAction
  executed: boolean
  error?: string
}

export interface StoneforgeDaemonDecisionProvider {
  decideDispatch(request: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest): Promise<StoneforgeDaemonDecisionResult>
  recordDispatchOutcome(outcome: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionOutcome): Promise<void>
}

interface XlotylTaskMeta {
  schema_version?: unknown
  run_id?: unknown
  task_card_id?: unknown
  workflow_id?: unknown
  execution_mode?: unknown
}

function asRecord(value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> | undefined {
  return typeof value === "object" && value !== null && !Array.isArray(value)
    ? (value as Record<string, unknown>)
    : undefined
}

function xlotylMeta(task: StoneforgeDaemonReadyTask): XlotylTaskMeta | undefined {
  return asRecord(asRecord(task.metadata)?.xlotyl) as XlotylTaskMeta | undefined
}

function taskCardIdForTask(task: StoneforgeDaemonReadyTask): string {
  const meta = xlotylMeta(task)
  return typeof meta?.task_card_id === "string" ? meta.task_card_id : `stoneforge:${task.stoneforge_task_id}`
}

function runIdForTask(task: StoneforgeDaemonReadyTask): string | undefined {
  const meta = xlotylMeta(task)
  return typeof meta?.run_id === "string" ? meta.run_id : undefined
}

function providerForAgent(agent: StoneforgeDaemonAgent, defaultProvider?: string): string | undefined {
  const agentMeta = asRecord(asRecord(agent.metadata)?.agent)
  const metadataProvider = agentMeta && typeof agentMeta.provider === "string" ? agentMeta.provider : undefined
  return agent.provider ?? metadataProvider ?? defaultProvider
}

function isIdleWorker(agent: StoneforgeDaemonAgent): boolean {
  if (agent.role !== "worker") {
    return false
  }
  if (agent.active_session_id) {
    return false
  }
  return !agent.session_status || agent.session_status === "idle"
}

function decisionId(request: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest, actionType: string, taskCardId: string, index: number): string {
  return `${request.poll_id}:${actionType}:${taskCardId}:${index}`
}

function inputSnapshotHash(request: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest): string {
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    poll_id: request.poll_id,
    tasks: request.ready_tasks.map((t) => t.stoneforge_task_id),
    agents: request.agents.map((a) => a.agent_id),
    busy: request.busy_worker_count,
  })
  return createHash("sha256").update(payload).digest("hex").slice(0, 16)
}

function noop(
  request: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest,
  reason: string,
  index = 0,
): StoneforgeDaemonDecisionResult {
  return {
    ok: true,
    decisions: [
      {
        action_type: "noop",
        decision_provider: "xlotyl",
        decision_class: "task_routing",
        decision_id: decisionId(request, "noop", "run", index),
        input_snapshot_hash: inputSnapshotHash(request),
        reason,
      },
    ],
    decision_log: daemonDecisionLogPath(request.workspace_root),
  }
}

function daemonDecisionLogPath(workspaceRoot: string): string {
  return path.join(path.resolve(workspaceRoot), ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "daemon", "decision-log.jsonl")
}

function runDecisionLogPath(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string): string {
  return path.join(path.resolve(workspaceRoot), ".stoneforge", "xlotyl", "runs", runId, "decision-log.jsonl")
}

export async function decideStoneforgeDispatch(
  request: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionRequest,
): Promise<StoneforgeDaemonDecisionResult> {
  const maxParallel =
    request.max_parallel_workers ??
    request.dispatch_policy?.max_parallel_workers ??
    Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY
  const remainingSlots = maxParallel - request.busy_worker_count
  if (remainingSlots <= 0) {
    return noop(request, "XLOTYL dispatch policy has no available worker slots.")
  }

  const readyTasks = [...request.ready_tasks]
    .filter((task) => !task.assignee && !task.assignee_id)
    .sort((left, right) => left.priority - right.priority || left.ready_order - right.ready_order)
  if (readyTasks.length === 0) {
    return noop(request, "No unassigned ready Stoneforge tasks are available.")
  }

  const allowedProviders = request.dispatch_policy?.allowed_worker_providers
  const defaultProvider = request.dispatch_policy?.default_worker_provider
  const idleWorkers = request.agents
    .filter(isIdleWorker)
    .filter((agent) => {
      if (!allowedProviders || allowedProviders.length === 0) {
        return true
      }
      const provider = providerForAgent(agent, defaultProvider)
      return Boolean(provider && allowedProviders.includes(provider))
    })
  if (idleWorkers.length === 0) {
    return noop(request, "No idle worker is eligible for the ready Stoneforge tasks.")
  }

  const snapshotHash = inputSnapshotHash(request)
  const decisions: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionAction[] = []
  let actionIndex = 0
  let remaining = remainingSlots
  for (const task of readyTasks) {
    if (remaining <= 0 || idleWorkers.length === 0) {
      break
    }
    const worker = idleWorkers.shift()!
    const taskCardId = taskCardIdForTask(task)
    const reason = `Selected highest-priority ready Stoneforge task ${taskCardId} for idle worker ${worker.agent_id}.`
    decisions.push({
      action_type: "dispatch_task",
      decision_provider: "xlotyl",
      decision_class: "task_routing",
      decision_id: decisionId(request, "dispatch_task", taskCardId, actionIndex++),
      input_snapshot_hash: snapshotHash,
      stoneforge_task_id: task.stoneforge_task_id,
      task_card_id: taskCardId,
      xlotyl_run_id: runIdForTask(task),
      agent_id: worker.agent_id,
      provider: providerForAgent(worker, defaultProvider),
      reason,
    })
    remaining -= 1
  }

  if (decisions.length === 0) {
    return noop(request, "No XLOTYL dispatch action was available.")
  }

  return {
    ok: true,
    decisions,
    decision_log: daemonDecisionLogPath(request.workspace_root),
  }
}

function recordFromOutcome(outcome: StoneforgeDaemonDecisionOutcome, now: () => string): Record<string, unknown> {
  const decision = outcome.decision
  return {
    schema_version: 1,
    ts: now(),
    poll_id: outcome.poll_id,
    decision_id: decision.decision_id,
    action_type: decision.action_type,
    task_card_id: decision.task_card_id,
    stoneforge_task_id: decision.stoneforge_task_id,
    agent_id: decision.agent_id,
    reason: decision.reason,
    executed: outcome.executed,
    ...(outcome.error ? { error: outcome.error } : {}),
    decision_provider: "xlotyl",
    ...(decision.xlotyl_run_id ? { xlotyl_run_id: decision.xlotyl_run_id } : {}),
  }
}

async function appendJsonLine(filePath: string, record: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
  await mkdir(path.dirname(filePath), { recursive: true })
  await appendFile(filePath, `${JSON.stringify(record)}\n`, "utf8")
}

export function createStoneforgeDaemonDecisionProvider(options: { now?: () => string } = {}): StoneforgeDaemonDecisionProvider {
  const now = options.now ?? (() => new Date().toISOString())
  return {
    decideDispatch: decideStoneforgeDispatch,
    async recordDispatchOutcome(outcome): Promise<void> {
      const root = path.resolve(outcome.workspace_root)
      const record = recordFromOutcome(outcome, now)
      await appendJsonLine(daemonDecisionLogPath(root), record)
      if (outcome.decision.xlotyl_run_id) {
        await appendJsonLine(runDecisionLogPath(root, outcome.decision.xlotyl_run_id), record)
      }
    },
  }
}
```

```ts
/** Stable schema id for dataset.jsonl rows (plan contract). */
export const XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_DATASET_SCHEMA_VERSION = "xlotyl_stoneforge_dataset_v0"

export function serializeDatasetRows(rows: Record<string, unknown>[]): string {
  const stamped = rows.map((row) => ({
    schema_version: XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_DATASET_SCHEMA_VERSION,
    ...row,
  }))
  return `${stamped.map((row) => JSON.stringify(row)).join("\n")}\n`
}
```

```ts
import type { StoneforgeBinding } from "../binding.js"
import { runSfJson } from "../sf-cli-binding.js"
import type { StoneforgeAdapter, StoneforgeAgent, StoneforgeReadyTask } from "./types.js"

export function createSfCliStoneforgeAdapter(workspaceRoot: string, binding: StoneforgeBinding): StoneforgeAdapter {
  if (binding.kind !== "sf-cli") {
    throw new Error("createSfCliStoneforgeAdapter requires sf-cli binding")
  }
  return {
    listReadyTasks: () => runSfJson<StoneforgeReadyTask[]>(workspaceRoot, binding.sfBinPath, ["ready"]),
    listAgents: () => runSfJson<StoneforgeAgent[]>(workspaceRoot, binding.sfBinPath, ["agent", "list"]),
    dispatchTask: async (taskId: string, agentId: string) => {
      await runSfJson(workspaceRoot, binding.sfBinPath, ["dispatch", taskId, agentId])
    },
    handoffTask: async (taskId: string, message: string) => {
      await runSfJson(workspaceRoot, binding.sfBinPath, ["task", "handoff", taskId, "--message", message])
    },
  }
}
```

```ts
import { appendFile, mkdir, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import {
  contextBundlePath,
  contextBundlesDirectory,
  decisionLogPath,
} from "../paths.js"
import type {
  ContextBundle,
  DecisionAction,
  DecisionExecution,
  DecisionLogRecord,
  OrchestrationState,
} from "./types.js"

export function buildContextBundle(state: OrchestrationState, taskCardId: string): ContextBundle {
  const taskCard = state.graph.tasks.find((task) => task.id === taskCardId)
  if (!taskCard) {
    throw new Error(`Cannot build context bundle for unknown taskCard ${taskCardId}`)
  }
  return {
    schema_version: 1,
    run_id: state.runId,
    task_card_id: taskCard.id,
    title: taskCard.title,
    source_goal: state.graph.source_goal,
    dependencies: taskCard.dependencies,
    scope: taskCard.scope,
    tools: taskCard.tools,
    acceptance_criteria: taskCard.acceptance_criteria,
    expected_artifacts: taskCard.expected_artifacts,
    metrics: taskCard.metrics,
  }
}

export function decisionLogRecordFromAction(
  action: DecisionAction,
  options: { ts: string; executed: boolean },
): DecisionLogRecord {
  return {
    schema_version: 1,
    ts: options.ts,
    decision_id: action.decision_id,
    action_type: action.action_type,
    task_card_id: action.task_card_id,
    stoneforge_task_id: action.stoneforge_task_id,
    agent_id: action.agent_id,
    reason: action.reason,
    executed: options.executed,
  }
}

export async function writeContextBundles(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  state: OrchestrationState,
  actions: DecisionAction[],
): Promise<string[]> {
  const dispatches = actions.filter((action) => action.action_type === "dispatch_task" && action.task_card_id)
  if (dispatches.length === 0) {
    return []
  }
  await mkdir(contextBundlesDirectory(workspaceRoot, state.runId), { recursive: true })
  const paths: string[] = []
  const written = new Set<string>()
  for (const action of dispatches) {
    const taskCardId = action.task_card_id!
    if (written.has(taskCardId)) {
      continue
    }
    const bundlePath = contextBundlePath(workspaceRoot, state.runId, taskCardId)
    await writeFile(bundlePath, `${JSON.stringify(buildContextBundle(state, taskCardId), null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
    paths.push(bundlePath)
    written.add(taskCardId)
  }
  return paths
}

export async function appendDecisionLogRecords(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  actions: DecisionAction[],
  executions: DecisionExecution[],
  now: () => string = () => new Date().toISOString(),
): Promise<string> {
  const executionByDecision = new Map(executions.map((execution) => [execution.decision_id, execution]))
  const lines = actions.map((action) => {
    const execution = executionByDecision.get(action.decision_id)
    const executed = execution ? execution.ok : false
    return JSON.stringify(decisionLogRecordFromAction(action, { ts: now(), executed }))
  })
  if (lines.length > 0) {
    await appendFile(decisionLogPath(workspaceRoot, runId), `${lines.join("\n")}\n`, "utf8")
  }
  return decisionLogPath(workspaceRoot, runId)
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/decision/router.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`

```ts
import type { StoneforgeTaskCard } from "../contract.js"
import type { DecisionAction, DecisionModule, OrchestrationState, TaskSnapshot } from "./types.js"

function decisionId(state: OrchestrationState, actionType: string, taskCardId: string | undefined, index: number): string {
  return `${state.runId}:${actionType}:${taskCardId ?? "run"}:${index}`
}

function handoffAllowed(taskCard: StoneforgeTaskCard | undefined): boolean {
  const policy = taskCard?.handoff_policy
  if (!policy || typeof policy !== "object" || Array.isArray(policy)) {
    return true
  }
  return (policy as { allow_handoff?: unknown }).allow_handoff !== false
}

function taskCardById(state: OrchestrationState, taskCardId: string | undefined): StoneforgeTaskCard | undefined {
  return taskCardId ? state.graph.tasks.find((task) => task.id === taskCardId) : undefined
}

function failureActions(state: OrchestrationState, startIndex: number): DecisionAction[] {
  let index = startIndex
  const actions: DecisionAction[] = []
  for (const event of state.recentEvents) {
    if (event.kind !== "evaluation" || !event.task_card_id || event.evaluation_status === "passed") {
      continue
    }
    if (event.evaluation_status !== "partial" && event.evaluation_status !== "failed") {
      continue
    }
    const taskCardId = event.task_card_id
    const stoneforgeTaskId = state.taskMap[taskCardId]
    if (event.requires_replan) {
      actions.push({
        decision_id: decisionId(state, "request_replan", taskCardId, index++),
        action_type: "request_replan",
        task_card_id: taskCardId,
        stoneforge_task_id: stoneforgeTaskId,
        reason: event.reason ?? `Evaluation for taskCard ${taskCardId} requires XLOTYL replan.`,
        executed: false,
      })
      continue
    }
    if (stoneforgeTaskId && handoffAllowed(taskCardById(state, taskCardId))) {
      actions.push({
        decision_id: decisionId(state, "handoff_task", taskCardId, index++),
        action_type: "handoff_task",
        task_card_id: taskCardId,
        stoneforge_task_id: stoneforgeTaskId,
        reason: event.reason ?? `Evaluation for taskCard ${taskCardId} needs handoff without replan.`,
        executed: false,
      })
      continue
    }
    actions.push({
      decision_id: decisionId(state, "noop", taskCardId, index++),
      action_type: "noop",
      task_card_id: taskCardId,
      stoneforge_task_id: stoneforgeTaskId,
      reason: event.reason ?? `No executable recovery action is available for taskCard ${taskCardId}.`,
      executed: false,
    })
  }
  return actions
}

function sortReadyTasks(tasks: TaskSnapshot[]): TaskSnapshot[] {
  return [...tasks]
    .filter((task) => task.ready && !task.assigned)
    .sort((left, right) => left.priority - right.priority || left.graphIndex - right.graphIndex)
}

export class SimpleTaskRouter implements DecisionModule {
  async decide(state: OrchestrationState): Promise<DecisionAction[]> {
    const actions = failureActions(state, 0)
    const busyWorkers = state.agents.filter((agent) => agent.role === "worker" && !agent.idle)
    const maxParallel = state.graph.dispatch_policy.max_parallel_workers ?? Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY
    let remainingSlots = maxParallel - busyWorkers.length
    if (remainingSlots <= 0) {
      return actions
    }

    const allowedProviders = state.graph.dispatch_policy.allowed_worker_providers
    const defaultProvider = state.graph.dispatch_policy.default_worker_provider
    const idleWorkers = state.agents
      .filter((agent) => agent.role === "worker" && agent.idle)
      .filter((agent) => {
        if (!allowedProviders || allowedProviders.length === 0) {
          return true
        }
        const effectiveProvider = agent.provider ?? defaultProvider
        return Boolean(effectiveProvider && allowedProviders.includes(effectiveProvider))
      })

    const readyTasks = sortReadyTasks(state.tasks)
    let actionIndex = actions.length
    for (const task of readyTasks) {
      if (remainingSlots <= 0 || idleWorkers.length === 0) {
        break
      }
      const worker = idleWorkers.shift()!
      const provider = worker.provider ?? defaultProvider
      const reason = `Selected highest-priority ready taskCard ${task.taskCardId} for idle worker ${worker.agentId}.`
      actions.push({
        decision_id: decisionId(state, "dispatch_task", task.taskCardId, actionIndex++),
        action_type: "dispatch_task",
        task_card_id: task.taskCardId,
        stoneforge_task_id: task.stoneforgeTaskId,
        agent_id: worker.agentId,
        reason,
        executed: false,
        routing: {
          taskId: task.stoneforgeTaskId,
          taskCardId: task.taskCardId,
          agentId: worker.agentId,
          provider,
          contextBundleIds: [task.taskCardId],
          priority: task.priority,
          reason,
        },
      })
      remainingSlots -= 1
    }
    return actions
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/decision/runner.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3069 bytes

```ts
import path from "node:path"
import type { StoneforgeBinding } from "../binding.js"
import { createSfCliStoneforgeAdapter } from "./adapter.js"
import { appendDecisionLogRecords, writeContextBundles } from "./artifacts.js"
import { SimpleTaskRouter } from "./router.js"
import { buildOrchestrationState } from "./snapshot.js"
import type { DecisionExecution, DecisionModule, DecisionRunResult } from "./types.js"

function errorMessage(error: unknown): string {
  return error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
}

export interface RunDecisionOptions {
  workspaceRoot: string
  runId: string
  binding: StoneforgeBinding
  decisionModule?: DecisionModule
}

// V1 intentionally runs outside the Stoneforge daemon. A future Stoneforge daemon refactor should delegate
// routing policy to this `DecisionModule` boundary before dispatch instead of duplicating policy inside the daemon.
export async function runDecisionCycle(options: RunDecisionOptions): Promise<DecisionRunResult> {
  const root = path.resolve(options.workspaceRoot)
  if (options.binding.kind !== "sf-cli") {
    return {
      ok: false,
      run_id: options.runId,
      decisions: [],
      executed: [],
      context_bundles: [],
      error: "xsf decide requires sf-cli binding so it can observe live Stoneforge ready tasks and agents.",
    }
  }
  try {
    const adapter = createSfCliStoneforgeAdapter(root, options.binding)
    const state = await buildOrchestrationState(root, options.runId, adapter)
    const decisions = await (options.decisionModule ?? new SimpleTaskRouter()).decide(state)
    const contextBundles = await writeContextBundles(root, state, decisions)
    const executed: DecisionExecution[] = []
    for (const decision of decisions) {
      if (decision.action_type === "dispatch_task" && decision.stoneforge_task_id && decision.agent_id) {
        try {
          await adapter.dispatchTask(decision.stoneforge_task_id, decision.agent_id)
          executed.push({ ...decision, ok: true })
        } catch (error) {
          executed.push({ ...decision, ok: false, error: errorMessage(error) })
        }
      } else if (decision.action_type === "handoff_task" && decision.stoneforge_task_id) {
        try {
          await adapter.handoffTask(decision.stoneforge_task_id, decision.reason)
          executed.push({ ...decision, ok: true })
        } catch (error) {
          executed.push({ ...decision, ok: false, error: errorMessage(error) })
        }
      }
    }
    const decisionLog = await appendDecisionLogRecords(root, options.runId, decisions, executed)
    const failedExecution = executed.find((execution) => !execution.ok)
    return {
      ok: !failedExecution,
      run_id: options.runId,
      decisions,
      executed,
      decision_log: decisionLog,
      context_bundles: contextBundles,
      error: failedExecution?.error,
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      run_id: options.runId,
      decisions: [],
      executed: [],
      context_bundles: [],
      error: errorMessage(error),
    }
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/decision/snapshot.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4067 bytes

```ts
import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import { readGraphFromDisk, type StoneforgeDraftPlan } from "../import-run.js"
import { dispatchLogPath, draftPlanPath, stoneforgeMapPath } from "../paths.js"
import type {
  AgentSnapshot,
  DecisionEventSnapshot,
  OrchestrationState,
  StoneforgeAdapter,
  StoneforgeAgent,
  StoneforgeReadyTask,
  TaskSnapshot,
} from "./types.js"

function asRecord(value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> | undefined {
  return value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value) ? value as Record<string, unknown> : undefined
}

function stringValue(value: unknown): string | undefined {
  return typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0 ? value : undefined
}

async function readJsonlRecords(filePath: string): Promise<DecisionEventSnapshot[]> {
  try {
    const text = await readFile(filePath, "utf8")
    return text
      .split("\n")
      .map((line) => line.trim())
      .filter(Boolean)
      .flatMap((line): DecisionEventSnapshot[] => {
        try {
          const parsed = JSON.parse(line)
          return asRecord(parsed) ? [parsed as DecisionEventSnapshot] : []
        } catch {
          return [{ kind: "error", reason: "malformed_jsonl_line" }]
        }
      })
  } catch {
    return []
  }
}

function agentSnapshot(agent: StoneforgeAgent): AgentSnapshot | null {
  const rootMeta = asRecord(agent.metadata) ?? {}
  const agentMeta = asRecord(rootMeta.agent) ?? rootMeta
  const role = stringValue(agentMeta.agentRole) ?? stringValue(agent.role)
  const sessionId = stringValue(agentMeta.sessionId) ?? stringValue(agent.sessionId)
  const sessionStatus = stringValue(agentMeta.sessionStatus) ?? stringValue(agent.sessionStatus)
  const provider = stringValue(agentMeta.provider) ?? stringValue(rootMeta.provider) ?? stringValue(agent.provider)
  const agentId = stringValue(agent.id)
  if (!agentId) {
    return null
  }
  return {
    agentId,
    name: stringValue(agent.name),
    role,
    provider,
    sessionId,
    sessionStatus,
    idle: role === "worker" && !sessionId && (!sessionStatus || sessionStatus === "idle"),
  }
}

function assigneeFrom(task: StoneforgeReadyTask): string | undefined {
  return stringValue(task.assignee) ?? stringValue(task.assigneeId)
}

export async function buildOrchestrationState(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  adapter: StoneforgeAdapter,
): Promise<OrchestrationState> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  const graph = await readGraphFromDisk(root, runId)
  const [mapRaw, draftRaw, readyTasks, agents, recentEvents] = await Promise.all([
    readFile(stoneforgeMapPath(root, runId), "utf8"),
    readFile(draftPlanPath(root, runId), "utf8"),
    adapter.listReadyTasks(),
    adapter.listAgents(),
    readJsonlRecords(dispatchLogPath(root, runId)),
  ])

  const taskMap = (JSON.parse(mapRaw) as { mapping?: Record<string, string> }).mapping ?? {}
  const draft = JSON.parse(draftRaw) as StoneforgeDraftPlan
  const readyById = new Map(readyTasks.flatMap((task) => (typeof task.id === "string" ? [[task.id, task]] : [])))
  const draftByTaskCard = new Map(draft.tasks.map((task) => [task.xlotyl_task_card_id, task]))

  const tasks: TaskSnapshot[] = graph.tasks.flatMap((taskCard, graphIndex) => {
    const stoneforgeTaskId = taskMap[taskCard.id] ?? draftByTaskCard.get(taskCard.id)?.stoneforge_task_id
    if (!stoneforgeTaskId) {
      return []
    }
    const readyTask = readyById.get(stoneforgeTaskId)
    const assignee = readyTask ? assigneeFrom(readyTask) : undefined
    return [{
      taskCardId: taskCard.id,
      stoneforgeTaskId,
      title: taskCard.title,
      priority: taskCard.priority,
      graphIndex,
      ready: Boolean(readyTask && !assignee),
      assigned: Boolean(assignee),
      assignee,
    }]
  })

  return {
    runId,
    graph,
    taskMap,
    tasks,
    dependencies: draft.dependencies,
    agents: agents.flatMap((agent) => {
      const snapshot = agentSnapshot(agent)
      return snapshot ? [snapshot] : []
    }),
    recentEvents,
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/evaluation.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 1050 bytes

```ts
import { z } from "zod"

export interface EvaluationEventInput {
  task_card_id: string
  evaluation_status: "passed" | "partial" | "failed"
  requires_replan?: boolean
  reason?: string
  passed_criteria?: number
  failed_criteria?: number
  partial_criteria?: number
}

const evaluationSchema = z.object({
  task_card_id: z.string().min(1),
  evaluation_status: z.enum(["passed", "partial", "failed"]),
  requires_replan: z.boolean().optional(),
  reason: z.string().optional(),
  passed_criteria: z.number().int().nonnegative().optional(),
  failed_criteria: z.number().int().nonnegative().optional(),
  partial_criteria: z.number().int().nonnegative().optional(),
})

export function parseEvaluationPayload(input: unknown):
  | { ok: true; value: EvaluationEventInput }
  | { ok: false; errors: string[] } {
  const parsed = evaluationSchema.safeParse(input)
  if (!parsed.success) {
    return { ok: false, errors: parsed.error.errors.map((issue) => `${issue.path.join(".")}: ${issue.message}`) }
  }
  return { ok: true, value: parsed.data }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/import-run.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 19003 bytes

```ts
import { appendFile, mkdir, readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import type { XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { parseEvaluationPayload } from "./evaluation.js"
import {
  activationPath,
  approvalPath,
  dispatchLogPath,
  draftPlanPath,
  graphJsonPath,
  runDirectory,
  stoneforgeMapPath,
} from "./paths.js"
import type { StoneforgeBinding } from "./binding.js"
import { renderTaskCardDescription } from "./task-card-renderer.js"
import { formatStoneforgeCliError, inspectSfCli, runSfJson } from "./sf-cli-binding.js"

export type { StoneforgeBinding as StoneforgeImportBinding }
export type ImportRunOptions = { binding?: StoneforgeBinding; dryRun?: boolean }

export interface StoneforgeDraftPlan {
  id: string
  title: string
  status: "draft" | "active"
  metadata: Record<string, unknown>
  tasks: Array<{
    stoneforge_task_id: string
    xlotyl_task_card_id: string
    title: string
    priority: number
    description: string
    metadata?: Record<string, unknown>
  }>
  dependencies: Array<{ blocked: string; blocker: string }>
}

export interface StoneforgeMap {
  run_id: string
  mapping: Record<string, string>
}

export interface ImportRunResult {
  run_id: string
  workspaceRoot: string
  paths: {
    graph: string
    map: string
    draftPlan: string
    log: string
  }
  draftPlan: StoneforgeDraftPlan
}

export interface ImportDryRunResult {
  ok: true
  dry_run: true
  run_id: string
  workspaceRoot: string
  task_count: number
  sf_cli?: {
    version: string
  }
}

export type ValidateAndImportRunResult =
  | { ok: true; result: ImportRunResult }
  | ImportDryRunResult
  | { ok: false; errors: string[] }

function nowIso(): string {
  return new Date().toISOString()
}

function syntheticTaskId(taskCardId: string): string {
  return `sf-task-${taskCardId.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]+/g, "-")}`
}

function xlotylTaskMetadata(graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph, taskCardId: string): Record<string, unknown> {
  const taskCard = graph.tasks.find((candidate) => candidate.id === taskCardId)
  return {
    xlotyl: {
      schema_version: 1,
      run_id: graph.run_id,
      task_card_id: taskCardId,
      workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
      execution_mode: graph.execution_mode ?? null,
      generation: taskCard?.generation ?? 0,
      parent_run_id: taskCard?.parent_run_id ?? null,
      parent_task_card_id: taskCard?.parent_task_card_id ?? null,
      decomposition_policy: taskCard?.decomposition_policy ?? "auto",
    },
  }
}

async function appendLog(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string, record: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
  const line = `${JSON.stringify({ ts: nowIso(), ...record })}\n`
  await appendFile(dispatchLogPath(workspaceRoot, runId), line, "utf8")
}

function xlotylPlanMetadata(graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph): Record<string, unknown> {
  return {
    xlotyl: {
      schema_version: 1,
      run_id: graph.run_id,
      workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
      execution_mode: graph.execution_mode ?? null,
      planning_owner: graph.planning_owner,
      runtime_target: graph.runtime_target,
    },
  }
}

function asRecord(value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> | undefined {
  return typeof value === "object" && value !== null && !Array.isArray(value)
    ? (value as Record<string, unknown>)
    : undefined
}

function unwrapShownElement(value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> | undefined {
  const record = asRecord(value)
  return asRecord(record?.element) ?? asRecord(record?.plan) ?? asRecord(record?.task) ?? record
}

function assertUniqueTaskCardTaskMapping(mapping: Record<string, string>): void {
  const byTask = new Map<string, string>()
  for (const [taskCardId, stoneforgeTaskId] of Object.entries(mapping)) {
    const previous = byTask.get(stoneforgeTaskId)
    if (previous && previous !== taskCardId) {
      throw new Error(
        `duplicate taskCard to Stoneforge task mapping: taskCards ${previous} and ${taskCardId} both map to ${stoneforgeTaskId}`,
      )
    }
    byTask.set(stoneforgeTaskId, taskCardId)
  }
}

async function verifySfCliImportMetadata(
  graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph,
  workspaceRoot: string,
  sfBinPath: string,
  planId: string,
  tasks: StoneforgeDraftPlan["tasks"],
): Promise<void> {
  const shownPlan = await runSfJson<unknown>(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, ["show", planId])
  const planXlotyl = asRecord(asRecord(unwrapShownElement(shownPlan)?.metadata)?.xlotyl)
  if (
    planXlotyl?.schema_version !== 1 ||
    planXlotyl.run_id !== graph.run_id ||
    planXlotyl.workflow_id !== graph.workflow_id ||
    planXlotyl.execution_mode !== (graph.execution_mode ?? null)
  ) {
    throw new Error(`sf-cli import metadata verification failed for plan ${planId}`)
  }

  for (const task of tasks) {
    const shownTask = await runSfJson<unknown>(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, ["show", task.stoneforge_task_id])
    const taskXlotyl = asRecord(asRecord(unwrapShownElement(shownTask)?.metadata)?.xlotyl)
    if (
      taskXlotyl?.schema_version !== 1 ||
      taskXlotyl.run_id !== graph.run_id ||
      taskXlotyl.workflow_id !== graph.workflow_id ||
      taskXlotyl.task_card_id !== task.xlotyl_task_card_id ||
      taskXlotyl.execution_mode !== (graph.execution_mode ?? null)
    ) {
      throw new Error(`sf-cli import metadata verification failed for task ${task.stoneforge_task_id}`)
    }
  }
}

async function loadExistingSfDraft(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
): Promise<{
  planId: string
  tasks: StoneforgeDraftPlan["tasks"]
  dependencies: StoneforgeDraftPlan["dependencies"]
  mapping: Record<string, string>
} | null> {
  try {
    const rawDraft = await readFile(draftPlanPath(workspaceRoot, runId), "utf8")
    const draft = JSON.parse(rawDraft) as {
      id?: string
      tasks?: StoneforgeDraftPlan["tasks"]
      dependencies?: StoneforgeDraftPlan["dependencies"]
    }
    if (typeof draft.id !== "string" || !draft.id.startsWith("el-")) {
      return null
    }
    const rawMap = await readFile(stoneforgeMapPath(workspaceRoot, runId), "utf8")
    const map = JSON.parse(rawMap) as { mapping?: Record<string, string> }
    return {
      planId: draft.id,
      tasks: draft.tasks ?? [],
      dependencies: draft.dependencies ?? [],
      mapping: map.mapping ?? {},
    }
  } catch {
    return null
  }
}

async function importViaSfCli(
  graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph,
  workspaceRoot: string,
  sfBinPath: string,
): Promise<StoneforgeDraftPlan> {
  try {
    await readFile(path.join(workspaceRoot, ".stoneforge", "stoneforge.db"), "utf8")
  } catch {
    await runSfJson(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, ["init", "--preset", "review"])
  }

  const existing = await loadExistingSfDraft(workspaceRoot, graph.run_id)
  let planId: string
  const mapping: Record<string, string> = { ...(existing?.mapping ?? {}) }
  const tasks: StoneforgeDraftPlan["tasks"] = [...(existing?.tasks ?? [])]
  const dependencies: StoneforgeDraftPlan["dependencies"] = [...(existing?.dependencies ?? [])]

  if (existing) {
    planId = existing.planId
    assertUniqueTaskCardTaskMapping(mapping)
  } else {
    const plan = await runSfJson<{ id: string }>(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, [
      "plan",
      "create",
      "--title",
      graph.workflow_title,
      "--status",
      "draft",
      "--actor",
      "xlotyl",
    ])
    planId = plan.id
  }

  const planMetadata = xlotylPlanMetadata(graph)
  await runSfJson(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, [
    "update",
    planId,
    "--metadata",
    JSON.stringify(planMetadata),
    "--actor",
    "xlotyl",
  ])

  for (const taskCard of graph.tasks) {
    if (mapping[taskCard.id]) {
      continue
    }
    const created = await runSfJson<{ id: string }>(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, [
      "task",
      "create",
      "--title",
      taskCard.title,
      "--priority",
      String(taskCard.priority),
      "--type",
      "task",
      "--description",
      renderTaskCardDescription(graph, taskCard),
      "--plan",
      planId,
      "--actor",
      "xlotyl",
    ])
    const metadata = xlotylTaskMetadata(graph, taskCard.id)
    await runSfJson(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, [
      "task",
      "update",
      created.id,
      "--metadata",
      JSON.stringify(metadata),
      "--actor",
      "xlotyl",
    ])
    mapping[taskCard.id] = created.id
    tasks.push({
      stoneforge_task_id: created.id,
      xlotyl_task_card_id: taskCard.id,
      title: taskCard.title,
      priority: taskCard.priority,
      description: renderTaskCardDescription(graph, taskCard),
      metadata: xlotylTaskMetadata(graph, taskCard.id),
    })
  }

  const depKey = (blocked: string, blocker: string) => `${blocked}::${blocker}`
  const depSeen = new Set(dependencies.map((d) => depKey(d.blocked, d.blocker)))

  for (const taskCard of graph.tasks) {
    for (const blocker of taskCard.dependencies) {
      const blockedId = mapping[taskCard.id]
      const blockerId = mapping[blocker]
      if (!blockedId || !blockerId) {
        continue
      }
      const key = depKey(blockedId, blockerId)
      if (depSeen.has(key)) {
        continue
      }
      await runSfJson(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, [
        "dependency",
        "add",
        blockedId,
        blockerId,
        "--type",
        "blocks",
      ])
      dependencies.push({ blocked: blockedId, blocker: blockerId })
      depSeen.add(key)
    }
  }

  const shown = await runSfJson<{ plan: { status: string } }>(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, ["plan", "show", planId])
  const planStatus: StoneforgeDraftPlan["status"] =
    shown.plan.status === "active" ? "active" : "draft"

  assertUniqueTaskCardTaskMapping(mapping)
  await verifySfCliImportMetadata(graph, workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, planId, tasks)

  return {
    id: planId,
    title: graph.workflow_title,
    status: planStatus,
    metadata: {
      xlotyl_run_id: graph.run_id,
      xlotyl_workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
      planning_owner: graph.planning_owner,
      runtime_target: graph.runtime_target,
      execution_mode: graph.execution_mode ?? null,
      dispatch_policy: graph.dispatch_policy,
    },
    tasks,
    dependencies,
  }
}

/**
 * Import a validated graph into the workspace run directory and emit adapter-local draft plan artifacts.
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * graph : XlotylStoneforgeGraph
 *     Already validated graph.
 * workspaceRoot : string
 *     Absolute path to workspace root (Stoneforge repo checkout).
 *
 * Returns
 * -------
 * ImportRunResult
 *     Paths and draft plan payload written to disk.
 */
export async function importRun(
  graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph,
  workspaceRoot: string,
  options: ImportRunOptions = {},
): Promise<ImportRunResult> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  const runId = graph.run_id
  await mkdir(runDirectory(root, runId), { recursive: true })

  await writeFile(graphJsonPath(root, runId), `${JSON.stringify(graph, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
  const binding = options.binding ?? { kind: "local-artifact" as const }
  if (binding.kind === "http") {
    throw new Error("importRun: http binding is not implemented (use local-artifact or sf-cli)")
  }
  if (binding.kind === "sf-cli") {
    await inspectSfCli(root, binding.sfBinPath)
  }
  let draftPlan: StoneforgeDraftPlan
  try {
    if (binding.kind === "sf-cli") {
      draftPlan = await importViaSfCli(graph, root, binding.sfBinPath)
    } else {
      const mapping: Record<string, string> = {}
      const tasks: StoneforgeDraftPlan["tasks"] = []
      const dependencies: StoneforgeDraftPlan["dependencies"] = []

      for (const taskCard of graph.tasks) {
        const stoneforge_task_id = syntheticTaskId(taskCard.id)
        mapping[taskCard.id] = stoneforge_task_id
        tasks.push({
          stoneforge_task_id,
        xlotyl_task_card_id: taskCard.id,
        title: taskCard.title,
        priority: taskCard.priority,
        description: renderTaskCardDescription(graph, taskCard),
        metadata: xlotylTaskMetadata(graph, taskCard.id),
      })
      }

      for (const taskCard of graph.tasks) {
        for (const blocker of taskCard.dependencies) {
          dependencies.push({ blocked: mapping[taskCard.id]!, blocker: mapping[blocker]! })
        }
      }

      draftPlan = {
        id: `draft-plan-${runId}`,
        title: graph.workflow_title,
        status: "draft",
        metadata: {
          xlotyl_run_id: runId,
          xlotyl_workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
          planning_owner: graph.planning_owner,
          runtime_target: graph.runtime_target,
          execution_mode: graph.execution_mode ?? null,
          dispatch_policy: graph.dispatch_policy,
        },
        tasks,
        dependencies,
      } satisfies StoneforgeDraftPlan
    }
  } catch (err) {
    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)
    await appendLog(root, runId, { kind: "import", status: "failed", error: message })
    throw err
  }
  const map: StoneforgeMap = {
    run_id: runId,
    mapping: Object.fromEntries(draftPlan.tasks.map((task) => [task.xlotyl_task_card_id, task.stoneforge_task_id])),
  }
  await writeFile(stoneforgeMapPath(root, runId), `${JSON.stringify(map, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
  await writeFile(draftPlanPath(root, runId), `${JSON.stringify(draftPlan, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")

  await appendLog(root, runId, { kind: "import", status: "ok", task_count: graph.tasks.length })

  return {
    run_id: runId,
    workspaceRoot: root,
    paths: {
      graph: graphJsonPath(root, runId),
      map: stoneforgeMapPath(root, runId),
      draftPlan: draftPlanPath(root, runId),
      log: dispatchLogPath(root, runId),
    },
    draftPlan,
  }
}

/**
 * Validate unknown input and import when valid.
 */
export async function validateAndImportRun(
  input: unknown,
  workspaceRoot: string,
  options: ImportRunOptions & { dryRun: true },
): Promise<ImportDryRunResult | { ok: false; errors: string[] }>
export async function validateAndImportRun(
  input: unknown,
  workspaceRoot: string,
  options?: ImportRunOptions & { dryRun?: false | undefined },
): Promise<{ ok: true; result: ImportRunResult } | { ok: false; errors: string[] }>
export async function validateAndImportRun(
  input: unknown,
  workspaceRoot: string,
  options: ImportRunOptions = {},
): Promise<ValidateAndImportRunResult> {
  const validation = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(input)
  if (!validation.ok) {
    return { ok: false, errors: validation.errors }
  }
  if (options.dryRun) {
    try {
      const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
      const binding = options.binding ?? { kind: "local-artifact" as const }
      const sfCli = binding.kind === "sf-cli" ? await inspectSfCli(root, binding.sfBinPath) : undefined
      return {
        ok: true,
        dry_run: true,
        run_id: validation.graph.run_id,
        workspaceRoot: root,
        task_count: validation.graph.tasks.length,
        ...(sfCli ? { sf_cli: sfCli } : {}),
      }
    } catch (error) {
      return { ok: false, errors: [formatStoneforgeCliError(error)] }
    }
  }
  try {
    const result = await importRun(validation.graph, workspaceRoot, options)
    return { ok: true, result }
  } catch (error) {
    return { ok: false, errors: [formatStoneforgeCliError(error)] }
  }
}

export interface ApprovalRecord {
  approved: boolean
  approved_by?: string
  approved_at?: string
  notes?: string
}

export async function writeApproval(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  record: ApprovalRecord,
): Promise<void> {
  const payload = { ...record, approved_at: record.approved_at ?? nowIso() }
  await writeFile(approvalPath(path.resolve(workspaceRoot), runId), `${JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
}

export async function readGraphFromDisk(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string): Promise<XlotylStoneforgeGraph> {
  const raw = await readFile(graphJsonPath(path.resolve(workspaceRoot), runId), "utf8")
  const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as unknown
  const validation = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(parsed)
  if (!validation.ok) {
    throw new Error(`Invalid graph.json: ${validation.errors.join("; ")}`)
  }
  return validation.graph
}

export async function activateRun(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  options: { force?: boolean; approvedBy?: string; binding?: StoneforgeBinding } = {},
): Promise<{ ok: true; idempotent?: boolean } | { ok: false; reason: string }> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  const graph = await readGraphFromDisk(root, runId)

  try {
    await readFile(activationPath(root, runId), "utf8")
    return { ok: true, idempotent: true }
  } catch {
    // First activation continues below.
  }

  if (graph.dispatch_policy.requires_human_approval_before_activation && !options.force) {
    try {
      const approvalRaw = await readFile(approvalPath(root, runId), "utf8")
      const approval = JSON.parse(approvalRaw) as ApprovalRecord
      if (!approval.approved) {
        return { ok: false, reason: "approval.json exists but approved is false" }
      }
    } catch {
      return { ok: false, reason: "requires_human_approval_before_activation but approval.json is missing" }
    }
  }

  const activation = {
    run_id: runId,
    activated_at: nowIso(),
    approved_by: options.approvedBy ?? "operator",
    planning_owner: graph.planning_owner,
    runtime_target: graph.runtime_target,
  }
  if (options.binding?.kind === "sf-cli") {
    try {
      const rawDraft = await readFile(draftPlanPath(root, runId), "utf8")
      const draft = JSON.parse(rawDraft) as { id?: string }
      if (typeof draft.id === "string" && draft.id.startsWith("el-")) {
        await runSfJson(root, options.binding.sfBinPath, ["plan", "activate", draft.id, "--actor", "xlotyl"])
      }
    } catch {
      return { ok: false, reason: "failed to activate Stoneforge plan via sf-cli binding" }
    }
  }
  await writeFile(activationPath(root, runId), `${JSON.stringify(activation, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
  await appendLog(root, runId, { kind: "activate", status: "ok" })
  return { ok: true }
}

export interface SyncEventInput {
  task_card_id: string
  status: string
  message?: string
  metrics?: Record<string, number>
  artifacts?: string[]
}

export async function appendSyncEvent(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  event: SyncEventInput,
): Promise<void> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  await appendLog(root, runId, {
    kind: "sync",
    task_card_id: event.task_card_id,
    status: event.status,
    message: event.message,
    metrics: event.metrics,
    artifacts: event.artifacts,
  })
}

export async function appendEvaluationEvent(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string, event: unknown): Promise<void> {
  const parsed = parseEvaluationPayload(event)
  if (!parsed.ok) {
    throw new Error(`appendEvaluationEvent: ${parsed.errors.join("; ")}`)
  }
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  await appendLog(root, runId, { kind: "evaluation", ...parsed.value })
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/mark-terminal.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5012 bytes

```ts
import { appendFile, readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"

import type { XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { dispatchLogPath, graphJsonPath } from "./paths.js"
import { validateTerminalTaskUnit } from "./terminality-validator.js"

/**
 * Mark Stoneforge task cards as terminal in an already-imported run graph.
 *
 * This is used by generational sequential proof flows where workers need a safe,
 * explicit way to declare terminality without changing import/activate behavior.
 *
 * Contract:
 * - Loads graph.json from `.stoneforge/xlotyl/runs/<run_id>/graph.json`
 * - Applies the mutation (one task or all tasks)
 * - Re-validates using `validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph`
 * - Writes the updated graph.json and appends a dispatch-log event
 */

function nowIso(): string {
  return new Date().toISOString()
}

async function appendLog(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string, record: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
  const line = `${JSON.stringify({ ts: nowIso(), ...record })}\n`
  await appendFile(dispatchLogPath(path.resolve(workspaceRoot), runId), line, "utf8")
}

export interface MarkTerminalOptions {
  taskId?: string
  all?: boolean
  markedBy?: string
  reason?: string
  evidenceRefs?: string[]
}

export type MarkTerminalResult =
  | {
      ok: true
      run_id: string
      updated_task_ids: string[]
      idempotent?: boolean
      marked_by?: string
      reason?: string
      evidence_refs?: string[]
    }
  | { ok: false; errors: string[] }

export async function markTerminal(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  options: MarkTerminalOptions = {},
): Promise<MarkTerminalResult> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  const graphPath = graphJsonPath(root, runId)

  let parsed: unknown
  try {
    const raw = await readFile(graphPath, "utf8")
    parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as unknown
  } catch (error) {
    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
    return { ok: false, errors: [`failed to read graph.json: ${message}`] }
  }

  const validation = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(parsed)
  if (!validation.ok) {
    return { ok: false, errors: [`invalid graph.json: ${validation.errors.join("; ")}`] }
  }
  const graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph = validation.graph

  const targetAll = Boolean(options.all)
  const targetTaskId = typeof options.taskId === "string" && options.taskId.length > 0 ? options.taskId : undefined
  if (!targetAll && !targetTaskId) {
    return { ok: false, errors: ["markTerminal requires either taskId or all=true"] }
  }
  if (targetAll && targetTaskId) {
    return { ok: false, errors: ["markTerminal forbids specifying both taskId and all=true"] }
  }

  const terminalityErrors: string[] = []
  const updated: string[] = []
  const nextTasks = graph.tasks.map((task) => {
    if (targetAll || task.id === targetTaskId) {
      const next = task.decomposition_policy === "terminal" ? task : { ...task, decomposition_policy: "terminal" as const }
      const terminality = validateTerminalTaskUnit(next)
      if (!terminality.ok) {
        const prefix = `tasks.${task.id}: `
        for (const error of terminality.errors) {
          terminalityErrors.push(`${prefix}${error}`)
        }
      }
      if (task.decomposition_policy !== "terminal") {
        updated.push(task.id)
      }
      return next
    }
    return task
  })
  if (terminalityErrors.length > 0) {
    return { ok: false, errors: terminalityErrors }
  }

  if (!targetAll && targetTaskId && !graph.tasks.some((t) => t.id === targetTaskId)) {
    return { ok: false, errors: [`unknown task id: ${targetTaskId}`] }
  }

  if (updated.length === 0) {
    // Even if the call is idempotent, emit an auditable record that it was evaluated.
    await appendLog(root, runId, {
      kind: "mark_terminal",
      status: "noop",
      updated_task_ids: [],
      idempotent: true,
      marked_by: options.markedBy,
      reason: options.reason,
      evidence_refs: options.evidenceRefs,
    })
    return {
      ok: true,
      run_id: runId,
      updated_task_ids: [],
      idempotent: true,
      marked_by: options.markedBy,
      reason: options.reason,
      evidence_refs: options.evidenceRefs,
    }
  }

  const nextGraph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph = { ...graph, tasks: nextTasks }
  const revalidated = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(nextGraph)
  if (!revalidated.ok) {
    return { ok: false, errors: revalidated.errors }
  }

  await writeFile(graphPath, `${JSON.stringify(nextGraph, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
  await appendLog(root, runId, {
    kind: "mark_terminal",
    status: "ok",
    updated_task_ids: updated,
    marked_by: options.markedBy,
    reason: options.reason,
    evidence_refs: options.evidenceRefs,
  })
  return {
    ok: true,
    run_id: runId,
    updated_task_ids: updated,
    marked_by: options.markedBy,
    reason: options.reason,
    evidence_refs: options.evidenceRefs,
  }
}

```

```ts
import type { XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"

/**
 * Whether the graph opts into strict Stoneforge director bypass semantics.
 */
export function isStrictStoneforgeMode(graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph): boolean {
  return graph.execution_mode === "xlotyl_stoneforge"
}

/**
 * Guard against Stoneforge Director decomposition while in strict XLOTYL mode.
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * graph : XlotylStoneforgeGraph
 *     Validated graph.
 * directorAttempted : boolean
 *     True when Stoneforge Director would create or reshape tasks outside adapter import.
 *
 * Raises
 * -----
 * Error
 *     When strict mode forbids the action.
 */
export function assertDirectorBypassAllowed(graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph, directorAttempted: boolean): void {
  if (isStrictStoneforgeMode(graph) && directorAttempted) {
    throw new Error("director_decomposition_forbidden_in_xlotyl_stoneforge_mode")
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/replan-pipeline.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4219 bytes

```ts
import { appendFile, readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { z } from "zod"
import type { StoneforgeBinding } from "./binding.js"
import { mergeGraphsForReplan } from "./replan.js"
import type { ImportRunResult } from "./import-run.js"
import { importRun, readGraphFromDisk } from "./import-run.js"
import { dispatchLogPath, replanStatePath } from "./paths.js"

const replanStateFileSchema = z
  .object({
    replan_cycles_completed: z.number().int().nonnegative(),
    last_idempotency_key: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  })
  .strict()

export type ReplanStateFile = z.infer<typeof replanStateFileSchema>

function nowIso(): string {
  return new Date().toISOString()
}

async function readReplanStateFile(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string): Promise<ReplanStateFile> {
  const p = replanStatePath(workspaceRoot, runId)
  let raw: string
  try {
    raw = await readFile(p, "utf8")
  } catch {
    return { replan_cycles_completed: 0, last_idempotency_key: null }
  }
  const parsed = replanStateFileSchema.safeParse(JSON.parse(raw) as unknown)
  if (!parsed.success) {
    return { replan_cycles_completed: 0, last_idempotency_key: null }
  }
  return {
    replan_cycles_completed: parsed.data.replan_cycles_completed,
    last_idempotency_key: parsed.data.last_idempotency_key ?? null,
  }
}

async function writeReplanStateFile(workspaceRoot: string, runId: string, state: ReplanStateFile): Promise<void> {
  const p = replanStatePath(workspaceRoot, runId)
  await writeFile(p, `${JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
}

async function appendReplanLog(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  record: Record<string, unknown>,
): Promise<void> {
  const line = `${JSON.stringify({ ts: nowIso(), ...record })}\n`
  await appendFile(dispatchLogPath(workspaceRoot, runId), line, "utf8")
}

export type RunReplanResult =
  | { ok: true; deduped: true; replan_cycles_completed: number }
  | { ok: true; deduped: false; import: ImportRunResult; replan_cycles_completed: number }
  | { ok: false; errors: string[] }

/**
 * Merge a replan delta, re-import artifacts, and maintain replan caps + idempotency state on disk.
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * workspaceRoot, runId, delta
 *     Same semantics as `mergeGraphsForReplan` + `importRun` after a successful merge.
 * options.idempotencyKey
 *     If provided and it matches the last successful replan key, returns `{ ok, deduped: true }` (retry safety).
 * options.binding
 *     Same as `importRun` (local-artifact or sf-cli; http is reserved and rejected at resolution).
 */
export async function runReplanMergeAndImport(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
  delta: unknown,
  options: { binding: StoneforgeBinding; idempotencyKey?: string },
): Promise<RunReplanResult> {
  if (options.binding.kind === "http") {
    return { ok: false, errors: ["http binding is not implemented"] }
  }
  const base = await readGraphFromDisk(workspaceRoot, runId)
  const state = await readReplanStateFile(workspaceRoot, runId)

  const idem = options.idempotencyKey
  if (idem && state.last_idempotency_key === idem) {
    return { ok: true, deduped: true, replan_cycles_completed: state.replan_cycles_completed }
  }

  const max = base.dispatch_policy.max_replan_cycles
  if (max !== undefined && state.replan_cycles_completed >= max) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      errors: [
        `replan blocked: max_replan_cycles (${max}) reached; raise the cap in graph dispatch_policy or reset state manually`,
      ],
    }
  }

  const merged = mergeGraphsForReplan(base, delta)
  if (!merged.ok) {
    return merged
  }

  const result = await importRun(merged.graph, workspaceRoot, { binding: options.binding })
  const next: ReplanStateFile = {
    replan_cycles_completed: state.replan_cycles_completed + 1,
    last_idempotency_key: idem ?? state.last_idempotency_key,
  }
  await writeReplanStateFile(workspaceRoot, runId, next)
  await appendReplanLog(workspaceRoot, runId, {
    kind: "replan",
    status: "ok",
    replan_cycles_completed: next.replan_cycles_completed,
    idempotency_key: idem ?? null,
  })

  return { ok: true, deduped: false, import: result, replan_cycles_completed: next.replan_cycles_completed }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/replan.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2085 bytes

```ts
import type { StoneforgeTaskCard, XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph, xlotylStoneforgeGraphSchema } from "./contract.js"

/**
 * Merge a replan delta graph into a base graph (new taskCards only).
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * base : XlotylStoneforgeGraph
 *     Previously imported graph.
 * delta : unknown
 *     JSON object shaped like a graph; must share `run_id` and only add new `tasks` ids.
 *
 * Returns
 * -------
 * GraphValidationResult
 *     Validated merged graph or errors.
 */
export function mergeGraphsForReplan(
  base: XlotylStoneforgeGraph,
  delta: unknown,
): ReturnType<typeof validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph> {
  const parsed = xlotylStoneforgeGraphSchema.safeParse(delta)
  if (!parsed.success) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      errors: parsed.error.errors.map((issue) => `${issue.path.join(".")}: ${issue.message}`),
    }
  }
  const deltaGraph = parsed.data
  if (deltaGraph.run_id !== base.run_id) {
    return { ok: false, errors: [`run_id mismatch: base=${base.run_id} delta=${deltaGraph.run_id}`] }
  }

  const existingIds = new Set(base.tasks.map((task) => task.id))
  const newTaskCards: StoneforgeTaskCard[] = []
  for (const task of deltaGraph.tasks) {
    if (existingIds.has(task.id)) {
      return { ok: false, errors: [`replan attempted to reuse existing taskCard id: ${task.id}`] }
    }
    newTaskCards.push(task)
  }

  if (newTaskCards.length === 0) {
    return { ok: false, errors: ["replan delta contains no new tasks"] }
  }

  const phaseById = new Map(base.phases.map((phase) => [phase.id, phase]))
  for (const phase of deltaGraph.phases) {
    if (!phaseById.has(phase.id)) {
      phaseById.set(phase.id, phase)
    }
  }

  const merged: XlotylStoneforgeGraph = {
    ...base,
    phases: [...phaseById.values()],
    tasks: [...base.tasks, ...newTaskCards],
    dispatch_policy: {
      ...base.dispatch_policy,
      ...deltaGraph.dispatch_policy,
    },
    aggregation: deltaGraph.aggregation ?? base.aggregation,
  }

  return validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(merged)
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/replay-run.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3124 bytes

```ts
import { writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import { aggregateRun } from "./aggregate-run.js"
import { readGraphFromDisk } from "./import-run.js"
import { draftPlanPath, stoneforgeMapPath } from "./paths.js"
import { renderTaskCardDescription } from "./task-card-renderer.js"

function syntheticTaskId(taskCardId: string): string {
  return `sf-task-${taskCardId.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]+/g, "-")}`
}

/**
 * Regenerate adapter artifacts from `graph.json` + current dispatch log, then aggregate.
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * workspaceRoot : string
 *     Workspace root containing `.stoneforge/xlotyl/runs/{run_id}/`.
 * runId : string
 *     Run identifier.
 *
 * Returns
 * -------
 * object
 *     Paths to regenerated `draft-plan.json`, `stoneforge-map.json`, report, dataset.
 */
export async function replayRun(
  workspaceRoot: string,
  runId: string,
): Promise<{ draftPlan: string; map: string; reportPath: string; datasetPath: string }> {
  const root = path.resolve(workspaceRoot)
  const graph = await readGraphFromDisk(root, runId)

  const mapping: Record<string, string> = {}
  const tasks: Array<{
    stoneforge_task_id: string
    xlotyl_task_card_id: string
    title: string
    priority: number
    description: string
    metadata: Record<string, unknown>
  }> = []
  const dependencies: Array<{ blocked: string; blocker: string }> = []

  for (const taskCard of graph.tasks) {
    const stoneforge_task_id = syntheticTaskId(taskCard.id)
    mapping[taskCard.id] = stoneforge_task_id
    tasks.push({
      stoneforge_task_id,
      xlotyl_task_card_id: taskCard.id,
      title: taskCard.title,
      priority: taskCard.priority,
      description: renderTaskCardDescription(graph, taskCard),
      metadata: {
        xlotyl: {
          schema_version: 1,
          run_id: runId,
          task_card_id: taskCard.id,
          workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
          execution_mode: graph.execution_mode ?? null,
        },
      },
    })
  }
  for (const taskCard of graph.tasks) {
    for (const blocker of taskCard.dependencies) {
      dependencies.push({ blocked: mapping[taskCard.id]!, blocker: mapping[blocker]! })
    }
  }

  const draftPlan = {
    id: `draft-plan-${runId}-replay`,
    title: graph.workflow_title,
    status: "draft" as const,
    metadata: {
      xlotyl_run_id: runId,
      xlotyl_workflow_id: graph.workflow_id,
      planning_owner: graph.planning_owner,
      runtime_target: graph.runtime_target,
      execution_mode: graph.execution_mode ?? null,
      dispatch_policy: graph.dispatch_policy,
      replay: true,
    },
    tasks,
    dependencies,
  }

  const map = { run_id: runId, mapping }
  await writeFile(stoneforgeMapPath(root, runId), `${JSON.stringify(map, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")
  await writeFile(draftPlanPath(root, runId), `${JSON.stringify(draftPlan, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8")

  const aggregated = await aggregateRun(root, runId)
  return {
    draftPlan: draftPlanPath(root, runId),
    map: stoneforgeMapPath(root, runId),
    reportPath: aggregated.reportPath,
    datasetPath: aggregated.datasetPath,
  }
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/sf-cli-binding.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 4101 bytes

```ts
import { execFile } from "node:child_process"
import { promisify } from "node:util"

const execFileAsync = promisify(execFile)

export type StoneforgeCliErrorCode =
  | "SF_CLI_COMMAND_FAILED"
  | "SF_CLI_EMPTY_JSON"
  | "SF_CLI_INVALID_JSON"
  | "SF_CLI_UNSUCCESSFUL"
  | "SF_CLI_VERSION_UNAVAILABLE"

export interface StoneforgeCliVersion {
  version: string
}

export class StoneforgeCliError extends Error {
  readonly code: StoneforgeCliErrorCode
  readonly command: string[]
  readonly stdout?: string
  readonly stderr?: string
  readonly exitCode?: number

  constructor(
    code: StoneforgeCliErrorCode,
    message: string,
    details: { command: string[]; stdout?: string; stderr?: string; exitCode?: number },
  ) {
    super(message)
    this.name = "StoneforgeCliError"
    this.code = code
    this.command = details.command
    this.stdout = details.stdout
    this.stderr = details.stderr
    this.exitCode = details.exitCode
  }
}

function errorField(error: unknown, key: "stdout" | "stderr"): string | undefined {
  const value = (error as Record<string, unknown> | null)?.[key]
  return typeof value === "string" ? value : undefined
}

function exitCode(error: unknown): number | undefined {
  const value = (error as Record<string, unknown> | null)?.code
  return typeof value === "number" ? value : undefined
}

function parseSfEnvelope<T>(
  stdout: string,
  stderr: string | undefined,
  command: string[],
): T {
  const trimmed = stdout.trim()
  if (!trimmed) {
    throw new StoneforgeCliError(
      "SF_CLI_EMPTY_JSON",
      `Stoneforge command returned empty JSON output: ${command.join(" ")}`,
      { command, stdout, stderr },
    )
  }

  let parsed: { success?: boolean; data?: T; error?: { message?: string } }
  try {
    parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed) as { success?: boolean; data?: T; error?: { message?: string } }
  } catch (error) {
    throw new StoneforgeCliError(
      "SF_CLI_INVALID_JSON",
      `Stoneforge command returned invalid JSON: ${command.join(" ")}: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`,
      { command, stdout, stderr },
    )
  }

  if (!parsed.success) {
    const message = parsed.error?.message ?? stderr?.trim() ?? "unknown Stoneforge CLI error"
    throw new StoneforgeCliError(
      "SF_CLI_UNSUCCESSFUL",
      `Stoneforge command failed: ${command.join(" ")}: ${message}`,
      { command, stdout, stderr },
    )
  }

  return parsed.data as T
}

export async function runSfJson<T>(workspaceRoot: string, sfBinPath: string, args: string[]): Promise<T> {
  const command = args.includes("--json") ? args : [...args, "--json"]
  try {
    const { stdout, stderr } = await execFileAsync(process.execPath, [sfBinPath, ...command], {
      cwd: workspaceRoot,
    })
    return parseSfEnvelope<T>(stdout, stderr, command)
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof StoneforgeCliError) {
      throw error
    }
    const stdout = errorField(error, "stdout")
    const stderr = errorField(error, "stderr")
    if (stdout?.trim()) {
      return parseSfEnvelope<T>(stdout, stderr, command)
    }
    throw new StoneforgeCliError(
      "SF_CLI_COMMAND_FAILED",
      `Stoneforge command failed before JSON output: ${command.join(" ")}: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`,
      { command, stdout, stderr, exitCode: exitCode(error) },
    )
  }
}

export async function inspectSfCli(workspaceRoot: string, sfBinPath: string): Promise<StoneforgeCliVersion> {
  const data = await runSfJson<{ version?: unknown }>(workspaceRoot, sfBinPath, ["--version"])
  if (typeof data.version !== "string" || data.version.length === 0) {
    throw new StoneforgeCliError(
      "SF_CLI_VERSION_UNAVAILABLE",
      "Stoneforge sf.js did not report a version from --version --json",
      { command: ["--version", "--json"] },
    )
  }
  return { version: data.version }
}

export function formatStoneforgeCliError(error: unknown): string {
  if (error instanceof StoneforgeCliError) {
    return `${error.code}: ${error.message}`
  }
  return error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
}
```
