### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/task-card-renderer.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3095 bytes

```ts
import type { StoneforgeTaskCard, XlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"

/**
 * Render a Stoneforge task description body from a governed XLOTYL taskCard.
 *
 * Parameters
 * ----------
 * graph : XlotylStoneforgeGraph
 *     Validated import graph.
 * taskCard : StoneforgeTaskCard
 *     TaskCard to render.
 *
 * Returns
 * -------
 * string
 *     Markdown suitable for a Stoneforge task description (includes doc-maintenance defaults).
 */
export function renderTaskCardDescription(graph: XlotylStoneforgeGraph, taskCard: StoneforgeTaskCard): string {
  const phase = taskCard.phase_id ? graph.phases.find((candidate) => candidate.id === taskCard.phase_id) : undefined
  const phaseLine = phase ? `${phase.id} — ${phase.name}` : "(no phase)"

  const include = taskCard.scope?.include_paths?.length
    ? taskCard.scope.include_paths.map((line) => `- ${line}`).join("\n")
    : "- (not specified)"
  const exclude = taskCard.scope?.exclude_paths?.length
    ? taskCard.scope.exclude_paths.map((line) => `- ${line}`).join("\n")
    : "- (not specified)"

  const toolLines = taskCard.tools ?? []
  const tools = toolLines.length > 0 ? toolLines.map((line) => `- ${line}`).join("\n") : "- (none listed)"
  const acceptance = taskCard.acceptance_criteria.map((line) => `- ${line}`).join("\n")
  const metrics = taskCard.metrics?.length ? taskCard.metrics.map((line) => `- ${line}`).join("\n") : "- (none listed)"
  const artifacts = taskCard.expected_artifacts?.length
    ? taskCard.expected_artifacts.map((line) => `- ${line}`).join("\n")
    : "- (none listed)"

  return [
    "# XLOTYL TaskCard",
    "",
    "## TaskCard identity",
    `- XLOTYL run: \`${graph.run_id}\``,
    `- TaskCard ID: \`${taskCard.id}\``,
    `- Phase: ${phaseLine}`,
    `- Worker role: ${taskCard.worker_role ?? "(unspecified)"}`,
    `- TaskCard type: \`${taskCard.task_card_type}\``,
    "",
    "## Workflow",
    `- workflow_id: \`${graph.workflow_id}\``,
    `- workflow_title: ${graph.workflow_title}`,
    "",
    "## Task",
    taskCard.title,
    "",
    "## Scope",
    "### Include",
    include,
    "",
    "### Exclude",
    exclude,
    "",
    "## Required tools",
    tools,
    "",
    "## Context",
    "Before starting:",
    "1. Search Stoneforge workspace docs and prior run artifacts for this `run_id`.",
    "2. Read relevant architecture/reference documents.",
    "3. Prefer minimal, reviewable diffs; do not expand scope beyond this taskCard.",
    "",
    "## Acceptance criteria",
    acceptance,
    "",
    "## Metrics to report",
    metrics,
    "",
    "## Expected artifacts",
    artifacts,
    "",
    "## Completion report",
    "When finished, include a JSON object with:",
    "- `xlotyl_run_id`, `xlotyl_task_card_id`, `stoneforge_task_id`",
    "- `status`",
    "- `acceptance` map (criterion -> passed|partial|failed)",
    "- `metrics` key/value numbers where applicable",
    "- `artifacts` paths",
    "- `followups` optional array of `{ title, reason }`",
    "",
    "## Source goal (for traceability)",
    graph.source_goal,
    "",
  ].join("\n")
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/terminality-validator.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2108 bytes

```ts
import type { StoneforgeTaskCard } from "./contract.js"

export interface TerminalityValidationSuccess {
  ok: true
}

export interface TerminalityValidationFailure {
  ok: false
  errors: string[]
}

export type TerminalityValidationResult = TerminalityValidationSuccess | TerminalityValidationFailure

/**
 * Validate that a Stoneforge task is a well-formed terminal unit.
 *
 * This is intentionally stricter than the graph schema: the schema allows these
 * fields to be omitted for backwards compatibility, but terminality governance
 * must reject tasks that are not execution-ready fundamentals.
 */
export function validateTerminalTaskUnit(task: StoneforgeTaskCard): TerminalityValidationResult {
  const errors: string[] = []

  if (typeof task.objective !== "string" || task.objective.trim().length === 0) {
    errors.push("objective is required for terminal tasks")
  }

  if (typeof task.runtime_environment_id !== "string" || task.runtime_environment_id.trim().length === 0) {
    errors.push("runtime_environment_id is required for terminal tasks")
  }

  if (typeof task.execution_adapter_id !== "string" || task.execution_adapter_id.trim().length === 0) {
    errors.push("execution_adapter_id is required for terminal tasks")
  }

  const hasValidatorIds = Array.isArray(task.validator_ids) && task.validator_ids.length > 0
  const expected = Array.isArray(task.expected_artifacts) ? task.expected_artifacts : []
  const requiresVerificationReport = expected.some((artifact) => artifact === "VERIFICATION_REPORT")
  if (!hasValidatorIds && !requiresVerificationReport) {
    errors.push("terminal tasks must declare validator_ids or require VERIFICATION_REPORT in expected_artifacts")
  }

  if (Array.isArray(task.clarification_dependencies) && task.clarification_dependencies.length > 0) {
    errors.push("terminal tasks must not have clarification_dependencies")
  }

  if (task.decomposition_policy !== "terminal") {
    errors.push("terminal tasks must have decomposition_policy=terminal")
  }

  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return { ok: false, errors }
  }
  return { ok: true }
}

```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/validator-registry.ts`

```ts
/**
 * Stoneforge validator registry.
 *
 * This file is intentionally a small, explicit registry of validator identifiers that
 * capability packages may reference in `validators[].id`.
 *
 * Why this exists:
 * - capability manifests are contracts and must only reference real, enforced gates
 * - the runtime should be the canonical source of truth for what validator ids exist
 * - CI needs a stable, reviewable list to validate manifests against
 */
export const STONEFORGE_VALIDATOR_IDS = [
  "graph_schema_validation",
  "acyclic_dependency_check",
  "approval_before_activation",
  "max_replan_cycles",
] as const

export type StoneforgeValidatorId = (typeof STONEFORGE_VALIDATOR_IDS)[number]

```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/stoneforge/xsf-cli.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 10354 bytes

```ts
import { readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import { resolveStoneforgeBindingFromXsfArgs } from "./binding.js"
import { aggregateRun } from "./aggregate-run.js"
import { validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph } from "./contract.js"
import { parseEvaluationPayload } from "./evaluation.js"
import {
  activateRun,
  appendEvaluationEvent,
  appendSyncEvent,
  validateAndImportRun,
  writeApproval,
} from "./import-run.js"
import { runReplanMergeAndImport } from "./replan-pipeline.js"
import { replayRun } from "./replay-run.js"
import { runDecisionCycle } from "./decision/index.js"
import { markTerminal } from "./mark-terminal.js"
import { compileCapabilityPackageGraph, terminalityPolicySchema } from "../capability-package/graph-compiler.js"

function valueAfter(args: string[], flag: string): string | undefined {
  const index = args.indexOf(flag)
  return index >= 0 ? args[index + 1] : undefined
}

function hasFlag(args: string[], flag: string): boolean {
  return args.includes(flag)
}

function valuesAfterFlag(args: string[], flag: string): string[] {
  const values: string[] = []
  for (let i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
    if (args[i] !== flag) continue
    const next = args[i + 1]
    if (typeof next === "string" && next.length > 0) {
      values.push(next)
    }
  }
  return values
}

function workspaceFrom(args: string[]): string {
  return valueAfter(args, "--workspace") ?? valueAfter(args, "--repo-root") ?? process.cwd()
}

export async function runXsfCli(args: string[]): Promise<string> {
  const [subcommand, ...rest] = args
  if (!subcommand || subcommand === "help" || subcommand === "--help") {
    return [
      "Usage: xlotyl-dev-services xsf <validate|import|approve|activate|compile-capability-graph|mark-terminal|sync|evaluate|replan|decide|aggregate|replay> [options]",
      "",
      "Options:",
      "  --graph <path>        Path to graph.json (validate/import/replan)",
      "  --workspace <path>    Repo root (default: cwd)",
      "  --run <run_id>        Run id (activate/sync/evaluate/aggregate/replan)",
      "  --approved-by <name>  Activator identity",
      "  --force               Skip approval file (dangerous; testing only)",
      "  --dry-run             Validate graph and binding without mutating Stoneforge",
      "  --payload <path>      JSON file for sync/evaluate bodies",
      "  --package-id <id>     Capability package id (compile-capability-graph)",
      "  --source-goal <text>  Goal text used to compile a deterministic graph (compile-capability-graph)",
      "  --terminality-policy  require_terminal|allow_auto (compile-capability-graph)",
      "  --out <path>          Write compiled graph to path (compile-capability-graph)",
      "  --task <task_id>      TaskCard id to mark terminal (mark-terminal)",
      "  --all                 Mark all taskCards terminal (mark-terminal)",
      "  --marked-by <id>     Marking identity for terminality governance (mark-terminal)",
      "  --reason <text>      Governance reason for terminality change (mark-terminal)",
      "  --evidence-ref <ref> Evidence artifact ref (repeatable) for terminality governance",
      "  --binding <mode>      Binding mode: local-artifact | sf-cli",
      "  --sf-bin <path>       Path to Stoneforge sf.js for sf-cli binding",
      "  --idempotency-key     Optional key; duplicate successful replan retries are no-ops",
      "Env:",
      "  XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_BINDING=local-artifact|sf-cli",
      "  STONEFORGE_SF_BIN=/abs/path/to/sf.js (or XLOTYL_STONEFORGE_SF_BIN)",
      "",
    ].join("\n")
  }

  const workspace = workspaceFrom(rest)
  const binding = resolveStoneforgeBindingFromXsfArgs(rest)

  if (subcommand === "validate") {
    const graphPath = valueAfter(rest, "--graph")
    if (!graphPath) {
      throw new Error("xsf validate requires --graph <path>")
    }
    const raw = JSON.parse(await readFile(path.resolve(graphPath), "utf8")) as unknown
    const result = validateXlotylStoneforgeGraph(raw)
    return `${JSON.stringify(result, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "compile-capability-graph") {
    const packageId = valueAfter(rest, "--package-id")
    const sourceGoal = valueAfter(rest, "--source-goal")
    if (!packageId || !sourceGoal) {
      throw new Error("xsf compile-capability-graph requires --package-id <id> --source-goal <text>")
    }
    const policyRaw = valueAfter(rest, "--terminality-policy") ?? "require_terminal"
    const terminalityPolicy = terminalityPolicySchema.parse(policyRaw)
    const outPath = valueAfter(rest, "--out")

    const compiled = await compileCapabilityPackageGraph({
      packageId,
      sourceGoal,
      terminalityPolicy,
    })
    if (outPath) {
      if (!compiled.ok) {
        await writeFile(path.resolve(outPath), JSON.stringify(compiled, null, 2) + "\n", "utf8")
      } else {
        await writeFile(path.resolve(outPath), JSON.stringify(compiled.graph, null, 2) + "\n", "utf8")
      }
    }
    return `${JSON.stringify(compiled, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "import") {
    const graphPath = valueAfter(rest, "--graph")
    if (!graphPath) {
      throw new Error("xsf import requires --graph <path>")
    }
    const raw = JSON.parse(await readFile(path.resolve(graphPath), "utf8")) as unknown
    const imported = hasFlag(rest, "--dry-run")
      ? await validateAndImportRun(raw, workspace, { binding, dryRun: true })
      : await validateAndImportRun(raw, workspace, { binding })
    return `${JSON.stringify(imported, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "activate") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    if (!runId) {
      throw new Error("xsf activate requires --run <run_id>")
    }
    const approvedBy = valueAfter(rest, "--approved-by")
    const result = await activateRun(workspace, runId, { force: hasFlag(rest, "--force"), approvedBy, binding })
    return `${JSON.stringify(result, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "approve") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    if (!runId) {
      throw new Error("xsf approve requires --run <run_id>")
    }
    await writeApproval(workspace, runId, {
      approved: true,
      approved_by: valueAfter(rest, "--approved-by") ?? "operator",
    })
    return `${JSON.stringify({ ok: true, runId }, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "sync") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    const payloadPath = valueAfter(rest, "--payload")
    if (!runId || !payloadPath) {
      throw new Error("xsf sync requires --run <run_id> --payload <path>")
    }
    const payload = JSON.parse(await readFile(path.resolve(payloadPath), "utf8")) as Record<string, unknown>
    await appendSyncEvent(workspace, runId, {
      task_card_id: String(payload.task_card_id ?? ""),
      status: String(payload.status ?? "unknown"),
      message: typeof payload.message === "string" ? payload.message : undefined,
      metrics: payload.metrics as Record<string, number> | undefined,
      artifacts: Array.isArray(payload.artifacts) ? (payload.artifacts as string[]) : undefined,
    })
    return `${JSON.stringify({ ok: true }, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "evaluate") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    const payloadPath = valueAfter(rest, "--payload")
    if (!runId || !payloadPath) {
      throw new Error("xsf evaluate requires --run <run_id> --payload <path>")
    }
    const payload = JSON.parse(await readFile(path.resolve(payloadPath), "utf8")) as unknown
    const parsed = parseEvaluationPayload(payload)
    if (!parsed.ok) {
      return `${JSON.stringify({ ok: false, errors: parsed.errors }, null, 2)}\n`
    }
    await appendEvaluationEvent(workspace, runId, parsed.value)
    return `${JSON.stringify({ ok: true }, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "replan") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    const graphPath = valueAfter(rest, "--graph")
    if (!runId || !graphPath) {
      throw new Error("xsf replan requires --run <run_id> --graph <delta_graph.json>")
    }
    const delta = JSON.parse(await readFile(path.resolve(graphPath), "utf8")) as unknown
    const idempotencyKey = valueAfter(rest, "--idempotency-key")
    const result = await runReplanMergeAndImport(workspace, runId, delta, {
      binding,
      idempotencyKey: idempotencyKey ?? undefined,
    })
    return `${JSON.stringify(
      result.ok
        ? result.deduped
          ? { ok: true, deduped: true, replan_cycles_completed: result.replan_cycles_completed }
          : { ok: true, merged: true, import: result.import, replan_cycles_completed: result.replan_cycles_completed }
        : { ok: false, errors: result.errors },
      null,
      2,
    )}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "decide") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    if (!runId) {
      throw new Error("xsf decide requires --run <run_id>")
    }
    const result = await runDecisionCycle({ workspaceRoot: workspace, runId, binding })
    return `${JSON.stringify(result, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "aggregate") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    if (!runId) {
      throw new Error("xsf aggregate requires --run <run_id>")
    }
    const result = await aggregateRun(workspace, runId)
    return `${JSON.stringify({ ok: true, ...result }, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "replay") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    if (!runId) {
      throw new Error("xsf replay requires --run <run_id>")
    }
    const result = await replayRun(workspace, runId)
    return `${JSON.stringify({ ok: true, ...result }, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  if (subcommand === "mark-terminal") {
    const runId = valueAfter(rest, "--run")
    if (!runId) {
      throw new Error("xsf mark-terminal requires --run <run_id>")
    }
    const taskId = valueAfter(rest, "--task")
    const markedBy = valueAfter(rest, "--marked-by")
    const reason = valueAfter(rest, "--reason")
    const evidenceRefs = valuesAfterFlag(rest, "--evidence-ref")
    const result = await markTerminal(workspace, runId, {
      taskId: taskId ?? undefined,
      all: hasFlag(rest, "--all"),
      markedBy: markedBy ?? undefined,
      reason: reason ?? undefined,
      evidenceRefs: evidenceRefs.length > 0 ? evidenceRefs : undefined,
    })
    return `${JSON.stringify(result, null, 2)}\n`
  }

  throw new Error(`Unknown xsf subcommand: ${subcommand}`)
}
```

### `services/core-dev-services/src/sync.test.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 3147 bytes

```ts
import { mkdir, mkdtemp, readFile, rm, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import { join } from "node:path"
import { tmpdir } from "node:os"
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest"
import { generateAdapters } from "./adapters.js"
import { defaultSourceRegistry } from "./manifest.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot } from "./paths.js"
import { importPinnedSources } from "./registry.js"
import { applySyncPlan, createSyncPlan, writeSyncPlan } from "./sync.js"

describe("sync planning", () => {
  it("plans repo-scoped writes without touching user-global files by default", () => {
    const plan = createSyncPlan(generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())), {
      repoRoot: "/repo",
      global: false,
    })

    expect(plan.operations.every((operation) => operation.destination.startsWith("/repo/"))).toBe(true)
    expect(plan.operations.some((operation) => operation.destination.includes(".gemini/antigravity"))).toBe(
      false,
    )
  })

  it("defaults repo-scoped writes to the core-dev-services root", () => {
    const plan = createSyncPlan(generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())), {})

    expect(plan.operations.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    expect(plan.operations.every((operation) => operation.destination.startsWith(defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()))).toBe(
      true,
    )
  })

  it("merges global Antigravity MCP config without replacing existing servers", () => {
    const existing = JSON.stringify({ mcpServers: { cloudrun: { command: "npx", args: ["cloudrun"] } } })
    const plan = createSyncPlan(generateAdapters(importPinnedSources(defaultSourceRegistry())), {
      repoRoot: "/repo",
      homeDir: "/home/max",
      global: true,
      existingFiles: {
        "/home/max/.gemini/antigravity/mcp_config.json": existing,
      },
    })

    const result = applySyncPlan(plan)
    const antigravity = JSON.parse(
      result.files["/home/max/.gemini/antigravity/mcp_config.json"] ?? "{}",
    ) as { mcpServers: Record<string, unknown> }
    expect(Object.keys(antigravity.mcpServers)).toEqual(
      expect.arrayContaining(["cloudrun", "xlotyl-dev-services"]),
    )
  })

  it("writes sync operations to disk and backs up existing files", async () => {
    const root = await mkdtemp(join(tmpdir(), "xlotyl-sync-"))
    try {
      const destination = join(root, ".cursor/mcp.json")
      await mkdir(join(root, ".cursor"), { recursive: true })
      await writeFile(destination, "{\"mcpServers\":{\"existing\":{\"command\":\"old\"}}}\n")

      const result = await writeSyncPlan({
        operations: [
          {
            action: "write",
            destination,
            content: "{\"mcpServers\":{\"xlotyl-dev-services\":{\"command\":\"xlotyl-dev-services\"}}}\n",
          },
        ],
      })

      const merged = await readFile(destination, "utf8")
      expect(merged).toContain("xlotyl-dev-services")
      expect(merged).toContain("existing")
      await expect(readFile(result.writes[0]?.backupPath ?? "", "utf8")).resolves.toContain("existing")
    } finally {
      await rm(root, { recursive: true, force: true })
    }
  })
})
```

---

### `services/core-dev-services/src/sync.ts`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 5498 bytes

```ts
import { mkdir, readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises"
import path from "node:path"
import type { VirtualFile } from "./adapters.js"
import { defaultCoreDevServicesRoot } from "./paths.js"

export interface SyncOperation {
  action: "write"
  destination: string
  content: string
}

export interface SyncPlan {
  operations: SyncOperation[]
}

export interface SyncPlanOptions {
  repoRoot?: string
  homeDir?: string
  global?: boolean
  existingFiles?: Record<string, string>
}

export interface SyncApplyResult {
  files: Record<string, string>
}

export interface SyncWrite {
  destination: string
  bytes: number
  backupPath?: string
}

export interface SyncWriteResult {
  writes: SyncWrite[]
}

export interface SyncWriteOptions {
  backupExisting?: boolean
}

function parseJsonObject(text: string | undefined): Record<string, unknown> {
  if (!text) {
    return {}
  }
  const parsed = JSON.parse(text) as unknown
  return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && !Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed as Record<string, unknown> : {}
}

function mergeMcpConfig(existingText: string | undefined, fragmentText: string): string {
  const existing = parseJsonObject(existingText)
  const fragment = parseJsonObject(fragmentText)
  const existingServers =
    existing.mcpServers && typeof existing.mcpServers === "object" && !Array.isArray(existing.mcpServers)
      ? existing.mcpServers as Record<string, unknown>
      : {}
  const fragmentServers =
    fragment.mcpServers && typeof fragment.mcpServers === "object" && !Array.isArray(fragment.mcpServers)
      ? fragment.mcpServers as Record<string, unknown>
      : {}
  return `${JSON.stringify({ ...existing, mcpServers: { ...existingServers, ...fragmentServers } }, null, 2)}\n`
}

function pluginName(plugin: unknown): string | undefined {
  if (!plugin || typeof plugin !== "object" || Array.isArray(plugin) || !("name" in plugin)) {
    return undefined
  }
  return typeof plugin.name === "string" ? plugin.name : undefined
}

function mergeMarketplaceConfig(existingText: string | undefined, fragmentText: string): string {
  const existing = parseJsonObject(existingText)
  const fragment = parseJsonObject(fragmentText)
  const plugins = [
    ...(Array.isArray(existing.plugins) ? existing.plugins : []),
  ]
  for (const plugin of Array.isArray(fragment.plugins) ? fragment.plugins : []) {
    const name = pluginName(plugin)
    const existingIndex = name === undefined ? -1 : plugins.findIndex((candidate) => pluginName(candidate) === name)
    if (existingIndex >= 0) {
      plugins[existingIndex] = plugin
    } else {
      plugins.push(plugin)
    }
  }
  return `${JSON.stringify({ ...existing, ...fragment, plugins }, null, 2)}\n`
}

function mergeKnownConfig(destination: string, existing: string | undefined, content: string): string {
  if (existing === undefined) {
    return content
  }
  const normalized = destination.replaceAll("\\", "/")
  if (
    normalized.endsWith("/mcp.json") ||
    normalized.endsWith("/.mcp.json") ||
    normalized.endsWith("/mcp_config.json")
  ) {
    return mergeMcpConfig(existing, content)
  }
  if (normalized.endsWith("/.agents/plugins/marketplace.json")) {
    return mergeMarketplaceConfig(existing, content)
  }
  return content
}

export function createSyncPlan(files: VirtualFile[], options: SyncPlanOptions): SyncPlan {
  const repoRoot = options.repoRoot ?? defaultCoreDevServicesRoot()
  const operations: SyncOperation[] = []
  for (const file of files) {
    if (file.path === ".gemini/antigravity/mcp_config.fragment.json") {
      if (!options.global || !options.homeDir) {
        continue
      }
      const destination = path.join(options.homeDir, ".gemini/antigravity/mcp_config.json")
      operations.push({
        action: "write",
        destination,
        content: mergeMcpConfig(options.existingFiles?.[destination], file.content),
      })
      continue
    }
    operations.push({
      action: "write",
      destination: path.join(repoRoot, file.path),
      content: file.content,
    })
  }
  return { operations }
}

export function applySyncPlan(plan: SyncPlan): SyncApplyResult {
  const files: Record<string, string> = {}
  for (const operation of plan.operations) {
    files[operation.destination] = operation.content
  }
  return { files }
}

async function readExistingFile(filePath: string): Promise<string | undefined> {
  try {
    return await readFile(filePath, "utf8")
  } catch (error) {
    if (error && typeof error === "object" && "code" in error && error.code === "ENOENT") {
      return undefined
    }
    throw error
  }
}

export async function writeSyncPlan(
  plan: SyncPlan,
  options: SyncWriteOptions = {},
): Promise<SyncWriteResult> {
  const backupExisting = options.backupExisting ?? true
  const writes: SyncWrite[] = []

  for (const operation of plan.operations) {
    await mkdir(path.dirname(operation.destination), { recursive: true })

    let backupPath: string | undefined
    const existing = await readExistingFile(operation.destination)
    if (backupExisting && existing !== undefined) {
      backupPath = `${operation.destination}.bak`
      await writeFile(backupPath, existing)
    }

    const content = mergeKnownConfig(operation.destination, existing, operation.content)
    await writeFile(operation.destination, content)
    writes.push({
      destination: operation.destination,
      bytes: Buffer.byteLength(content, "utf8"),
      backupPath,
    })
  }

  return { writes }
}
```
